// **************** Evaluation ends here ****************************



//******************** Re-Evaluation starts here, extract the filenames and put the according amplitudes into an array for re-processing of the data *********************


if (option == "6. Re-Evaluation") {


pathfile=File.openDialog("Please choose the <Amplitudes only.txt> \nor <Amplitudes (selected).txt> file to be opened:");
data=File.openAsString(pathfile);
print(pathfile);
print("");

//***************** extract path from opened file start here ************************

strt=lastIndexOf(pathfile, "\\");
rmve=substring(pathfile, strt+1, lengthOf(pathfile)); 
dir=replace(pathfile, rmve, "");
rmve=replace(rmve, ".txt", "");

//***************** extract path from opened file ends here ************************


titles=newArray();
amplits=newArray();

lines=split(data,"\n");


//************** is it an amplitudes Only file, check starts here
ampltest="false";
atest=0;
while(ampltest=="false" && atest<lines.length){if(indexOf(lines[atest], "amplitudes=newArray(")<0){ampltest="false";}else{ampltest="true";}{atest++;}}
if (ampltest=="false") {exit("Sorry, but this seems not to be an" + "\n" + "<Amplitudes only>-File." + "\n" + "Please choose one.");}

//**************** is it an amplitudes only file, check ends here


count=0;
for (i = 0; i < lines.length; i+=4) {
titles=Array.concat(titles,lines[i]);	
count++;
}

count=0;
for (i = 2; i < lines.length; i+=4) {
amplits=Array.concat(amplits,lines[i]);	
count++;
}


for (runs = 0; runs < 500000; runs++) {
	


// ******************************* Please apply your settings here; you may also change the default-values *******************************

if (runs==0) {

Dialog.create("Please apply your parameters");

Dialog.addNumber("Detection", 20);
Dialog.addNumber("Threshold 1 [%]", 10);
Dialog.addNumber("Threshold 2 [%]", 20);
Dialog.addNumber("Threshold 3 [%]", 50);
Dialog.addNumber("Threshold 4 [%]", 90);
Dialog.addNumber("Framerate  [fps]", 120);

Dialog.show();
detection=Dialog.getNumber();
thresh0=Dialog.getNumber()/100;
thresh1=Dialog.getNumber()/100;
thresh2=Dialog.getNumber()/100;
thresh3=Dialog.getNumber()/100;
fps=Dialog.getNumber();

if(detection<1.1){detection=1.1;}

print("Applied Threshold 1: " + thresh0*100 + "%");
print("Applied Threshold 2: " + thresh1*100 + "%");
print("Applied Threshold 3: " + thresh2*100 + "%");
print("Applied Threshold 4: " + thresh3*100 + "%");
print("Applied Framerate: " + fps);
print("Applied Detection: " + detection);

}

// ******************************* Mark the previous settings starts here, settings are remembered for the next evaluation *******************************

if (runs>0) {
	
Dialog.create("Please apply your parameters");

Dialog.addNumber("Detection", detection);
Dialog.addNumber("Threshold 1 [%]", thresh0*100);
Dialog.addNumber("Threshold 2 [%]", thresh1*100);
Dialog.addNumber("Threshold 3 [%]", thresh2*100);
Dialog.addNumber("Threshold 4 [%]", thresh3*100);
Dialog.addNumber("Framerate  [fps]", fps);

Dialog.show();
detection=Dialog.getNumber();
thresh0=Dialog.getNumber()/100;
thresh1=Dialog.getNumber()/100;
thresh2=Dialog.getNumber()/100;
thresh3=Dialog.getNumber()/100;
fps=Dialog.getNumber();

if(detection<1.1){detection=1.1;}

print("Applied Threshold 1: " + thresh0*100 + "%");
print("Applied Threshold 2: " + thresh1*100 + "%");
print("Applied Threshold 3: " + thresh2*100 + "%");
print("Applied Threshold 4: " + thresh3*100 + "%");
print("Applied Framerate: " + fps);
print("Applied Detection: " + detection);

}

// ******************************* Mark the previous settings ends here *******************************

// ****************************************************** End of user-settings *******************************************



//************** Select your data and convert it into an array for further evaluation starts here **************


Dialog.create("Select your data");
Dialog.addChoice("Please select:", titles);
Dialog.show();
option=Dialog.getChoice();

print("");
print("Selected data: " + option);
print("");

elmt=0;
while (option!=titles[elmt]) {elmt++;}

amplitudes=amplits[elmt];
amplitudes=replace(amplitudes, "amplitudes=newArray", "");
amplitudes=replace(amplitudes, "\\);", "");
amplitudes=replace(amplitudes, "\\(", "");
amplitudes=split(amplitudes, ",");


for (pf=0; pf<amplitudes.length; pf++) {
aa=parseFloat(amplitudes[pf]);

if (isNaN(aa)) {
	aa = 0;
}

amplitudes[pf]=aa;
}

//*************** Select your data and convert it into an array for further evaluation ends here ******************

// ************ Here, Re-evaluation of the data with the applied parameters starts ********************



Array.getStatistics(amplitudes, pmin, pmax, pmean, pstdDev);

ampRange = pmax - pmin;

if (isNaN(ampRange)) {
	ampRange = 0;
}

if (ampRange < 0) {
	ampRange = 0;
}

detectDelta = 0;

if (detection > 0) {
	detectDelta = ampRange/detection;
}

maxima=Array.findMaxima(amplitudes, detectDelta);
minima=Array.findMinima(amplitudes, detectDelta);
Array.sort(maxima);
Array.sort(minima);

min=0;
max=0;
beats=1;
btimea=0;
btimeabs="";
btimeold=0;
beattimes=newArray();
threshold=thresh0;



//*************** Here, all the minima are paired with the according (following) maxima and the amplitudes are calculated **************************** 


truncmin=Array.copy(minima);
truncmax=Array.copy(maxima);

if(truncmin.length<1 || truncmax.length<1){
print(" ");
print("Sorry, no maxima/minima were detected with the applied settings!");
exit();
}

if (truncmax[0]<truncmin[0]){
truncmax=Array.slice(truncmax,1,truncmax.length);
}


if(truncmax.length>truncmin.length){
	truncmax=Array.slice(truncmax,0,truncmin.length);
}

if(truncmax.length<truncmin.length){
	truncmin=Array.slice(truncmin,0,truncmax.length);
}


maxamplitudes=newArray(truncmax.length);

for (www=0; www<truncmax.length; www++){
	maxamplitudes[www]=amplitudes[truncmax[www]]-amplitudes[truncmin[www]];
}

//********************* Printing of the data starts here *******************

// Create Arrays that contain the transition points before and after maxima for the different thresholds starts here

systuserstart=newArray(truncmax.length);
diastuserend=newArray(truncmax.length);

syst10start=newArray(truncmax.length);
diast10end=newArray(truncmax.length);

syst50start=newArray(truncmax.length);
diast50end=newArray(truncmax.length);

syst90start=newArray(truncmax.length);
diast90end=newArray(truncmax.length);


for (transition = 0; transition < truncmax.length; transition++) {

//amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh10*maxamplitudes[ampl]

//thresh0
dropleft=truncmax[transition];
dropright=truncmax[transition];
while(dropleft>0 && amplitudes[dropleft]>((maxamplitudes[transition])*thresh0)+amplitudes[truncmin[transition]]){dropleft=dropleft-1;}
while(dropright<amplitudes.length-1 && amplitudes[dropright]>((maxamplitudes[transition])*thresh0)+amplitudes[truncmin[transition]]){dropright++;}
systuserstart[transition]=dropleft;
diastuserend[transition]=dropright;

//thresh1
dropleft=truncmax[transition];
dropright=truncmax[transition];
while(dropleft>0 && amplitudes[dropleft]>((maxamplitudes[transition])*thresh1)+amplitudes[truncmin[transition]]){dropleft=dropleft-1;}
while(dropright<amplitudes.length-1 && amplitudes[dropright]>((maxamplitudes[transition])*thresh1)+amplitudes[truncmin[transition]]){dropright++;}
syst10start[transition]=dropleft;
diast10end[transition]=dropright;


//thresh2
dropleft=truncmax[transition];
dropright=truncmax[transition];
while(dropleft>0 && amplitudes[dropleft]>((maxamplitudes[transition])*thresh2)+amplitudes[truncmin[transition]]){dropleft=dropleft-1;}
while(dropright<amplitudes.length-1 && amplitudes[dropright]>((maxamplitudes[transition])*thresh2)+amplitudes[truncmin[transition]]){dropright++;}
syst50start[transition]=dropleft;
diast50end[transition]=dropright;

//thresh3
dropleft=truncmax[transition];
dropright=truncmax[transition];
while(dropleft>0 && amplitudes[dropleft]>((maxamplitudes[transition])*thresh3)+amplitudes[truncmin[transition]]){dropleft=dropleft-1;}
while(dropright<amplitudes.length-1 && amplitudes[dropright]>((maxamplitudes[transition])*thresh3)+amplitudes[truncmin[transition]]){dropright++;}
syst90start[transition]=dropleft;
diast90end[transition]=dropright;
	
}


// Create Arrays that contain the transition points before and after maxima for the different thresholds ends here



//********** defining necessary constants starts here ********************

ampl=0;

peaktime=0;
peaktimeabs=0;
peaktimeold=0;

peaktime10=0;
peaktime10abs=0;
peaktime10old=0;

peaktime50=0;
peaktime50abs=0;
peaktime50old=0;

peaktime90=0;
peaktime90abs=0;
peaktime90old=0;

systime=0;
systimeabs="";
systimeold=0;

diastime=0;
diastimeabs=0;
diastimeold=0;

systime10=0;
systime10abs="";
systime10old=0;

diastime10=0;
diastime10abs=0;
diastime10old=0;

systime50=0;
systime50abs="";
systime50old=0;

diastime50=0;
diastime50abs=0;
diastime50old=0;

systime90=0;
systime90abs="";
systime90old=0;

diastime90=0;
diastime90abs=0;
diastime90old=0;

sys10=newArray();
sys50=newArray();
sys90=newArray();
sysuser=newArray();

dias10=newArray();
dias50=newArray();
dias90=newArray();
diasuser=newArray();

btime10=newArray();
btime50=newArray();
btime90=newArray();
btimeuser=newArray();

thres0line=newArray(amplitudes.length-1);
thres1line=newArray(amplitudes.length-1);
thres2line=newArray(amplitudes.length-1);
thres3line=newArray(amplitudes.length-1);


//********** Defining necessary constants ends here ********************

// ************ Printing the headlines starts here ********************


print("Frame #" + "\t" + "Time [sec]" + "\t" + "Amplitude [a.u.]" + "\t" + "Amplitude baselined [a.u.]" + "\t" + "Amplitude baselined nomalized [a.u.]" + "\t" + "1st deriv. of amplitude" + "\t" + "Absol. 1st deriv. of amplitude" + "\t" + "Maxima [a.u.]" + "\t" + "Loc. Maxamplitudes [a.u.]" + "\t" + "Minima [a.u.]" + "\t" + "Since last beat [sec]" + "\t" + "Since last beat abs. time [sec]" + "\t" + "Sum of beats" + "\t" + "User threshold (" + thresh0*100 + "%) [a.u.]" + "\t" + "Peak time user [sec]" + "\t" + "Peak time user absolute [sec]" + "\t" + "Contract. interval (user) [sec]" + "\t" + "Contract. interval (user) absol. [sec]" + "\t" + "Relax. interval (user) [sec]" + "\t" + "Relax. interval (user) absol. [sec]" + "\t" + "Thr(" + thresh1*100 + "%) [a.u.]" + "\t" + "Peak time Thr(" + thresh1*100 + "%) [sec]" + "\t" + "Peak time Thr(" + thresh1*100 + "%) absol. [sec]" + "\t" + "Contract. interval Thr(" + thresh1*100 + "%) [sec]" + "\t" + "Contract. interval Thr(" + thresh1*100 + "%) absol. [sec]" + "\t" + "Relax. interval Thr(" + thresh1*100 + "%) [sec]" + "\t" + "Relax. interval Thr(" + thresh1*100 + "%) absol. [sec]" + "\t" + "Thr(" + thresh2*100 + "%) [a.u.]" + "\t" + "Peak time Thr(" + thresh2*100 + "%) [sec]" + "\t" + "Peak time Thr(" + thresh2*100 + "%) absol. [sec]" + "\t" + "Contract. interval Thr(" + thresh2*100 + "%) [sec]" + "\t" + "Contract. interval Thr(" + thresh2*100 + "%) absol. [sec]" + "\t" + "Relax. interval Thr(" + thresh2*100 + "%) [sec]" + "\t" + "Relax. interval Thr(" + thresh2*100 + "%) absol. [sec]" + "\t" + "Thr(" + thresh3*100 + "%) [a.u.]" + "\t" + "Peak time Thr(" + thresh3*100 + "%) [sec]" + "\t" + "Peak time Thr(" + thresh3*100 + "%) absol. [sec]" + "\t" + "Contract. interval Thr(" + thresh3*100 + "%) [sec]" + "\t" + "Contract. interval Thr(" + thresh3*100 + "%) absol. [sec]" + "\t" + "Relax. interval Thr(" + thresh3*100 + "%) [sec]" + "\t" + "Relax. interval Thr(" + thresh3*100 + "%) absol. [sec]");


// ************ Printing the headlines ends here

for (rr=0; rr<amplitudes.length-1; rr++){

ampNorm = 0;

if (ampRange > 0) {
	ampNorm = (amplitudes[rr]-pmin)/ampRange;
}

if (isNaN(ampNorm)) {
	ampNorm = 0;
}

//******************** Calculation of the systoles and diastoles for the thresholds (user, 10, 50 and 90%) starts here *************************


if (rr>systuserstart[ampl] && rr<truncmax[ampl]){
	systime=systime+1/fps; 
	systimeold=systime;
}
 else {systime=0;}

// NEU for Gesamtsystole starts here *****************************************************************
if (rr==truncmax[ampl] && systime==0 && systime<=systimeold){
	systimeabs=systimeold;
	sysuser=Array.concat(sysuser, systimeabs);
	
}
 else {systimeabs="";}
// NEU for Gesamtsystole ends here ******************************************************************* 

if (rr>=truncmax[ampl] && rr<diastuserend[ampl]){
	diastime=diastime+1/fps;
	diastimeold=diastime;

}
 else {diastime=0;}


// NEU for GesamtDIAstole starts here *****************************************************************
 if (diastimeold>diastime){
	diastimeabs=diastimeold;
	diastimeold=0;
        diasuser=Array.concat(diasuser, diastimeabs);
}
 else {diastimeabs="";}
// NEU for GesamtDIAstole ends here ******************************************************************* 


if (rr>syst10start[ampl] && rr<truncmax[ampl]){
	systime10=systime10+1/fps;
	systime10old=systime10;
}
 else {systime10=0;}

// NEU for Gesamtsystole 10 starts here *****************************************************************
if (rr==truncmax[ampl] && systime10==0 && systime10<=systime10old){
	systime10abs=systime10old;
	sys10=Array.concat(sys10, systime10abs);
	
}
 else {systime10abs="";}
// NEU for Gesamtsystole 10 ends here ******************************************************************* 



if (rr>=truncmax[ampl] && rr<diast10end[ampl]){
	diastime10=diastime10+1/fps;
	diastime10old=diastime10;
}
 else {diastime10=0;}



// NEU fuer GesamtDIAstole 10 starts here *****************************************************************
 if (diastime10old>diastime10){
	diastime10abs=diastime10old;
	diastime10old=0;
	dias10=Array.concat(dias10, diastime10abs);
}
 else {diastime10abs="";}
// NEU for GesamtDIAstole 10 ends here ******************************************************************* 

if (rr>syst50start[ampl] && rr<truncmax[ampl]){
	systime50=systime50+1/fps;
	systime50old=systime50;
}
 else {systime50=0;}

// NEU for Gesamtsystole 50 starts here *****************************************************************
if (rr==truncmax[ampl] && systime50==0 && systime50<=systime50old){
	systime50abs=systime50old;
	sys50=Array.concat(sys50, systime50abs);
	
}
 else {systime50abs="";}
// NEU for Gesamtsystole 50 ends here ******************************************************************* 

 
if (rr>1){
if (rr>=truncmax[ampl] && rr<diast50end[ampl]){
	diastime50=diastime50+1/fps;
	diastime50old=diastime50;
}
 else {diastime50=0;}}


// NEU fuer GesamtDIAstole 50 starts here *****************************************************************
 if (diastime50old>diastime50){
	diastime50abs=diastime50old;
	diastime50old=0;
	dias50=Array.concat(dias50, diastime50abs);
}
 else {diastime50abs="";}
// NEU for GesamtDIAstole 50 ends here ******************************************************************* 


if (rr>syst90start[ampl] && rr<truncmax[ampl]){
	systime90=systime90+1/fps;
	systime90old=systime90;
}
 else {systime90=0;}


// NEU for Gesamtsystole 90 starts here *****************************************************************
if (rr==truncmax[ampl] && systime90==0 && systime90<=systime90old){
	systime90abs=systime90old;
	sys90=Array.concat(sys90, systime90abs);
	
}
 else {systime90abs="";}
// NEU for Gesamtsystole 90 ends here ******************************************************************* 


if (rr>1){
if (rr>=truncmax[ampl] && rr<diast90end[ampl]){
	diastime90=diastime90+1/fps;
	diastime90old=diastime90;
}
 else {diastime90=0;}}


// NEU for GesamtDIAstole 90 starts here *****************************************************************
 if (diastime90old>diastime90){
	diastime90abs=diastime90old;
	diastime90old=0;
	dias90=Array.concat(dias90, diastime90abs);
}
 else {diastime90abs="";}
// NEU for GesamtDIAstole 90 ends here ******************************************************************* 


// ************************** Calculation of peak times starts here ***************************


if (diastime>0 || systime>0){
	peaktime=peaktime+1/fps;
	peaktimeold=peaktime;

}
 else {peaktime=0;}

if(systime==(1/fps)){peaktime=(1/fps);}

// NEU for Gesamtpeakzeit starts here *****************************************************************

if (peaktimeold>peaktime){
	peaktimeabs=peaktimeold;
	peaktimeold=0;
	btimeuser=Array.concat(btimeuser, peaktimeabs);
}
 else {peaktimeabs="";}

// NEU for Gesamtpeakzeit ends here ******************************************************************* 

if (diastime10>0 || systime10>0){
	peaktime10=peaktime10+1/fps;
	peaktime10old=peaktime10;
}
 else {peaktime10=0;}

if(systime10==(1/fps)){peaktime10=(1/fps);}

// NEU for Gesamtpeakzeit 10 starts here *****************************************************************

if (peaktime10old>peaktime10){
	peaktime10abs=peaktime10old;
	peaktime10old=0;
	btime10=Array.concat(btime10, peaktime10abs);
}
 else {peaktime10abs="";}

// NEU for Gesamtpeakzeit 10 ends here ******************************************************************* 

if (diastime50>0 || systime50>0){
	peaktime50=peaktime50+1/fps;
	peaktime50old=peaktime50;
}
 else {peaktime50=0;}

if(systime50==(1/fps)){peaktime50=(1/fps);}

// NEU for Gesamtpeakzeit 50 starts here *****************************************************************

if (peaktime50old>peaktime50){
	peaktime50abs=peaktime50old;
	peaktime50old=0;
	btime50=Array.concat(btime50, peaktime50abs);
}
 else {peaktime50abs="";}

// NEU for Gesamtpeakzeit 50 ends here ******************************************************************* 


if (diastime90>0 || systime90>0){
	peaktime90=peaktime90+1/fps;
	peaktime90old=peaktime90;
}
 else {peaktime90=0;}

if(systime90==(1/fps)){peaktime90=(1/fps);}

 // NEU for Gesamtpeakzeit 90 starts here *****************************************************************

if (peaktime90old>peaktime90){
	peaktime90abs=peaktime90old;
	peaktime90old=0;
	btime90=Array.concat(btime90, peaktime90abs);
}
 else {peaktime90abs="";}

// NEU for Gesamtpeakzeit 90 ends here ******************************************************************* 




// ************************** Calculation of peak times ends here ***************************



//******************** Calculation of the systoles and diastoles for the thresholds (user, 10, 50 and 90%) ends here *************************

btimeold=btimea;
btimea=btimea+(1/fps);



if (systimeabs==0) {
systimeabs="";
}


if (systime10abs==0) {
systime10abs="";
}


if (systime50abs==0) {
systime50abs="";
}


if (systime90abs==0) {
systime90abs="";
}


if(minima[min]==rr) {
print((rr+1) + "\t" + rr/fps + "\t" + amplitudes[rr] + "\t" + (amplitudes[rr]-pmin) + "\t" + ampNorm + "\t" + (amplitudes[rr+1]-amplitudes[rr]) + "\t"  + abs((amplitudes[rr+1]-amplitudes[rr])) + "\t" + "0" + "\t" + "\t" + round(pmax+1) + "\t" + btimea + "\t" + "\t" + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(threshold*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime + "\t" + peaktimeabs + "\t" + systime + "\t" + systimeabs + "\t" + diastime + "\t" + diastimeabs + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh1*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime10 + "\t" + peaktime10abs + "\t" + systime10 + "\t" + systime10abs + "\t" + diastime10 + "\t" + diastime10abs + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh2*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime50 + "\t" + peaktime50abs + "\t" + systime50 + "\t" + systime50abs + "\t" + diastime50 + "\t" + diastime50abs + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh3*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime90 + "\t" + peaktime90abs + "\t" + systime90 + "\t" + systime90abs + "\t" + diastime90 + "\t" + diastime90abs);

thres0line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(threshold*maxamplitudes[ampl]));
thres1line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh1*maxamplitudes[ampl]));
thres2line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh2*maxamplitudes[ampl]));
thres3line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh3*maxamplitudes[ampl]));


min=min+1;
if (min>minima.length-1){
	min=minima.length-1;
}


} else if (maxima[max]==rr) {
spacer="";
if (rr==0){btimea=0; spacer=0;}
print((rr+1) + "\t" + rr/fps + "\t" + amplitudes[rr] + "\t" + (amplitudes[rr]-pmin) + "\t" + ampNorm + "\t" + (amplitudes[rr+1]-amplitudes[rr]) + "\t" + abs((amplitudes[rr+1]-amplitudes[rr])) + "\t" + round(pmax+1) + "\t" + maxamplitudes[ampl] + "\t" + "0" + "\t" + btimea + "\t" +spacer+  "\t" + beats + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(threshold*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime + "\t" + peaktimeabs + "\t" +  systime + "\t" + systimeabs + "\t" + diastime + "\t" + diastimeabs + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh1*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime10 + "\t" + peaktime10abs + "\t" + systime10 + "\t" + systime10abs + "\t" + diastime10 + "\t" + diastime10abs + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh2*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime50 + "\t" + peaktime50abs + "\t" + systime50 + "\t" + systime50abs + "\t" + diastime50 + "\t" + diastime50abs + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh3*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime90 + "\t" + peaktime90abs + "\t" + systime90 + "\t" + systime90abs + "\t" + diastime90 + "\t" + diastime90abs);
beattimes=Array.concat(beattimes,btimea);
btimea=0;
beats=beats+1;
max=max+1;


thres0line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(threshold*maxamplitudes[ampl]));
thres1line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh1*maxamplitudes[ampl]));
thres2line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh2*maxamplitudes[ampl]));
thres3line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh3*maxamplitudes[ampl]));


if (max>maxima.length-1){
	max=maxima.length-1;
}
} else {
print((rr+1) + "\t" + rr/fps + "\t" + amplitudes[rr] + "\t" + (amplitudes[rr]-pmin) + "\t" + ampNorm + "\t" + (amplitudes[rr+1]-amplitudes[rr]) + "\t" + abs((amplitudes[rr+1]-amplitudes[rr])) + "\t" + "0" + "\t" + "\t" + "0" + "\t" + btimea + "\t" + btimeabs + "\t" + "\t"  + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(threshold*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t"  + peaktime + "\t" + peaktimeabs + "\t" + systime + "\t" + systimeabs + "\t" + diastime + "\t" + diastimeabs + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh1*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime10 + "\t" + peaktime10abs + "\t" + systime10 + "\t" + systime10abs + "\t" + diastime10 + "\t" + diastime10abs + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh2*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime50 + "\t" + peaktime50abs + "\t" + systime50 + "\t" + systime50abs + "\t" + diastime50 + "\t" + diastime50abs + "\t" + (amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh3*maxamplitudes[ampl])) + "\t" + peaktime90 + "\t" + peaktime90abs + "\t" + systime90 + "\t" + systime90abs + "\t" + diastime90 + "\t" + diastime90abs);

thres0line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(threshold*maxamplitudes[ampl]));
thres1line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh1*maxamplitudes[ampl]));
thres2line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh2*maxamplitudes[ampl]));
thres3line[rr]=(amplitudes[truncmin[ampl]]+(thresh3*maxamplitudes[ampl]));


}

if (rr<amplitudes.length && ampl<truncmax.length-1){
	
if   (rr>=(truncmin[ampl+1])) {

	ampl=ampl+1;

}

}


// NEU for GesamtBeatzeit starts here *****************************************************************
 if (btimeold>btimea){
	btimeabs=btimeold+1/fps;
	btimeold=0;
}
 else {btimeabs="";}
// NEU for GesamtBeatzeit ends here ******************************************************************* 

}


// ****************** Getting statistics from the arrays starts here *********************************

Array.getStatistics(beattimes, beattimesmin, beattimesmax, beattimesmean, beattimesstdDev);
Array.getStatistics(maxamplitudes, maxamplitudesmin, maxamplitudesmax, maxamplitudesmean, maxamplitudesstd);

Array.getStatistics(dias90, dias90min, dias90max, dias90mean, dias90std);

frequencies=Array.copy(beattimes);
frequencies=Array.deleteValue(frequencies,0);

for (freq = 0; freq < frequencies.length; freq++) {
frequencies[freq]=1/frequencies[freq];	
}

Array.getStatistics(frequencies, freqmin, freqmax, freqmean, freqstd);


// ****************** Getting statistics from the arrays ends here **********************

//******************************Plotting the data starts here, thresholds are displayed, according images and numeric output can be saved ******************

allminima=newArray(amplitudes.length);
allmaxima=newArray(amplitudes.length);

Array.fill(allminima, 0);
Array.fill(allmaxima, 0);

for (allmax=0; allmax<maxima.length; allmax++){
	allmaxima[maxima[allmax]]=round(pmax+1);
	}


for (allmin=0; allmin<minima.length; allmin++){
	allminima[minima[allmin]]=round(pmax+1);
	}


times=newArray(amplitudes.length);

for (tt=0; tt<amplitudes.length; tt++) {
times[tt]=tt/fps;
}


run("Profile Plot Options...", "width=1920 height=700 font=10 minimum=pmin maximum=pmax draw draw_ticks interpolate sub-pixel");

Plot.create("Amplitudes", "Time [sec]", "Amplitude [a.u.]", times, amplitudes);
setJustification("center");
Plot.addText("Amplitude (black)", 0.1, 0);
Plot.addText("Maxima (red)", 0.2, 0);
Plot.addText("Minima (green)", 0.3, 0);
Plot.addText("Thr(" + 100*thresh0 + "%, orange)", 0.4, 0);
Plot.addText("Thr(" + 100*thresh1 + "%, cyan)", 0.55, 0);
Plot.addText("Thr(" + 100*thresh2 + "%, pink)", 0.7, 0);
Plot.addText("Thr(" + 100*thresh3 + "%, blue)", 0.85, 0);
Plot.addText("Det=" + detection, 0.95, 0);


Plot.setColor("red"); 
Plot.add("line", times, allmaxima);

Plot.setColor("green");
Plot.add("line", times, allminima);

Plot.setColor("pink");
Plot.setLineWidth(2);
Plot.add("line", times, thres2line);

Plot.setLineWidth(2);

// ************************************* DATA EXTRACTION for Statistics starts here

if (option == "7. Data Extraction") {

for (repeats = 0; repeats < 1000000; repeats++) {

// ****************** Header for date and time starts here


run("Colors...", "foreground=black background=black selection=yellow");
run("Set Measurements...", "area mean standard modal min centroid center perimeter bounding fit shape feret's integrated median skewness kurtosis area_fraction stack limit display redirect=None   decimal=3");
run("Input/Output...", "jpeg=90 gif=-1 file=.txt use_file copy_column copy_row save_column save_row");

getDateAndTime(year, month, dayOfWeek, dayOfMonth, hour, minute, second, msec);
MonthNames = newArray("Jan","Feb","Mar","Apr","May","Jun","Jul","Aug","Sep","Oct","Nov","Dec"); 

if (hour<10) {hours = "0"+hour;}
else {hours=hour;}
if (minute<10) {minutes = "0"+minute;}
else {minutes=minute;}
if (second<10) {seconds = "0"+second;}
else {seconds=second;}
if (month<10) {months = "0"+(month+1);}
else {months=month+1;}
if (dayOfMonth<10) {dayOfMonths = "0"+dayOfMonth;}
else {dayOfMonths=dayOfMonth;}

// ****************** Header for date and time ends here

// Read the Data-File 

// extract correct path and filename
	
pathfile=File.openDialog("Please choose a <Results>-file to be opened for extraction:");

print(pathfile);

data=File.openAsString(pathfile);

strt=lastIndexOf(pathfile, "\\");
dir=substring(pathfile, 0, strt+1);

filename=substring(pathfile, strt+1, lengthOf(pathfile));
filename=replace(filename, ".txt", "");



// Neuer Code fuer die Extraktion START hier


// --- Zeilenenden zuerst normalisieren ---
data = replace(data, "\r\n", "\n");
data = replace(data, "\r", "\n");

// --- Funktionen für Tab-Ersetzung ---
function tabs(n) {
    s = "";
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++) s = s + "\t";
    return s;
}
function repNoNL(n) {
    s = "\t";
    for (i = 1; i < n; i++) s = s + "gap\t";
    return s;
}
function repNL(n) {
    s = "";
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++) s = s + "\tgap";
    s = s + "\n";
    return s;
}

// --- Lücken (Tabs) bis Länge 35 in "gap" umwandeln ---
for (n = 35; n >= 2; n--) {
    data = replace(data, tabs(n) + "\n", repNL(n));
    data = replace(data, tabs(n), repNoNL(n));
}

// --- Sonderfall: genau ein fehlendes Feld am Zeilenende ---
data = replace(data, "\t\n", "\tgap\n");

// --- NaN durch -1 ersetzen ---
data = replace(data, "\tNaN", "\t-1");

// --- Splitten ---
lines = split(data, "\n");

// --- Tab-Zählfunktion ---
function countTabs(s) {
    c = 0;
    for (k = 0; k < lengthOf(s); k++) if (substring(s, k, k+1) == "\t") c++;
    return c;
}

Headline = lines[3];

// --- Zeilen filtern (nur mit Ziffern und >= 40 Spalten) ---
newLines = newArray(lines.length);
j = 0;
for (i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
    line = lines[i];
    if (matches(line, "^[0-9].*")) {
        splittest = split(line, "\t");
        if (splittest.length >= 40) newLines[j++] = line;
    }
}
newLines = Array.slice(newLines, 0, j);

// --- Fehlende Spalten auffüllen ---
expectedCols = countTabs(Headline) + 1;
expectedTabs = expectedCols - 1;
fixed = newArray(newLines.length);
for (i = 0; i < newLines.length; i++) {
    line = newLines[i];
    tcnt = countTabs(line);
    while (tcnt < expectedTabs) {
        line += "\tgap";
        tcnt++;
    }
    fixed[i] = line;
}
lines = fixed;

// --- Arrays für Ausgabe vorbereiten ---
maxamplitudes = newArray(lines.length); sincelastbeatabs = newArray(lines.length);
peakuserabs = newArray(lines.length); systuserabs = newArray(lines.length); diasuserabs = newArray(lines.length);
peak10abs = newArray(lines.length); syst10abs = newArray(lines.length); dias10abs = newArray(lines.length);
peak50abs = newArray(lines.length); syst50abs = newArray(lines.length); dias50abs = newArray(lines.length);
peak90abs = newArray(lines.length); syst90abs = newArray(lines.length); dias90abs = newArray(lines.length);
FinalMaxima = newArray(lines.length);
FrameNumbers = newArray(lines.length); Times = newArray(lines.length);
AllMinima = newArray(lines.length); AllMaxima = newArray(lines.length);

// --- Maxima finden ---
maxCount = 0;
for (dist = 0; dist < lines.length; dist++) {
    SingleData = split(lines[dist], "\t");
    if (parseFloat(SingleData[9]) > 0) {
        AllMaxima[maxCount++] = dist;
    }
}
AllMaxima = Array.slice(AllMaxima, 0, maxCount);

// --- Kontraktionen verarbeiten ---
finalCount = 0;
for (max = 0; max < AllMaxima.length-1; max++) {
    Start = AllMaxima[max];
    Stop = AllMaxima[max+1];

    Tempmaxamplitudes = -1; Tempsincelastbeatabs = -1;
    Temppeakuserabs = -1; Tempsystuserabs = -1; Tempdiasuserabs = -1;
    Temppeak10abs = -1; Tempsyst10abs = -1; Tempdias10abs = -1;
    Temppeak50abs = -1; Tempsyst50abs = -1; Tempdias50abs = -1;
    Temppeak90abs = -1; Tempsyst90abs = -1; Tempdias90abs = -1;
 
    for (range = Start; range < Stop; range++) {
        SingleData = split(lines[range], "\t");

        if (Tempmaxamplitudes < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[10], "gap") < 0) Tempmaxamplitudes = SingleData[10];
        if (Tempsincelastbeatabs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[13], "gap") < 0) Tempsincelastbeatabs = SingleData[13];
        if (Temppeakuserabs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[17], "gap") < 0) Temppeakuserabs = SingleData[17];
        if (Tempsystuserabs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[19], "gap") < 0) Tempsystuserabs = SingleData[19];
        if (Tempdiasuserabs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[21], "gap") < 0) Tempdiasuserabs = SingleData[21];
        if (Temppeak10abs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[24], "gap") < 0) Temppeak10abs = SingleData[24];
        if (Tempsyst10abs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[26], "gap") < 0) Tempsyst10abs = SingleData[26];
        if (Tempdias10abs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[28], "gap") < 0) Tempdias10abs = SingleData[28];
        if (Temppeak50abs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[31], "gap") < 0) Temppeak50abs = SingleData[31];
        if (Tempsyst50abs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[33], "gap") < 0) Tempsyst50abs = SingleData[33];
        if (Tempdias50abs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[35], "gap") < 0) Tempdias50abs = SingleData[35];
        if (Temppeak90abs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[38], "gap") < 0) Temppeak90abs = SingleData[38];
        if (Tempsyst90abs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[40], "gap") < 0) Tempsyst90abs = SingleData[40];
        if (Tempdias90abs < 0 && indexOf(SingleData[42], "gap") < 0) Tempdias90abs = SingleData[42];
    }



    if (Tempmaxamplitudes > -1 && Tempsincelastbeatabs > 0 && Temppeakuserabs > -1 && Tempsystuserabs > -1 && Tempdiasuserabs > -1 &&
        Temppeak10abs > -1 && Tempsyst10abs > -1 && Tempdias10abs > -1 && Temppeak50abs > -1 && Tempsyst50abs > -1 && Tempdias50abs > -1 &&
        Temppeak90abs > -1 && Tempsyst90abs > -1 && Tempdias90abs > -1) {
        

// Hier müssen noch weitere Optionen hin; eine Option ist die Summenbildung aus Systole und Diastole; weicht die zu sehr ab, dann raus mit der Zeile!

RandDatensatz = 0;



if (abs(parseFloat(Temppeakuserabs) - (parseFloat(Tempsystuserabs) + parseFloat(Tempdiasuserabs))) > parseFloat(0.15)) { RandDatensatz = 1; }
if (abs(parseFloat(Temppeak10abs)  - (parseFloat(Tempsyst10abs)  + parseFloat(Tempdias10abs)))  > parseFloat(0.15)) { RandDatensatz = 1; }
if (abs(parseFloat(Temppeak50abs)  - (parseFloat(Tempsyst50abs)  + parseFloat(Tempdias50abs)))  > parseFloat(0.15)) { RandDatensatz = 1; }
if (abs(parseFloat(Temppeak90abs)  - (parseFloat(Tempsyst90abs)  + parseFloat(Tempdias90abs)))  > parseFloat(0.15)) { RandDatensatz = 1; }

if(RandDatensatz<1){

        FinalMaxima[finalCount] = Start + 1;
        maxamplitudes[finalCount] = Tempmaxamplitudes;
        sincelastbeatabs[finalCount] = Tempsincelastbeatabs;
        peakuserabs[finalCount] = Temppeakuserabs;
        systuserabs[finalCount] = Tempsystuserabs;
        diasuserabs[finalCount] = Tempdiasuserabs;
        peak10abs[finalCount] = Temppeak10abs;
        syst10abs[finalCount] = Tempsyst10abs;
        dias10abs[finalCount] = Tempdias10abs;
        peak50abs[finalCount] = Temppeak50abs;
        syst50abs[finalCount] = Tempsyst50abs;
        dias50abs[finalCount] = Tempdias50abs;
        peak90abs[finalCount] = Temppeak90abs;
        syst90abs[finalCount] = Tempsyst90abs;
        dias90abs[finalCount] = Tempdias90abs;
        finalCount++;
}
    
    }
}

// --- Arrays kürzen ---
FinalMaxima = Array.slice(FinalMaxima, 0, finalCount);
maxamplitudes = Array.slice(maxamplitudes, 0, finalCount);
sincelastbeatabs = Array.slice(sincelastbeatabs, 0, finalCount);
peakuserabs = Array.slice(peakuserabs, 0, finalCount);
systuserabs = Array.slice(systuserabs, 0, finalCount);
diasuserabs = Array.slice(diasuserabs, 0, finalCount);
peak10abs = Array.slice(peak10abs, 0, finalCount);
syst10abs = Array.slice(syst10abs, 0, finalCount);
dias10abs = Array.slice(dias10abs, 0, finalCount);
peak50abs = Array.slice(peak50abs, 0, finalCount);
syst50abs = Array.slice(syst50abs, 0, finalCount);
dias50abs = Array.slice(dias50abs, 0, finalCount);
peak90abs = Array.slice(peak90abs, 0, finalCount);
syst90abs = Array.slice(syst90abs, 0, finalCount);
dias90abs = Array.slice(dias90abs, 0, finalCount);


// //Bevor wir mit diesen Daten irgendwas rechnen, muessen die alle geparsefloated werden!!!

// Hilfsfunktion: wandelt alle Elemente eines Arrays in Float
function convertToFloat(arr) {
    for (i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
        arr[i] = parseFloat(arr[i]);
    }
    return arr;
}

// Jetzt für alle deine Arrays anwenden
FinalMaxima       = convertToFloat(FinalMaxima);
maxamplitudes     = convertToFloat(maxamplitudes);
sincelastbeatabs  = convertToFloat(sincelastbeatabs);
peakuserabs       = convertToFloat(peakuserabs);
systuserabs       = convertToFloat(systuserabs);
diasuserabs       = convertToFloat(diasuserabs);
peak10abs         = convertToFloat(peak10abs);
syst10abs         = convertToFloat(syst10abs);
dias10abs         = convertToFloat(dias10abs);
peak50abs         = convertToFloat(peak50abs);
syst50abs         = convertToFloat(syst50abs);
dias50abs         = convertToFloat(dias50abs);
peak90abs         = convertToFloat(peak90abs);
syst90abs         = convertToFloat(syst90abs);
dias90abs         = convertToFloat(dias90abs);


// Neuer Code fuer die Extraktion ENDE hier


// Neue Statistik und Bildausgabe
// Aus den obigen Datenarrays direkt Abbildungen fertigen

// =================================================================
// 1. ALLGEMEINE EINSTELLUNGEN UND DATEN-INITIALISIERUNG
// =================================================================
PlotBoxHeight = 800;
PlotBoxWidth = 1350;
Schriftgroesse = 25;

Array.getStatistics(peakuserabs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}
Array.getStatistics(systuserabs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}
Array.getStatistics(diasuserabs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}
Array.getStatistics(peak10abs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}
Array.getStatistics(syst10abs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}
Array.getStatistics(dias10abs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}
Array.getStatistics(peak50abs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}
Array.getStatistics(syst50abs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}
Array.getStatistics(dias50abs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}
Array.getStatistics(peak90abs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}
Array.getStatistics(syst90abs, min, max, mean, stdDev); Means3=Array.concat(Means3,mean); StdDevs3=Array.concat(StdDevs3,stdDev); if((mean+stdDev)>AbsMaxNorm3){AbsMaxNorm3=mean+stdDev;}

// =================================================================
// 4. DEFINITION DER WIEDERVERWENDBAREN ZEICHENFUNKTION
// =================================================================
function zeichnePanel(xOffset, panelMeans, panelStdDevs, panelArrayNamen, panelAbsMaxNorm, panelID) {
    yPadding = 200;
    plotHeight = PlotBoxHeight - yPadding;

    // Workaround for ceil() using floor()
    if (panelAbsMaxNorm <= 0) panelAbsMaxNorm = 1; // Avoid division by zero
    tempVal = panelAbsMaxNorm;
    if (tempVal < 1) {
        step = 0.1;
    } else if (tempVal < 10) {
        step = 1;
    } else {
        step = 10;
    }
    panelMaxY = (floor(tempVal / step) + 1) * step; // Mimics ceil behavior

    Normierungsfaktor = plotHeight / panelMaxY;

    barWidth = 30;
    if (panelMeans.length > 1) {
        barSpacing = 40;
    } else {
        barSpacing = 0;
    }
    startX = xOffset + 60;

    setColor(0,0,0);
    setLineWidth(2);
    panelWidth = (panelMeans.length * (barWidth + barSpacing)) - barSpacing + 20;
    if (panelMeans.length == 1) {
        panelWidth = barWidth + 20;
    }
        
    drawLine(startX - 15, yPadding / 2, startX + panelWidth, yPadding / 2); // Top line
    drawLine(startX - 15, plotHeight + (yPadding / 2), startX + panelWidth, plotHeight + (yPadding / 2)); // Bottom line
    drawLine(startX - 10, yPadding / 2, startX - 10, plotHeight + (yPadding / 2)); // Left line
    drawLine(startX + panelWidth, yPadding / 2, startX + panelWidth, plotHeight + (yPadding / 2)); // Right line

    // Draw vertical y-axis label
    setFont("SansSerif", Schriftgroesse);
    if (panelID == 1) {label = yLabel1; LabelPosY=30; totalLabelHeight = lengthOf(label)*(Schriftgroesse*0.82); LabelPosX=PlotBoxHeight/2-totalLabelHeight/3;}
    else if (panelID == 2) {label = yLabel2; LabelPosY=220; totalLabelHeight = lengthOf(label)*(Schriftgroesse*0.82);  LabelPosX=PlotBoxHeight/2-totalLabelHeight/3;}
    else {label = yLabel3; LabelPosY=420; totalLabelHeight = lengthOf(label)*(Schriftgroesse*0.82); LabelPosX=PlotBoxHeight/2-totalLabelHeight/4;}
    
    run("Rotate 90 Degrees Right");
    drawString(label, LabelPosX, LabelPosY);  
    run("Rotate 90 Degrees Left");

    setFont("SansSerif", Schriftgroesse - 10);
    for (j = 0; j < panelMeans.length; j++) {
        xPos = startX + j * (barWidth + barSpacing);
        meanHeight = panelMeans[j] * Normierungsfaktor;
        stdDevHeight = panelStdDevs[j] * Normierungsfaktor;
        yPos = plotHeight - meanHeight + (yPadding / 2);

        if (panelID == 3) {
            colorIndex = j + 2;
        } else {
            colorIndex = panelID - 1;
        }

        if(colorIndex>=2 && colorIndex<=4){setColor(255,0,0);}
        else if(colorIndex>=5 && colorIndex<=7){setColor(0,200,0);}
        else if(colorIndex>=8 && colorIndex<=10){setColor(0,0, 255);}
        else if(colorIndex>=11 && colorIndex<=13){setColor(255,128, 0);}
        else if(colorIndex==1){setColor(0,128,255);}
        else{setColor(128,128,128);}

        fillRect(xPos, yPos, barWidth, meanHeight);

        setColor(0,0,0);
        drawRect(xPos, yPos, barWidth, meanHeight);

        stdDevTopY = yPos - stdDevHeight;
        drawLine(xPos + barWidth/2, yPos, xPos + barWidth/2, stdDevTopY);
        drawLine(xPos, stdDevTopY, xPos + barWidth, stdDevTopY);

        if(j%2==0){drawString(panelArrayNamen[j], xPos-Schriftgroesse/2, plotHeight + 100+Schriftgroesse);}else{drawString(panelArrayNamen[j], xPos-Schriftgroesse/2, plotHeight + 100+(2*Schriftgroesse));}
    }

    setFont("SansSerif", Schriftgroesse - 5);
    for (i = 0; i <= 10; i++) {
        val = panelMaxY * (i / 10.0);
        yTickPos = plotHeight + (yPadding / 2) - (plotHeight * (i / 10.0));
        // Replace ternary operator with if/else if
        if (panelMaxY < 1) {
            decimals = 2;
        } else if (panelMaxY < 10) {
            decimals = 1;
        } else {
            decimals = 0;
        }
        drawString(d2s(val, decimals), xOffset + 5, yTickPos + (Schriftgroesse / 3));
        drawLine(startX - 10, yTickPos, startX - 5, yTickPos);
    }
}


// Erstellten Plot speichern und dann schliessen

selectWindow("Multi-Panel BoxPlot");
saveAs("Jpeg", dir+"Extracted results Plot "+filename+".jpg");
close("Multi-Panel BoxPlot");

// =====================
// HISTOGRAMM MIT ACHSENBESCHRIFTUNGEN
// =====================
function drawHistogramWithLabels(values, title, xAxisLabel, yAxisLabel) {
    bins = 20;
    Array.getStatistics(values, vmin, vmax, vmean, vsd);
    if (vmin==vmax) { vmin = vmin - 1e-9; vmax = vmax + 1e-9; }
    binWidth = (vmax - vmin) / bins;

    // Histogrammdaten
    h = newArray(bins); for (i=0;i<bins;i++) h[i]=0;
    for (i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
        b = floor((values[i] - vmin) / binWidth);
        if (b < 0) b = 0; if (b >= bins) b = bins - 1;
        h[b]++;
    }

    // Canvas
    W = 900; H = 650;
    newImage(title, "RGB white", W, H, 1);
    setFont("SansSerif", 12);
    setColor(0,0,0);

    // Ränder und Plotfläche
    marginL=80; marginR=40; marginT=50; marginB=110;
    plotW = W - marginL - marginR;
    plotH = H - marginT - marginB;

    // Achsen
    setLineWidth(2);
    drawRect(marginL, marginT, plotW, plotH);
    // Y-Skalierung
    Array.getStatistics(h, hmin, hmax, hmean, hsd);
    if (hmax<1) hmax=1;
    scaleY = plotH / hmax;
    barW = plotW / bins;

    // ======= NEU: Balkenfarbe je Parameter wählen (nur Farbe, keine Logik geändert) =======
    function BalkenFarbeFestlegen(){
    if (indexOf(xAxisLabel, "Max. amplitude") >= 0) {setColor(128,128,128);}           // Mittelgrau
    else if (indexOf(xAxisLabel, "Time between contractions") >= 0) {setColor(0,128,255);} // Hellblau
    else if (indexOf(xAxisLabel, "user") >= 0 || indexOf(xAxisLabel, "User") >= 0) {setColor(255,0,0);} // Rot
    else if (indexOf(xAxisLabel, "10%") >= 0) {setColor(0,200,0);}                       // Grün
    else if (indexOf(xAxisLabel, "50%") >= 0) {setColor(0,0,255);}                       // Blau
    else if (indexOf(xAxisLabel, "90%") >= 0) {setColor(255,128,0);}                     // Orange
    }
    
    // ======= ENDE NEU =======

    // Balken + X-Werte (Bin-Mitte)
    for (b = 0; b < bins; b++) {
        bh = h[b] * scaleY;
        x = marginL + b * barW;
        y = marginT + plotH - bh;

        BalkenFarbeFestlegen();                // <— hier die gewählte Farbe verwenden
        fillRect(x+1, y, barW-2, bh);
        setColor(0,0,0);
        drawRect(x+1, y, barW-2, bh);

        // Bin-Mitte beschriften
        xm = vmin + (b+0.5)*binWidth;
        drawString(d2s(xm, 2), x+2, marginT + plotH + 25);
    }

    // X-Achsenlabel
    setFont("SansSerif", 20);
    drawString(xAxisLabel, marginL + (plotW/2) - (getStringWidth(xAxisLabel)/2), H - 40);

    // Y-Achsenlabel (vertikal, via Rotation)
    run("Rotate 90 Degrees Right");
    setFont("SansSerif", 20);
    drawString(yAxisLabel, (getWidth()/2) - (getStringWidth(yAxisLabel)/2), 50);
    run("Rotate 90 Degrees Left");

    // Titelinfo
    setFont("SansSerif", 16);
    drawString("n="+values.length+", mean="+d2s(vmean,3)+", sd="+d2s(vsd,3),
               marginL, marginT - 15);


title2=replace(title, "Histogram: ", "");

saveAs("Jpeg", dir+"Histogram "+ title2+".jpg");

selectWindow(title);
close();

}

// =====================

xLabelSys = "Systolic time [s]";
yLabelDia = "Diastolic time [s]";

// =====================
// SCATTER: Systole vs Diastole (equal scale + diagonal)
// =====================
function scatterSysDia(sysArr, diaArr, title, xAxisLabel, yAxisLabel) {
    n = minOf(sysArr.length, diaArr.length);
    if (n <= 0) return;

    // Bereich mit gleichem Maßstab (X und Y gemeinsam)
    Array.getStatistics(sysArr, smin, smax, smean, ssd);
    Array.getStatistics(diaArr, dmin, dmax, dmean, dsd);
    xmin = minOf(smin, dmin);
    xmax = maxOf(smax, dmax);
    if (xmin == xmax) { xmin = xmin - 1e-9; xmax = xmax + 1e-9; }

    // Canvas
    W = 900; H = 700;
    marginL = 90; marginR = 40; marginT = 60; marginB = 110;
    plotW = W - marginL - marginR;
    plotH = H - marginT - marginB;

    newImage(title, "RGB white", W, H, 1);
    setColor(0,0,0);
    setLineWidth(2);

    // Rahmen/Achsen
    drawRect(marginL, marginT, plotW, plotH);

    // Diagonale (y=x, gleicher Maßstab)
    x1 = marginL;                y1 = marginT + plotH;  // (xmin,xmin)
    x2 = marginL + plotW;        y2 = marginT;          // (xmax,xmax)
    setColor(200,0,0);
    drawLine(x1, y1, x2, y2);
    setColor(0,0,0);

    // Ticks & numerische Skala (5 Teilstriche)
    nt = 5;
    step = (xmax - xmin) / nt;
    if (step <= 0) step = 1e-3;

    // Dezimalstellen wie bei dir (grobe Heuristik)
    if (xmax - xmin < 1) decimals = 2;
    else if (xmax - xmin < 10) decimals = 1;
    else decimals = 0;

    setFont("SansSerif", 16);
    for (t = 0; t <= nt; t++) {
        val = xmin + t * step;

        // X-Tick
        px = marginL + ( (val - xmin) / (xmax - xmin) ) * plotW;
        drawLine(px, marginT + plotH, px, marginT + plotH + 6);
        drawString(d2s(val, decimals), px - 12, marginT + plotH + 26);

        // Y-Tick (gleicher Wertebereich)
        py = marginT + plotH - ( (val - xmin) / (xmax - xmin) ) * plotH;
        drawLine(marginL - 6, py, marginL, py);
        drawString(d2s(val, decimals), marginL - 60, py + 6);
    }

    // Punkte (kleine Kreuze)
    setLineWidth(1);
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        vx = sysArr[i]; vy = diaArr[i];
        px = marginL + ( (vx - xmin) / (xmax - xmin) ) * plotW;
        py = marginT + plotH - ( (vy - xmin) / (xmax - xmin) ) * plotH; // gleicher Maßstab
        drawLine(px-2, py-2, px+2, py+2);
        drawLine(px-2, py+2, px+2, py-2);
    }

    // X-Achsenlabel
    setFont("SansSerif", 20);
    drawString(xAxisLabel, marginL + (plotW/2) - (getStringWidth(xAxisLabel)/2), H - 40);

    // Y-Achsenlabel (vertikal wie in deinem Code)
    run("Rotate 90 Degrees Right");
    setFont("SansSerif", 20);
    drawString(yAxisLabel, (getWidth()/2) - (getStringWidth(yAxisLabel)/2), 30);
    run("Rotate 90 Degrees Left");

    // Infozeile (n)
    setFont("SansSerif", 16);
    drawString("n = " + n, marginL, marginT - 15);
}

// =====================
// 4) CORRELATION MATRIX (PEARSON-r) + HEATMAP
// =====================

// Kurze Labels für die Matrix (Reihenfolge = Datenarrays unten)
corrLabels = newArray(
  "MaxAmp","Beat",
  "UserPeak","UserSys","UserDia",
  "10Peak","10Sys","10Dia",
  "50Peak","50Sys","50Dia",
  "90Peak","90Sys","90Dia"
);

// --- Zugriff auf deine Arrays ohne Arrays-von-Arrays ---
function getLen(idx) {
  if (idx==0)  return maxamplitudes.length;
  if (idx==1)  return sincelastbeatabs.length;

  if (idx==2)  return peakuserabs.length;
  if (idx==3)  return systuserabs.length;
  if (idx==4)  return diasuserabs.length;

  if (idx==5)  return peak10abs.length;
  if (idx==6)  return syst10abs.length;
  if (idx==7)  return dias10abs.length;

  if (idx==8)  return peak50abs.length;
  if (idx==9)  return syst50abs.length;
  if (idx==10) return dias50abs.length;

  if (idx==11) return peak90abs.length;
  if (idx==12) return syst90abs.length;
  if (idx==13) return dias90abs.length;
  return 0;
}
function getVal(idx, k) {
  if (idx==0)  return maxamplitudes[k];
  if (idx==1)  return sincelastbeatabs[k];

  if (idx==2)  return peakuserabs[k];
  if (idx==3)  return systuserabs[k];
  if (idx==4)  return diasuserabs[k];

  if (idx==5)  return peak10abs[k];
  if (idx==6)  return syst10abs[k];
  if (idx==7)  return dias10abs[k];

  if (idx==8)  return peak50abs[k];
  if (idx==9)  return syst50abs[k];
  if (idx==10) return dias50abs[k];

  if (idx==11) return peak90abs[k];
  if (idx==12) return syst90abs[k];
  if (idx==13) return dias90abs[k];
  return NaN;
}

// Pearson-r zwischen zwei Datensätzen (über minimale gemeinsame Länge)
function pearsonIdx(i, j) {
  nA = getLen(i);
  nB = getLen(j);
  if (nA == 0 || nB == 0) return NaN; // Schutz vor leeren Arrays
  n = minOf(nA, nB);
  if (n < 2) return NaN;

  // Mittelwerte
  sx = 0.0; sy = 0.0; validCount = 0;
  for (k = 0; k < n; k++) {
    valX = getVal(i, k);
    valY = getVal(j, k);
    if (valX == valX && valY == valY) { // Prüft, ob nicht NaN
      sx += valX;
      sy += valY;
      validCount++;
    }
  }
  if (validCount < 2) return NaN;
  mx = sx / validCount; my = sy / validCount;

  // Kovarianz & Varianzen
  num = 0; dx = 0; dy = 0;
  for (k = 0; k < n; k++) {
    valX = getVal(i, k);
    valY = getVal(j, k);
    if (valX == valX && valY == valY) { // Prüft, ob nicht NaN
      vx = valX - mx;
      vy = valY - my;
      num += vx * vy;
      dx += vx * vx;
      dy += vy * vy;
    }
  }
  den = sqrt(dx * dy);
  if (den == 0) return NaN;
  return num / den;
}

// Farbabbildung r∈[-1,1] → (blau-weiß-rot)
function rgbFromR(r) {
  if (r!=r) r = 0;           // NaN → 0
  t = (r + 1) / 2;           // 0..1
  R = floor(255 * t);
  G = floor(255 * (1 - abs(r)));
  B = floor(255 * (1 - t));
  return newArray(R, G, B);
}

// Heatmap zeichnen & optional speichern
function drawCorrHeatmap(labels, title, outPath) {
  m = labels.length;

  // r-Matrix flach anlegen
  rflat = newArray(m * m);
  for (i = 0; i < m; i++) {
    for (j = 0; j < m; j++) {
      rflat[i * m + j] = pearsonIdx(i, j);
    }
  }

  // Canvasgröße
  cell = 46;                     // Zellgröße (anpassbar)
  margin = 120;
  W = margin + m * cell + margin;
  H = margin + m * cell + margin;

  newImage(title, "RGB white", W, H, 1);
  setFont("SansSerif", 14);

  // Zellen zeichnen
  for (i = 0; i < m; i++) {
    for (j = 0; j < m; j++) {
      r = rflat[i * m + j];
      rgb = rgbFromR(r);
      setColor(rgb[0], rgb[1], rgb[2]);
      x = margin + j * cell;
      y = margin + i * cell;
      fillRect(x, y, cell, cell);
      setColor(0,0,0);
      drawRect(x, y, cell, cell);

      // r-Wert beschriften
      setFont("SansSerif", 14);
      setColor(0,0,0);
      drawString(d2s(r, 2), x + 6, y + cell/2 + 4);
    }
  }

  // Row-Labels links
  setFont("SansSerif", 16);
  for (i = 0; i < m; i++) {
    drawString(labels[i], margin - 10 - getStringWidth(labels[i]),
               margin + i * cell + cell * 0.65);
  }

  // Column-Labels oben (hochkant)
  setFont("SansSerif", 16);
  
  run("Rotate 90 Degrees Left");
  
  labels2=Array.copy(labels);
  labels2=Array.reverse(labels2);
  
  for (j = 0; j < m; j++) {
    tx = margin+15  + j * cell + cell * 0.35; // X-Position: Mitte der Zelle
    ty = margin -85; // Y-Position: oberhalb der Matrix
    drawString(labels2[j], ty, tx); // Nach Rotation: X/Y getauscht   
  }

run("Rotate 90 Degrees Right");

  // Rahmen um gesamte Matrix
  setColor(0,0,0); setLineWidth(2);
  drawRect(margin, margin, m * cell, m * cell);

  // Legende (-1..1)
  lx = margin; ly = margin + m * cell + 40; lw = m * cell; lh = 15;
  for (p = 0; p <= lw; p++) {
    r = (p / lw) * 2 - 1;    // -1..1
    rgb = rgbFromR(r);
    setColor(rgb[0], rgb[1], rgb[2]);
    drawLine(lx + p, ly, lx + p, ly + lh);
  }
  setColor(0,0,0); setLineWidth(1);
  drawRect(lx, ly, lw, lh);
  setFont("SansSerif", 14);
  drawString("-1", lx - 10, ly + lh + 18);
  drawString("0",  lx + lw/2 - 4, ly + lh + 18);
  drawString("1",  lx + lw - 4,   ly + lh + 18);

  // Titel
  setFont("SansSerif", 18);
  drawString(title, margin, margin - 90);

  // speichern
  if (outPath != "") saveAs("Jpeg", outPath);
  close("*");
}

// ===== Aufruf =====
drawCorrHeatmap(corrLabels, "Correlation heatmap (Pearson r)", dir + "CorrHeatmap_" + filename + ".jpg");


// --- Finale Datenausgabe ---

print("\\Clear");
print("Loc. Maxamplitude [a.u]\tSince last beat abs. time [sec]\tPeak time user absolute [sec]\tContract. interval (user) absol. [sec]\tRelax. interval (user) absol. [sec]\tPeak time Thr(10%) absol. [sec]\tContract. interval Thr(10%) absol. [sec]\tRelax. interval Thr(10%) absol. [sec]\tPeak time Thr(50%) absol. [sec]\tContract. interval Thr(50%) absol. [sec]\tRelax. interval Thr(50%) absol. [sec]\tPeak time Thr(90%) absol. [sec]\tContract. interval Thr(90%) absol. [sec]\tRelax. interval Thr(90%) absol. [sec]");

for (prn = 0; prn < FinalMaxima.length; prn++) {
    print(maxamplitudes[prn] + "\t" + sincelastbeatabs[prn] + "\t" +
          peakuserabs[prn] + "\t" + systuserabs[prn] + "\t" + diasuserabs[prn] + "\t" +
          peak10abs[prn] + "\t" + syst10abs[prn] + "\t" + dias10abs[prn] + "\t" +
          peak50abs[prn] + "\t" + syst50abs[prn] + "\t" + dias50abs[prn] + "\t" +
          peak90abs[prn] + "\t" + syst90abs[prn] + "\t" + dias90abs[prn]);
}


extract=getInfo("log");

File.saveString(extract, dir + "Extracted results (eng) "+ filename + ".txt");

extract=replace(extract, ".", ",");
extract=replace(extract, "\\[a,u\\]", "[a.u]");

File.saveString(extract, dir + "Extracted results (ger) "+ filename + ".txt");



// ***** The COMPLETE DATA EXTRACTION ends here

}

}

    // Den letzten Backslash vor "\VidsMovement" finden

    // Verzeichnistitel extrahieren (zwischen dem letzten Backslash und "\VidsMovement")
    if (lastSlashIndex != -1) {

    }

// Statistics for the selected/included samples of a single experiment

if (option == "9. Statistics for selected Samples") {

for (LoopIt = 0; LoopIt < 1000000; LoopIt++) {


print("\\Clear");

else {hours=hour;}
if (minute<10) {minutes = "0"+minute;}
else {minutes=minute;}

else {months=month+1;}

else {dayOfMonths=dayOfMonth;}

// Das sind die Namen der ausgewerteten Zellen; die werden nur einmal ausgelesen
Cells=newArray();

// Das ist die Zeile, in der die entsprechenden Daten der Einzelzelle beginnen
CellsDataStart=newArray();

// FIX: Merkt sich, welche Zellen später wirklich in ANOVA/Heatmaps enthalten sind
UsedInANOVA = newArray();   // wird nach dem Einlesen von Cells initialisiert

ANOVAAmplitude=newArray();
 ANOVAContThr10=newArray();

Lines=split(data, "\n\r");

// Cells => Name der Einzelzelle
// CellsDataStart hier faengt der eigentliche Datensatz besagter Zelle an

for (i = 0; i < Lines.length; i++) {

	}

// Und das hier ist die komplette Liste mit Name und Startzeile, die ich zur Uebersicht ausgebe

}

// FIX: UsedInANOVA passend zur Anzahl Cells initialisieren

for (i = 0; i < Cells.length; i++) UsedInANOVA[i] = 0;

for (cls = 0; cls < Cells.length; cls++) {

// Das hier wird immer frisch und neu definiert
MainParameters=newArray();

// Hier lesen wir den aktuellen Namen der verarbeiteten Einzelzelle ein
CurrentSampleName=Cells[cls];

// Wir extrahieren solange, bis die Zeile aus keinen Unterelementen mehr besteht!
// Haben wir bei der letzten Einzelzelle nur eine Startzeile, dann lesen wir bis zum Ende des Lines-Arrays

StartLine=CellsDataStart[cls];
if(cls<CellsDataStart.length-1){StopLine=CellsDataStart[cls+1];}else{StopLine=Lines.length;}

// Problem, die Tabs werden zusammen mit leeren Elementen allesamt komplett geloescht und die Werte verschieben sich!
// Also ersetzen wir Doppeltabs \t\t durch \t@EMPTY@\t

for (i = StartLine; i < StopLine; i++) {

while (indexOf(Lines[i], "\t\t") >= 0) {
    Lines[i] = replace(Lines[i], "\t\t", "\t@EMPTY@\t");
}

// Zeile in ein Array aus Parametern zerlegen; das ist alles, was extrahiert wird, davon benoetigen wir Folgende

// Wir brauchen aus jeder Zeile die folgenden Elemente wenn sie eine Zahl sind
/*  0, Frames
 *  1, Times
 * 10, LocMaxAmplitude
 * 19 Kontraktionszeit 20% User
 * 21 Relaxation User 20% User
 * 26 Kontrationszeit 10%
 * 28 Relaxationszeit 10%
 * 33 Contraktionszeit 50%
 * 35 Relaxationszeit 50%
 * 40 Kontraktionszeit 90%
 * 42 Relaxationszeit 90%
 */
 
 // Diese Parameter beschreiben eine Kontraktion und werden nun vereinzelt und in die entsprechenden Arrays sortiert

Parameter=split(Lines[i], "\t\n\r");

// Haben wir das Ende des aktuellen Datensatzes erreicht, also die erste Zeile der statistischen Auswertung danach, 
// dann brechen wir den Lese-Loop ab!
// Okay, hier lesen wir es in der Reihenfolge ein wie es im Datensatz steht

if(Parameter[0]=="Statistics INCLUDING the first and last event"){break;}

// Nur nach Parametern suchen, wenn das Zeilenarray ueberhaupt lang genug ist

	if(Parameter[10]>0 && Parameter[10]!="@EMPTY@"){MainParameters=Array.concat(MainParameters, Parameter[0]+"\t"+Parameter[1]+"\t"+Parameter[10]+"\t"+"Max");}
	
	if(Parameter[19]>0 && Parameter[19]!="@EMPTY@"){MainParameters=Array.concat(MainParameters, Parameter[0]+"\t"+Parameter[1]+"\t"+Parameter[19]+"\t"+"ContThrUser");}
	if(Parameter[21]>0 && Parameter[21]!="@EMPTY@"){MainParameters=Array.concat(MainParameters, Parameter[0]+"\t"+Parameter[1]+"\t"+Parameter[21]+"\t"+"RelThrUser");}
	
	if(Parameter[26]>0 && Parameter[26]!="@EMPTY@"){MainParameters=Array.concat(MainParameters, Parameter[0]+"\t"+Parameter[1]+"\t"+Parameter[26]+"\t"+"ContThr10%");}
	if(Parameter[28]>0 && Parameter[28]!="@EMPTY@"){MainParameters=Array.concat(MainParameters, Parameter[0]+"\t"+Parameter[1]+"\t"+Parameter[28]+"\t"+"RelThr10%");}
	
	if(Parameter[33]>0 && Parameter[33]!="@EMPTY@"){MainParameters=Array.concat(MainParameters, Parameter[0]+"\t"+Parameter[1]+"\t"+Parameter[33]+"\t"+"ContThr50%");}
	if(Parameter[35]>0 && Parameter[35]!="@EMPTY@"){MainParameters=Array.concat(MainParameters, Parameter[0]+"\t"+Parameter[1]+"\t"+Parameter[35]+"\t"+"RelThr50%");}
	
	if(Parameter[40]>0 && Parameter[40]!="@EMPTY@"){MainParameters=Array.concat(MainParameters, Parameter[0]+"\t"+Parameter[1]+"\t"+Parameter[40]+"\t"+"ContThr90%");}
	if(Parameter.length>42){if(Parameter[42]>0 && Parameter[42]!="@EMPTY@"){MainParameters=Array.concat(MainParameters, Parameter[0]+"\t"+Parameter[1]+"\t"+Parameter[42]+"\t"+"RelThr90%");}}
}

}


// Okay, hier gehen wir die MainParameters durch und flippen ContThr10% mit ContThrUser

// Dazu brauchen wir ein Backup der mMinparameters:

MainParametersBackup=Array.copy(MainParameters);

ZerlegteZeile2=split(MainParameters[i+1], "\t\n\r");

// Zeilen tauschen die Plaetze, wenn die Bedingungen stimmen

	MainParameters[i]=MainParametersBackup[i+1];
	MainParameters[i+1]=MainParametersBackup[i];
	}

}

// Okay, besagter Tausch scheint soweit zu funktionieren


// Und nun beschneiden wir das Array, wenn Datensaetze nicht vollstaendig sind

// Test, ob der erste Datensatz vollstaendig ist Erstes und zweites Maximum identifizieren

// Ist der erste Wert ein Maximum, dann loeschen wir den sofort

// Wir haben nun folgendes Format: Frame /t Zeit /t Wert /t Kontraktionsteil

// Maximum gefolgt von den 8 Werten, welche die Kontraktion beschreiben => Ein kompletter Datensatz

// Nun wollen wir alles loeschen, das VOR dem ersten KOMPLETTEN Datensatz steht!

// Definiere die Reihenfolge der Parameter, die einen vollständigen Datensatz ausmachen


CorrectOrder = newArray("Max", "ContThr10%", "ContThrUser", "ContThr50%", "ContThr90%", "RelThr90%", "RelThr50%", "RelThrUser", "RelThr10%");



// Extrahiere den Datentyp aus MainParameters
DataType = newArray();

for (i = 0; i < MainParameters.length; i++) {
    Einzeldaten = split(MainParameters[i], "\t\n\r");
    if (Einzeldaten.length > 3) {
        DataType = Array.concat(DataType, Einzeldaten[3]);
    }
}



// Problem: Es ist jedoch moeglich, dass der Datensatz durch 9 Teilbar ist und dennoch Fragmente enthaelt;
// Neue Idee um einen vollstaendigen Datensatz zu identifizieren!
// Zuerst loeschen wir alles VOR dem ersten MAX, denn das KANN kein vollstaendiger Datensatz sein!



// Annahme: MainParameters, DataType und CorrectOrder sind bereits definiert.
// CorrectOrder = newArray("Max", "ContThrUser", "ContThr10%", "ContThr50%", "ContThr90%", "RelThr90%", "RelThr50%", "RelThrUser", "RelThr10%");

// Groesse eines kompletten Datensatzes
blockSize = CorrectOrder.length;

// Neue Arrays fuer die gefilterten, vollstaendigen Datensaetze
NewMainParameters = newArray();
NewDataType = newArray();

// Durchlaufe DataType, um komplette Datensaetze zu finden (auch "mittendrin")
i = 0;
while (i <= DataType.length - blockSize) {
    isComplete = true;
    // Ueberpruefe, ob ab Index i ein kompletter Datensatz beginnt:
    for (j = 0; j < blockSize; j++) {
        if (DataType[i+j] != CorrectOrder[j]) {
            isComplete = false;
            break;
        }
    }
    if (isComplete) {
        // Kompletten Block in die neuen Arrays uebernehmen:
        for (j = 0; j < blockSize; j++) {
            NewMainParameters = Array.concat(NewMainParameters, newArray(MainParameters[i+j]));
            NewDataType = Array.concat(NewDataType, newArray(DataType[i+j]));
        }
        // Weiterspringen um Ueberschneidungen zu vermeiden:
        i += blockSize;
    } else {
        // Andernfalls zum naechsten Element gehen:
        i++;
    }
}



// Ueberschreibe die Originalarrays mit den gefilterten, vollstaendigen Datensaetzen
MainParameters = NewMainParameters;
DataType = NewDataType;

// XXX Das hier ist nur zum Testen...ob der Datensatz korrekt beschnitten wurde


if(MainParameters.length%9>0){
	
	print("\\Clear");
	print("Hier passt etwas nicht"); 
	print(MainParameters.length);
	print("Cls= "+cls);
	
	// Checkfinder Testarray drucken
	print("OriginalArray:");
	
	for (test = 0; test < Checkfinder.length; test++) {
	print(Checkfinder[test]);
	}
	
	print("BeschnittenesArray:");
	// Beschnittenes Array drucken
	for (test = 0; test < MainParameters.length; test++) {
	print(MainParameters[test]);
	}

AllData=getInfo("log");
AllData=replace(AllData, ".", ",");

print("\\Clear");

print(AllData);

	exit();
	}


// Und nun den finalen Datensatz ausgeben; das scheint soweit zu passen

//for (i = 0; i < MainParameters.length; i++) {print(MainParameters[i]);}

// Die Arrays von oben erstellen, damit man alle Parameter der Kontraktionen getrennt hat?
// Ja, das ist besser! Also durchgehen und einsortieren!

// Mainparameters mindestens 7*9 = 63 Elemente beinhaltet


// Hier fehlt das ELSE!

if(MainParameters.length>=63){

// ******************* Das hier sind die Datenarrays, jeweils frisch erstellen **************

LocMaxAmplitudes=newArray();

 ContractionThr90=newArray();
 RelaxationThr90=newArray();

//***************************************************************

for (i = 0; i < MainParameters.length; i++) {
dats=split(MainParameters[i], "\t\n\r");

if(dats[3]=="Max"){LocMaxAmplitudes=Array.concat(LocMaxAmplitudes, parseFloat(dats[2])); MaxTimes=Array.concat(MaxTimes, parseFloat(dats[1])); MaxFrames=Array.concat(MaxFrames, parseInt(dats[0]));}

if(dats[3]=="ContThr10%"){ContractionThr10=Array.concat(ContractionThr10, parseFloat(dats[2]));}
if(dats[3]=="ContThrUser"){ContractionThrUser=Array.concat(ContractionThrUser, parseFloat(dats[2]));}
if(dats[3]=="ContThr50%"){ContractionThr50=Array.concat(ContractionThr50, parseFloat(dats[2]));}
if(dats[3]=="ContThr90%"){ContractionThr90=Array.concat(ContractionThr90, parseFloat(dats[2]));}
if(dats[3]=="RelThr90%"){RelaxationThr90=Array.concat(RelaxationThr90, parseFloat(dats[2]));}
if(dats[3]=="RelThr50%"){RelaxationThr50=Array.concat(RelaxationThr50, parseFloat(dats[2]));}
if(dats[3]=="RelThrUser"){RelaxationThrUser=Array.concat(RelaxationThrUser, parseFloat(dats[2]));}
if(dats[3]=="RelThr10%"){RelaxationThr10=Array.concat(RelaxationThr10, parseFloat(dats[2]));}

}


// Hier zur kontrolle User-abnickbar die Laenge aller erstellten Arrays ausgeben!
// Der Datensatz wurde oben bereits beschnitten, die Datensaetze sollten somit vollstaendig sein!!

// Wenn es hier kein problem gibt, werden Elemente dann spaeter geloescht???

testlaenge=MaxTimes.length;


//print("\\Clear");

// Hier werden zur Sicherheit die Arraylaengen ausgegeben



// Das hier gibt genau einmal die Main-Parameters aus (Frame, Zeit, Wert (Zeit oder Amplitude) und Typ)
// Eigentlich brauchen wir das fuer jede Zelle


// Aus diesem Datensatz sollte nun die Amplitudenkurve vernuenftig reproduzierbar sein!


if(cls==0){
for (i = 0; i < MainParameters.length; i++) {
print(MainParameters[i]);
}
}


// Das hier greift, sollten die Parameter-Arrays NICHT allesamt gleich lang sein!

if(MaxTimes.length!=testlaenge || MaxFrames.length!=testlaenge || ContractionThr10.length!=testlaenge || 
RelaxationThr10.length!=testlaenge || ContractionThrUser.length!=testlaenge || RelaxationThrUser.length!=testlaenge ||

for (i = 0; i < MainParameters.length; i++) {
print(MainParameters[i]);
}

exit();

}


// Und nun genau diese Daten in die Uebergeordneten Arrays fuer den ANOVA rein; 
// Einfach jeweils anhaengen und in ein Counter-Array die jeweilige Laenge der Datensaetze fuer die Einzelzellen

ANOVAAmplitude=Array.concat(ANOVAAmplitude,LocMaxAmplitudes);
 ANOVAContThr10=Array.concat(ANOVAContThr10,ContractionThr10);
ANOVAContUser=Array.concat(ANOVAContUser,ContractionThrUser);
 ANOVAContThr50=Array.concat(ANOVAContThr50,ContractionThr50);
ANOVAContThr90=Array.concat(ANOVAContThr90,ContractionThr90);
 ANOVARelThr10=Array.concat(ANOVARelThr10,RelaxationThr10);
ANOVARelUser=Array.concat(ANOVARelUser,RelaxationThrUser);
