        nm = Dialog.getString();
        if (nm == "") nm = "Group_"+(g+1);
        groupNames[g] = nm;
    }

    // 6. Interactive Assignment (Chunked Dialogs)
    choiceList = Array.concat(groupNames, "Exclude");
    assignments = newArray(nFiles);
    for (a = 0; a < nFiles; a++) assignments[a] = groupNames[0]; // Default to first group

    CHUNK = 20; 
    for (start = 0; start < nFiles; start += CHUNK) {
        stop = start + CHUNK; 
        if (stop > nFiles) stop = nFiles;
        
        Dialog.create("Assign Groups (" + (start+1) + "-" + stop + "/" + nFiles + ")");
        for (i = start; i < stop; i++) {
            fullPath = FoundStatFiles[i];
            rootLen  = lengthOf(rootDir);
            // Show only relative path to keep dialog readable
            if (lengthOf(fullPath) > rootLen) {
                displayPath = substring(fullPath, rootLen);
            } else {
                displayPath = fullPath;
            }
            // The "" + ensures everything is treated as a string to avoid numeric errors
            label = "" + (i + 1) + ") " + displayPath;
            Dialog.addChoice(label, choiceList, assignments[i]);
        }
        Dialog.show();
        for (i = start; i < stop; i++) {
            assignments[i] = Dialog.getChoice();
        }
    }

    // 7. Data Ingestion & Flattening
    AllDataRows = newArray();
    ColumnHeadline = "";

    for (i = 0; i < nFiles; i++) {
        group = assignments[i];
        if (group == "Exclude") continue;

        DatenString = File.openAsString(FoundStatFiles[i]);
        DatenSet = split(DatenString, "\r\n");

        // Cell (0,0) as Probe ID
        FirstLineParts = split(DatenSet[0], "\t");
        probeID = FirstLineParts[0];

        // Store Header from the first valid file processed (Row index 1)
        if (ColumnHeadline == "" && DatenSet.length > 1) {
            ColumnHeadline = "Probe_ID\tGroup_Assignment\t" + DatenSet[1];
        }

        // Process actual data rows (starting row index 3)
        for (row = 3; row < DatenSet.length; row++) {
            parts = split(DatenSet[row], "\t");
            // Basic validation: row must contain data
            if (parts.length > 20 && lengthOf(parts[0]) > 2) {
                // Prepend Probe Name and assigned Group
                fullRow = probeID + "\t" + group + "\t" + DatenSet[row];
                AllDataRows = Array.concat(AllDataRows, fullRow);
            }
        }
    }

    // 8. Save Final ANOVA Table
    outDir = getDirectory("Choose Output Folder for ANOVA files");
    if (outDir == "") outDir = rootDir;
    
    // Ab hier werden nun die Daten vorbereitet wir extrahieren nun nur die Mittelwerte der jeweiligen Parameter, Minima, maxima, Stabw bleiben aussen vor

ExtraktionsArray=newArray(0,1,2,3,6,10,14,18,22,26,30,34,38,42,46,50,54,58,62);


// Build ANOVA-ready mean table, but exclude cell rows with invalid numeric values.
// This prevents NaN / Infinity rows from entering ANOVA_Ready_Data LONG and downstream exports.

DatenArrayMittelwerte = newArray();

Clean_ExcludedRows = 0;
Clean_ExcludedRowsText = "Excluded_Row\tReason\tOriginal_Row\n";

for (splt = 0; splt < AllDataRows.length; splt++) {

    DatenArray = split(AllDataRows[splt], "\t\n\r");

    // Keep the existing cleanup logic
    DatenArray = Array.deleteValue(DatenArray, "");
    DatenArray = Array.deleteValue(DatenArray, " ");

    TempString = "";
    Clean_RowOK = 1;
    Clean_BadToken = "";
    Clean_BadColumn = "";

    for (att = 0; att < ExtraktionsArray.length; att++) {

        Clean_Token = "";

        if (DatenArray.length > ExtraktionsArray[att]) {
            Clean_Token = DatenArray[ExtraktionsArray[att]];
        }

        if (att > 0) TempString += "\t";
        TempString += Clean_Token;

        // Columns 0-2 are metadata:
        // 0 Probe_ID
        // 1 Group_Assignment
        // 2 Filename
        //
        // Column 3 and all following columns must be valid numeric values.
        if (att >= 3) {

            Clean_TestVal = parseFloat(Clean_Token);

            if (Clean_Token == "") Clean_RowOK = 0;
            if (Clean_Token == " ") Clean_RowOK = 0;
            if (Clean_Token == "NaN") Clean_RowOK = 0;
            if (Clean_Token == "nan") Clean_RowOK = 0;
            if (Clean_Token == "N/A") Clean_RowOK = 0;
            if (Clean_Token == "NA") Clean_RowOK = 0;
            if (Clean_Token == "Infinity") Clean_RowOK = 0;
            if (Clean_Token == "-Infinity") Clean_RowOK = 0;
            if (Clean_Token == "Inf") Clean_RowOK = 0;
            if (Clean_Token == "-Inf") Clean_RowOK = 0;

            if (isNaN(Clean_TestVal)) {
                Clean_RowOK = 0;
            }

            if (Clean_RowOK == 0 && Clean_BadToken == "") {
                Clean_BadToken = Clean_Token;
                Clean_BadColumn = "" + att;
            }
        }
    }

    if (Clean_RowOK == 1) {

        print(TempString);
        DatenArrayMittelwerte = Array.concat(DatenArrayMittelwerte, TempString);

    } else {

        Clean_ExcludedRows++;
        Clean_ExcludedRowsText += (splt + 1) + "\tColumn_" + Clean_BadColumn + " bad token: " + Clean_BadToken + "\t" + AllDataRows[splt] + "\n";
    }
}
        

FinalDataHeadline="Probe_ID\tGroup_Assignment\tFilenames\tBeats counted [N]\tAmplitudes mean [au]\tBeatTimes mean [s]\tFrequencies mean [1/s]\tPeakTimes10% mean [s]\tSystoles10% mean [s]\tDiastoles10% mean [s]\tPeakTimesUser mean [s]\tSystolesUser mean [s]\tDiastolesUser mean [s]\tPeakTimes50% mean [s]\tSystoles50% mean [s]\tDiastoles50% mean [s]\tPeakTimes90% mean [s]\tSystoles90% mean [s]\tDiastoles90% mean [s]";

FinalDataArray=newArray(DatenArrayMittelwerte.length);
    
    finalText = FinalDataHeadline + "\n";
    for (r = 0; r < DatenArrayMittelwerte.length; r++) {
        finalText += DatenArrayMittelwerte[r] + "\n";
        FinalDataArray[r]=DatenArrayMittelwerte[r];
    }

    

fileNameBase = "ANOVA_Ready_Data_" + year + "-" + MonthNames[month] + "-" + dayOfMonths;

// Save English version (dot)
File.saveString(finalText, outDir + fileNameBase + " LONG (ENG).txt");

// Save German version (comma)
germanText = replace(finalText, ".", ",");
File.saveString(germanText, outDir + fileNameBase + " LONG (GER).txt");

// Save report of excluded invalid rows, if any
if (Clean_ExcludedRows > 0) {
    File.saveString(Clean_ExcludedRowsText, outDir + fileNameBase + " EXCLUDED_INVALID_ROWS (ENG).txt");
    File.saveString(replace(Clean_ExcludedRowsText, ".", ","), outDir + fileNameBase + " EXCLUDED_INVALID_ROWS (GER).txt");
}


    print("\\Clear");
    print("--- ANOVA Preparation Finished ---");
    print("Processed Files: " + FoundStatFiles.length);
    print("Total Data Rows: " + AllDataRows.length);
    print("Output Path: " + outDir);
    
 waitForUser("Success", "ANOVA table created with " + DatenArrayMittelwerte.length + " valid rows.\nExcluded invalid rows: " + Clean_ExcludedRows + "\nFiles saved as (ENG) and (GER).");



// *********************** Normalisierung START ***********************************



// ============================================================
// ADD-ON: WIDE-ONLY NORMALIZATION TO USER-DEFINED CONTROL MEDIAN
// ImageJ Macro SAFE / no Java collections / no nested arrays
//
// Creates WIDE files only:
//
// 1) Ratio-normalized BLOCK-WIDE file
//    ratio = raw_cell_mean / median(control_cell_means in same experiment parent folder)
//
// 2) LOG2-normalized BLOCK-WIDE file
//    log2 = log(ratio) / log(2)
//
// 3) Reference table with all used control medians
// 4) Warning table
//
// IMPORTANT:
// - NO normalized LONG files are written.
// - Beats counted [N] is kept unchanged and is NOT normalized.
// - Only mean parameter columns are normalized.
// - Normalization is performed separately within each biological/experimental parent folder.
// - The user-defined control group is selected from groupNames.
// - The output preserves parent folders so the user can see which animal/experiment each block belongs to.
// - Output layout: Control block on the left, empty separator, treated groups on the right.
// - Existing Function 10 code outside this add-on is not modified.
// ============================================================


// ------------------------------------------------------------
// 0) Select reference/control group
// ------------------------------------------------------------

Dialog.create("Normalization: Reference group");
Dialog.addChoice("Control/reference group:", groupNames, groupNames[0]);
Dialog.show();

Norm_ControlGroup = Dialog.getChoice();


// ------------------------------------------------------------
// 1) Safe output directory and filename date
// ------------------------------------------------------------

Norm_outDir = replace(outDir, "\\", "/");
if (!endsWith(Norm_outDir, "/")) Norm_outDir += "/";

Norm_rootDir = replace(rootDir, "\\", "/");
if (!endsWith(Norm_rootDir, "/")) Norm_rootDir += "/";

// Use the already validated Function-10 filename base.
// This prevents "_NaN" in normalization filenames.
Norm_DateStamp = replace(fileNameBase, "ANOVA_Ready_Data_", "");

// ------------------------------------------------------------
// 2) Headers
// ------------------------------------------------------------

Norm_HeadParts = split(FinalDataHeadline, "\t");
Norm_nCols = Norm_HeadParts.length;

// Expected layout:
// 0 Probe_ID
// 1 Group_Assignment
// 2 Filenames
// 3 Beats counted [N]
// 4... mean parameters
Norm_firstParamCol = 4;
Norm_nParams = Norm_nCols - Norm_firstParamCol;

Norm_RatioHeadline = "";
Norm_Log2Headline  = "";

for (Norm_h = 0; Norm_h < Norm_nCols; Norm_h++) {

    if (Norm_h > 0) {
        Norm_RatioHeadline += "\t";
        Norm_Log2Headline  += "\t";
    }

    if (Norm_h < Norm_firstParamCol) {
        Norm_RatioHeadline += Norm_HeadParts[Norm_h];
        Norm_Log2Headline  += Norm_HeadParts[Norm_h];
    } else {
        Norm_RatioHeadline += Norm_HeadParts[Norm_h] + " ratio_raw_div_ControlMedian";
        Norm_Log2Headline  += Norm_HeadParts[Norm_h] + " log2_raw_div_ControlMedian";
    }
}


// ------------------------------------------------------------
// 3) Re-ingest stat files with path provenance
//
// This is necessary because FinalDataArray no longer contains
// the original file path / experimental parent folder.
//
// Critical parent-folder logic:
//
// root/T1/Control/VidsMovement.../diffMov/.../file.txt
// root/T1/H2O2 01/VidsMovement.../diffMov/.../file.txt
// root/T1/H2O2 02/VidsMovement.../diffMov/.../file.txt
//
// must all become:
//
// parentKey = root/T1/
//
// Therefore:
// 1) remove generated MYOCYTER result folders from the path
//    e.g. VidsMovement..., diffMov, dataplots
// 2) get the biological sample/treatment folder
//    e.g. root/T1/Control/
// 3) use its direct parent as experimental parent
//    e.g. root/T1/
// ------------------------------------------------------------

Norm_RawDataArray = newArray();
Norm_RowParents   = newArray();

Norm_ParentKeys    = newArray();
Norm_ParentDisplay = newArray();

Norm_WarningsText = "Warning_Type\tParent_Folder\tParameter\tDetails\n";

Norm_WarnShortRows = 0;
Norm_WarnBadRaw = 0;
Norm_WarnNoMedianCells = 0;
Norm_WarnLogNonPositive = 0;

for (Norm_i = 0; Norm_i < nFiles; Norm_i++) {

    Norm_group = assignments[Norm_i];
    if (Norm_group == "Exclude") continue;

    Norm_filePath = replace(FoundStatFiles[Norm_i], "\\", "/");

    // --------------------------------------------------------
    // First get the directory containing the stats file
    // --------------------------------------------------------

    Norm_lastSlash = -1;
    for (Norm_c = 0; Norm_c < lengthOf(Norm_filePath); Norm_c++) {
        if (substring(Norm_filePath, Norm_c, Norm_c + 1) == "/") {
            Norm_lastSlash = Norm_c;
        }
    }

    if (Norm_lastSlash >= 0) {
        Norm_fileDir = substring(Norm_filePath, 0, Norm_lastSlash + 1);
    } else {
        Norm_fileDir = Norm_rootDir;
    }

    // --------------------------------------------------------
    // Cut away generated MYOCYTER result folders.
    // Most reliable marker: "/VidsMovement"
    // Fallback markers: "/diffMov", "/dataplots"
    // --------------------------------------------------------

    Norm_cut = indexOf(Norm_filePath, "/VidsMovement");

    if (Norm_cut < 0) Norm_cut = indexOf(Norm_filePath, "/diffMov");
    if (Norm_cut < 0) Norm_cut = indexOf(Norm_filePath, "/dataplots");

    if (Norm_cut >= 0) {
        // root/T1/Control/VidsMovement... -> root/T1/Control/
        Norm_sampleDir = substring(Norm_filePath, 0, Norm_cut + 1);
    } else {
        // Fallback: use the directory of the stats file
        Norm_sampleDir = Norm_fileDir;
    }

    if (!endsWith(Norm_sampleDir, "/")) Norm_sampleDir += "/";

    // --------------------------------------------------------
    // If videos were inside an additional folder named AVI/Videos,
    // step one level up to the treatment/sample folder.
    //
    // root/T1/Control/AVI/VidsMovement... -> root/T1/Control/
    // --------------------------------------------------------

    Norm_sampleNoSlash = Norm_sampleDir;
    if (endsWith(Norm_sampleNoSlash, "/")) {
        Norm_sampleNoSlash = substring(Norm_sampleNoSlash, 0, lengthOf(Norm_sampleNoSlash) - 1);
    }

    Norm_lastSlashSample = -1;
    for (Norm_c3 = 0; Norm_c3 < lengthOf(Norm_sampleNoSlash); Norm_c3++) {
        if (substring(Norm_sampleNoSlash, Norm_c3, Norm_c3 + 1) == "/") {
            Norm_lastSlashSample = Norm_c3;
        }
    }

    Norm_lastFolderName = "";
    if (Norm_lastSlashSample >= 0) {
        Norm_lastFolderName = substring(Norm_sampleNoSlash, Norm_lastSlashSample + 1, lengthOf(Norm_sampleNoSlash));
    }

    Norm_isVideoFolder = 0;
    if (Norm_lastFolderName == "AVI") Norm_isVideoFolder = 1;
    if (Norm_lastFolderName == "avi") Norm_isVideoFolder = 1;
    if (Norm_lastFolderName == "Video") Norm_isVideoFolder = 1;
    if (Norm_lastFolderName == "video") Norm_isVideoFolder = 1;
    if (Norm_lastFolderName == "Videos") Norm_isVideoFolder = 1;
    if (Norm_lastFolderName == "videos") Norm_isVideoFolder = 1;

    if (Norm_isVideoFolder == 1) {
        if (Norm_lastSlashSample >= 0) {
            Norm_sampleDir = substring(Norm_sampleNoSlash, 0, Norm_lastSlashSample + 1);
        }
    }

    // --------------------------------------------------------
    // Now get the direct parent of the biological sample/treatment folder.
    // root/T1/Control/ -> root/T1/
    // --------------------------------------------------------

    Norm_sampleNoSlash = Norm_sampleDir;
    if (endsWith(Norm_sampleNoSlash, "/")) {
        Norm_sampleNoSlash = substring(Norm_sampleNoSlash, 0, lengthOf(Norm_sampleNoSlash) - 1);
    }

    Norm_lastSlashParent = -1;
    for (Norm_c4 = 0; Norm_c4 < lengthOf(Norm_sampleNoSlash); Norm_c4++) {
        if (substring(Norm_sampleNoSlash, Norm_c4, Norm_c4 + 1) == "/") {
            Norm_lastSlashParent = Norm_c4;
        }
    }

    if (Norm_sampleDir == Norm_rootDir) {
        Norm_parentKey = Norm_rootDir;
    } else {
        if (Norm_lastSlashParent >= 0) {
            Norm_parentKey = substring(Norm_sampleNoSlash, 0, Norm_lastSlashParent + 1);
        } else {
            Norm_parentKey = Norm_rootDir;
        }
    }

    // Safety catch: do not go above selected root directory
    if (indexOf(Norm_sampleDir, Norm_rootDir) == 0 && indexOf(Norm_parentKey, Norm_rootDir) != 0) {
        Norm_parentKey = Norm_rootDir;
    }

    if (!endsWith(Norm_parentKey, "/")) Norm_parentKey += "/";

    // Short display path relative to root
    if (indexOf(Norm_parentKey, Norm_rootDir) == 0) {
        Norm_parentDisp = substring(Norm_parentKey, lengthOf(Norm_rootDir), lengthOf(Norm_parentKey));
        if (Norm_parentDisp == "") Norm_parentDisp = "[root]";
    } else {
        Norm_parentDisp = Norm_parentKey;
    }

    // Add parent folder to unique list if not present
    Norm_parentExists = 0;
    for (Norm_pp = 0; Norm_pp < Norm_ParentKeys.length; Norm_pp++) {
        if (Norm_ParentKeys[Norm_pp] == Norm_parentKey) {
            Norm_parentExists = 1;
        }
    }

    if (Norm_parentExists == 0) {
        Norm_ParentKeys    = Array.concat(Norm_ParentKeys, Norm_parentKey);
        Norm_ParentDisplay = Array.concat(Norm_ParentDisplay, Norm_parentDisp);
    }

    // --------------------------------------------------------
    // Read and parse file
    // --------------------------------------------------------

    Norm_DatenString = File.openAsString(Norm_filePath);
    Norm_DatenString = replace(Norm_DatenString, "\r\n", "\n");
    Norm_DatenString = replace(Norm_DatenString, "\r", "\n");
    Norm_DatenSet = split(Norm_DatenString, "\n");

    if (Norm_DatenSet.length < 4) {
        Norm_WarningsText += "FILE_TOO_SHORT\t" + Norm_parentDisp + "\tALL\t" + Norm_filePath + "\n";
        continue;
    }

    Norm_FirstLineParts = split(Norm_DatenSet[0], "\t");
    Norm_probeID = Norm_FirstLineParts[0];

    // Process actual data rows
    for (Norm_row = 3; Norm_row < Norm_DatenSet.length; Norm_row++) {

        Norm_parts = split(Norm_DatenSet[Norm_row], "\t");

        if (Norm_parts.length > 20 && lengthOf(Norm_parts[0]) > 2) {

            Norm_fullRow = Norm_probeID + "\t" + Norm_group + "\t" + Norm_DatenSet[Norm_row];

            Norm_DatenArray = split(Norm_fullRow, "\t\n\r");
            Norm_DatenArray = Array.deleteValue(Norm_DatenArray, "");
            Norm_DatenArray = Array.deleteValue(Norm_DatenArray, " ");

            // Highest extraction index is 62
            if (Norm_DatenArray.length > 62) {

                // ----------------------------------------------------
// Build extracted row AND validate it before inclusion.
//
// Rule:
// If ANY numeric value required for normalization is NaN,
// empty, Infinity, -Infinity, or not parseable as number,
// the WHOLE cell row is excluded from normalization.
//
// Columns in extracted row:
// 0 Probe_ID              text
// 1 Group_Assignment     text
// 2 Filenames            text
// 3 Beats counted [N]    numeric but NOT normalized
// 4... mean parameters   numeric and normalized
// ----------------------------------------------------

Norm_TempString = "";
Norm_RowIsValid = 1;
Norm_BadToken = "";
Norm_BadColumn = "";

for (Norm_att = 0; Norm_att < ExtraktionsArray.length; Norm_att++) {

    Norm_token = "";

    if (Norm_DatenArray.length > ExtraktionsArray[Norm_att]) {
        Norm_token = Norm_DatenArray[ExtraktionsArray[Norm_att]];
    }

    if (Norm_att > 0) Norm_TempString += "\t";
    Norm_TempString += Norm_token;

    // Validate all numeric columns from Beats counted [N] onward.
    // Metadata columns 0-2 are allowed to be text.
    if (Norm_att >= 3) {

        Norm_testToken = Norm_token;

        if (Norm_testToken == "") Norm_RowIsValid = 0;
        if (Norm_testToken == " ") Norm_RowIsValid = 0;
        if (Norm_testToken == "NaN") Norm_RowIsValid = 0;
        if (Norm_testToken == "nan") Norm_RowIsValid = 0;
        if (Norm_testToken == "N/A") Norm_RowIsValid = 0;
        if (Norm_testToken == "NA") Norm_RowIsValid = 0;
        if (Norm_testToken == "Infinity") Norm_RowIsValid = 0;
        if (Norm_testToken == "-Infinity") Norm_RowIsValid = 0;
        if (Norm_testToken == "Inf") Norm_RowIsValid = 0;
        if (Norm_testToken == "-Inf") Norm_RowIsValid = 0;

        Norm_testVal = parseFloat(Norm_testToken);

        if (isNaN(Norm_testVal)) {
            Norm_RowIsValid = 0;
        }

        if (Norm_RowIsValid == 0 && Norm_BadToken == "") {
            Norm_BadToken = Norm_testToken;
            Norm_BadColumn = "" + Norm_att;
        }
    }
}

if (Norm_RowIsValid == 1) {

    Norm_RawDataArray = Array.concat(Norm_RawDataArray, Norm_TempString);
    Norm_RowParents   = Array.concat(Norm_RowParents, Norm_parentKey);

} else {

    Norm_WarnBadRaw++;
    Norm_WarningsText += "ROW_EXCLUDED_BAD_NUMERIC_VALUE\t" + Norm_parentDisp + "\tColumn_" + Norm_BadColumn + "\tBad token: " + Norm_BadToken + " | Row: " + Norm_DatenSet[Norm_row] + "\n";
}

            } else {
                Norm_WarnShortRows++;
                Norm_WarningsText += "ROW_TOO_SHORT\t" + Norm_parentDisp + "\tALL\t" + Norm_DatenSet[Norm_row] + "\n";
            }
        }
    }
}


// ------------------------------------------------------------
// 4) Calculate control medians per parent folder and parameter
// ------------------------------------------------------------

Norm_nRows    = Norm_RawDataArray.length;
Norm_nParents = Norm_ParentKeys.length;

Norm_Medians   = newArray(Norm_nParents * Norm_nParams);
Norm_MedianOK  = newArray(Norm_nParents * Norm_nParams);
Norm_ControlNs = newArray(Norm_nParents * Norm_nParams);

Norm_ReferenceText = "Parent_Folder\tControl_Group\tParameter\tN_Control_Cells\tControl_Median\tStatus\n";

if (Norm_nRows == 0) {

    Norm_WarningsText += "NO_ROWS\tALL\tALL\tNo rows available for normalization.\n";
    print("NORMALIZATION skipped: no rows available.");

} else {

    for (Norm_pp = 0; Norm_pp < Norm_nParents; Norm_pp++) {

        Norm_parentKey2  = Norm_ParentKeys[Norm_pp];
        Norm_parentDisp2 = Norm_ParentDisplay[Norm_pp];

        for (Norm_param = 0; Norm_param < Norm_nParams; Norm_param++) {

            Norm_col = Norm_firstParamCol + Norm_param;
            Norm_vals = newArray();

            for (Norm_r = 0; Norm_r < Norm_nRows; Norm_r++) {

                if (Norm_RowParents[Norm_r] == Norm_parentKey2) {

                    Norm_cells = split(Norm_RawDataArray[Norm_r], "\t");

                    if (Norm_cells.length > Norm_col) {

                        Norm_grp = Norm_cells[1];

                        if (Norm_grp == Norm_ControlGroup) {

                            Norm_val = parseFloat(Norm_cells[Norm_col]);

                            if (!isNaN(Norm_val)) {
                                Norm_vals = Array.concat(Norm_vals, Norm_val);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            Norm_flatIdx = Norm_pp * Norm_nParams + Norm_param;
            Norm_ControlNs[Norm_flatIdx] = Norm_vals.length;

            if (Norm_vals.length > 0) {

                Array.sort(Norm_vals);

                Norm_N = Norm_vals.length;
                Norm_mid = floor(Norm_N / 2);

                // even number of values
                if (2 * Norm_mid == Norm_N) {
                    Norm_median = (Norm_vals[Norm_mid - 1] + Norm_vals[Norm_mid]) / 2;
                }

                // odd number of values
                if (2 * Norm_mid != Norm_N) {
                    Norm_median = Norm_vals[Norm_mid];
                }

                Norm_Medians[Norm_flatIdx] = Norm_median;

                if (Norm_median > 0) {
                    Norm_MedianOK[Norm_flatIdx] = 1;
                    Norm_status = "OK";
                    Norm_medianText = "" + Norm_median;
                } else {
                    Norm_MedianOK[Norm_flatIdx] = 0;
                    Norm_status = "INVALID_MEDIAN_LE_ZERO";
                    Norm_medianText = "" + Norm_median;
                    Norm_WarningsText += "INVALID_CONTROL_MEDIAN\t" + Norm_parentDisp2 + "\t" + Norm_HeadParts[Norm_col] + "\tMedian <= 0\n";
                }

            } else {

                Norm_MedianOK[Norm_flatIdx] = 0;
                Norm_status = "NO_VALID_CONTROL_VALUES";
                Norm_medianText = "";

                Norm_WarningsText += "NO_CONTROL_MEDIAN\t" + Norm_parentDisp2 + "\t" + Norm_HeadParts[Norm_col] + "\tNo valid numeric values in selected control group\n";
            }

            Norm_ReferenceText += Norm_parentDisp2 + "\t" + Norm_ControlGroup + "\t" + Norm_HeadParts[Norm_col] + "\t" + Norm_ControlNs[Norm_flatIdx] + "\t" + Norm_medianText + "\t" + Norm_status + "\n";
        }
    }


    // --------------------------------------------------------
    // 5) Generate ratio-normalized and log2-normalized arrays in memory
    //    These arrays are NOT saved as LONG files.
    //    They are only used to create BLOCK-WIDE outputs.
    // --------------------------------------------------------

    Norm_RatioDataArray = newArray(Norm_nRows);
    Norm_Log2DataArray  = newArray(Norm_nRows);

    Norm_LogBase2 = log(2);

    for (Norm_r = 0; Norm_r < Norm_nRows; Norm_r++) {

        Norm_cells = split(Norm_RawDataArray[Norm_r], "\t");
        Norm_parentKeyRow = Norm_RowParents[Norm_r];

        // Find parent index
        Norm_pIdx = -1;
        for (Norm_pp = 0; Norm_pp < Norm_nParents; Norm_pp++) {
            if (Norm_ParentKeys[Norm_pp] == Norm_parentKeyRow) {
                Norm_pIdx = Norm_pp;
            }
        }

        // Copy metadata columns unchanged
        Norm_RatioRow = "";
        Norm_Log2Row  = "";

        for (Norm_meta = 0; Norm_meta < Norm_firstParamCol; Norm_meta++) {

            Norm_metaVal = "";
            if (Norm_cells.length > Norm_meta) {
                Norm_metaVal = Norm_cells[Norm_meta];
            }

            if (Norm_meta > 0) {
                Norm_RatioRow += "\t";
                Norm_Log2Row  += "\t";
            }

            Norm_RatioRow += Norm_metaVal;
            Norm_Log2Row  += Norm_metaVal;
        }

        // Normalize mean parameter columns only
        for (Norm_param = 0; Norm_param < Norm_nParams; Norm_param++) {

            Norm_col = Norm_firstParamCol + Norm_param;

            Norm_ratioText = "";
            Norm_log2Text  = "";

            if (Norm_cells.length > Norm_col) {

                Norm_rawVal = parseFloat(Norm_cells[Norm_col]);

                if (!isNaN(Norm_rawVal)) {

                    if (Norm_pIdx >= 0) {

                        Norm_flatIdx = Norm_pIdx * Norm_nParams + Norm_param;

                        if (Norm_MedianOK[Norm_flatIdx] == 1) {

                            Norm_med = Norm_Medians[Norm_flatIdx];

                            Norm_ratio = Norm_rawVal / Norm_med;
                            Norm_ratioText = d2s(Norm_ratio, 8);

                            if (Norm_ratio > 0) {
                                Norm_log2 = log(Norm_ratio) / Norm_LogBase2;
                                Norm_log2Text = d2s(Norm_log2, 8);
                            } else {
                                Norm_log2Text = "";
                                Norm_WarnLogNonPositive++;
                            }

                        } else {
                            Norm_ratioText = "";
                            Norm_log2Text = "";
                            Norm_WarnNoMedianCells++;
                        }

                    } else {
                        Norm_ratioText = "";
                        Norm_log2Text = "";
                        Norm_WarnNoMedianCells++;
                    }

                } else {
                    Norm_ratioText = "";
                    Norm_log2Text = "";
                    Norm_WarnBadRaw++;
                }

            } else {
                Norm_ratioText = "";
                Norm_log2Text = "";
                Norm_WarnBadRaw++;
            }

            Norm_RatioRow += "\t" + Norm_ratioText;
            Norm_Log2Row  += "\t" + Norm_log2Text;
        }

        Norm_RatioDataArray[Norm_r] = Norm_RatioRow;
        Norm_Log2DataArray[Norm_r]  = Norm_Log2Row;
    }


    // --------------------------------------------------------
    // 6) Save reference table
    // --------------------------------------------------------

    Norm_ReferenceFileBase = "Normalization_REFERENCES_ControlMedian_" + Norm_DateStamp;

    File.saveString(Norm_ReferenceText, Norm_outDir + Norm_ReferenceFileBase + " (ENG).txt");
    File.saveString(replace(Norm_ReferenceText, ".", ","), Norm_outDir + Norm_ReferenceFileBase + " (GER).txt");


    // --------------------------------------------------------
    // 7) Create BLOCK-WIDE outputs for ratio and log2 data
    //
    // Layout:
    // Experiment_Parent_Folder | Row_in_Parent |
    // Control metadata + all normalized Control parameters |
    // EMPTY separator column |
    // Treated group 1 metadata + all normalized parameters |
    // EMPTY separator column |
    // Treated group 2 metadata + all normalized parameters | ...
    //
    // This preserves the experimental/tier parent folders.
    // It also keeps Probe_ID, so folders such as Control, H2O2 01,
    // H2O2 02 remain visible in the WIDE table.
    // --------------------------------------------------------

    for (Norm_Mode = 0; Norm_Mode < 2; Norm_Mode++) {

        if (Norm_Mode == 0) {
            Norm_CurrentRows = Norm_RatioDataArray;
            Norm_CurrentHeadline = Norm_RatioHeadline;
            Norm_OutputFileBase = "Normalized_RATIO_raw_div_ControlMedian_BLOCKWIDE_ControlLeft_TreatedRight_" + Norm_DateStamp;
        }

        if (Norm_Mode == 1) {
            Norm_CurrentRows = Norm_Log2DataArray;
            Norm_CurrentHeadline = Norm_Log2Headline;
            Norm_OutputFileBase = "Normalized_LOG2_raw_div_ControlMedian_BLOCKWIDE_ControlLeft_TreatedRight_" + Norm_DateStamp;
        }

        Norm_WideHeadParts = split(Norm_CurrentHeadline, "\t");
        Norm_Wide_nCols = Norm_WideHeadParts.length;

        // --------------------------------------------------------
        // 7.1 Build header
        // --------------------------------------------------------

        Norm_WideText = "";
        Norm_WideText += "Experiment_Parent_Folder\tRow_in_Parent";

        // Control block: metadata
        Norm_WideText += "\t" + Norm_ControlGroup + "__Probe_ID";
        Norm_WideText += "\t" + Norm_ControlGroup + "__Filename";

        // Control block: values, starting with Beats counted [N]
        for (Norm_col = 3; Norm_col < Norm_Wide_nCols; Norm_col++) {

            Norm_WideColName = Norm_WideHeadParts[Norm_col];
            Norm_WideColName = replace(Norm_WideColName, "\r", " ");
            Norm_WideColName = replace(Norm_WideColName, "\n", " ");
            Norm_WideColName = replace(Norm_WideColName, "\t", " ");

            Norm_WideText += "\t" + Norm_WideColName + "__" + Norm_ControlGroup;
        }

        // Empty separator column between Control and treated cells
        Norm_WideText += "\t";

        // Treated/non-control group blocks
        for (Norm_g = 0; Norm_g < nGroups; Norm_g++) {

            if (groupNames[Norm_g] != Norm_ControlGroup) {

                Norm_WideText += "\t" + groupNames[Norm_g] + "__Probe_ID";
                Norm_WideText += "\t" + groupNames[Norm_g] + "__Filename";

                for (Norm_col = 3; Norm_col < Norm_Wide_nCols; Norm_col++) {

                    Norm_WideColName = Norm_WideHeadParts[Norm_col];
                    Norm_WideColName = replace(Norm_WideColName, "\r", " ");
                    Norm_WideColName = replace(Norm_WideColName, "\n", " ");
                    Norm_WideColName = replace(Norm_WideColName, "\t", " ");

                    Norm_WideText += "\t" + Norm_WideColName + "__" + groupNames[Norm_g];
                }

                // Empty separator column between treated groups
                Norm_WideText += "\t";
            }
        }

        Norm_WideText += "\n";


        // --------------------------------------------------------
        // 7.2 Write data parent-folder by parent-folder
        // --------------------------------------------------------

        for (Norm_pp = 0; Norm_pp < Norm_nParents; Norm_pp++) {

            Norm_parentKeyNow  = Norm_ParentKeys[Norm_pp];
            Norm_parentDispNow = Norm_ParentDisplay[Norm_pp];

            // Count Control rows for this parent
            Norm_controlCount = 0;

            for (Norm_i2 = 0; Norm_i2 < Norm_CurrentRows.length; Norm_i2++) {

                if (Norm_RowParents[Norm_i2] == Norm_parentKeyNow) {

                    Norm_tmpCells = split(Norm_CurrentRows[Norm_i2], "\t");

                    if (Norm_tmpCells.length > 1) {
                        if (Norm_tmpCells[1] == Norm_ControlGroup) {
                            Norm_controlCount++;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            // Count maximum rows among treated groups for this parent
            Norm_parentMaxN = Norm_controlCount;

            for (Norm_g = 0; Norm_g < nGroups; Norm_g++) {

                if (groupNames[Norm_g] != Norm_ControlGroup) {

                    Norm_groupCount = 0;

                    for (Norm_i2 = 0; Norm_i2 < Norm_CurrentRows.length; Norm_i2++) {

                        if (Norm_RowParents[Norm_i2] == Norm_parentKeyNow) {

                            Norm_tmpCells = split(Norm_CurrentRows[Norm_i2], "\t");

                            if (Norm_tmpCells.length > 1) {
                                if (Norm_tmpCells[1] == groupNames[Norm_g]) {
                                    Norm_groupCount++;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    if (Norm_groupCount > Norm_parentMaxN) {
                        Norm_parentMaxN = Norm_groupCount;
                    }
                }
            }

            // If a parent has no rows, skip
            if (Norm_parentMaxN == 0) {
                Norm_WarningsText += "PARENT_SKIPPED_NO_ROWS\t" + Norm_parentDispNow + "\tALL\tNo rows in this parent folder\n";
                continue;
            }

            // ----------------------------------------------------
            // Write rows for this parent
            // ----------------------------------------------------

            for (Norm_rep = 0; Norm_rep < Norm_parentMaxN; Norm_rep++) {

                Norm_WideLine = "";
                Norm_WideLine += Norm_parentDispNow + "\t" + (Norm_rep + 1);

                // ------------------------------------------------
                // Control block: find rep-th Control row in this parent
                // ------------------------------------------------

                Norm_foundRow = "";
                Norm_foundCount = 0;

                for (Norm_i2 = 0; Norm_i2 < Norm_CurrentRows.length; Norm_i2++) {

                    if (Norm_RowParents[Norm_i2] == Norm_parentKeyNow) {

                        Norm_tmpCells = split(Norm_CurrentRows[Norm_i2], "\t");

                        if (Norm_tmpCells.length > 1) {

                            if (Norm_tmpCells[1] == Norm_ControlGroup) {

                                if (Norm_foundCount == Norm_rep && Norm_foundRow == "") {
                                    Norm_foundRow = Norm_CurrentRows[Norm_i2];
                                }

                                Norm_foundCount++;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (Norm_foundRow != "") {

                    Norm_srcCells = split(Norm_foundRow, "\t");

                    // Probe_ID and Filename
                    if (Norm_srcCells.length > 0) Norm_WideLine += "\t" + Norm_srcCells[0];
                    else Norm_WideLine += "\t";

                    if (Norm_srcCells.length > 2) Norm_WideLine += "\t" + Norm_srcCells[2];
                    else Norm_WideLine += "\t";

                    // Values: Beats counted [N] plus normalized parameters
                    for (Norm_col = 3; Norm_col < Norm_Wide_nCols; Norm_col++) {

                        Norm_valText = "";

                        if (Norm_srcCells.length > Norm_col) {
                            Norm_valText = Norm_srcCells[Norm_col];
                        }

                        if (Norm_valText == "NaN") Norm_valText = "";
                        if (Norm_valText == "Infinity") Norm_valText = "";
                        if (Norm_valText == "-Infinity") Norm_valText = "";

                        Norm_WideLine += "\t" + Norm_valText;
                    }

                } else {

                    // Empty Control block
                    Norm_WideLine += "\t\t"; // Probe_ID + Filename

                    for (Norm_col = 3; Norm_col < Norm_Wide_nCols; Norm_col++) {
                        Norm_WideLine += "\t";
                    }
                }

                // Empty separator column
                Norm_WideLine += "\t";


                // ------------------------------------------------
                // Treated/non-control group blocks
                // ------------------------------------------------

                for (Norm_g = 0; Norm_g < nGroups; Norm_g++) {

                    if (groupNames[Norm_g] != Norm_ControlGroup) {

                        Norm_foundRow = "";
                        Norm_foundCount = 0;

                        for (Norm_i2 = 0; Norm_i2 < Norm_CurrentRows.length; Norm_i2++) {

                            if (Norm_RowParents[Norm_i2] == Norm_parentKeyNow) {

                                Norm_tmpCells = split(Norm_CurrentRows[Norm_i2], "\t");

                                if (Norm_tmpCells.length > 1) {

                                    if (Norm_tmpCells[1] == groupNames[Norm_g]) {

                                        if (Norm_foundCount == Norm_rep && Norm_foundRow == "") {
                                            Norm_foundRow = Norm_CurrentRows[Norm_i2];
                                        }

                                        Norm_foundCount++;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        if (Norm_foundRow != "") {

                            Norm_srcCells = split(Norm_foundRow, "\t");

                            // Probe_ID and Filename
                            if (Norm_srcCells.length > 0) Norm_WideLine += "\t" + Norm_srcCells[0];
                            else Norm_WideLine += "\t";

                            if (Norm_srcCells.length > 2) Norm_WideLine += "\t" + Norm_srcCells[2];
                            else Norm_WideLine += "\t";

                            // Values: Beats counted [N] plus normalized parameters
                            for (Norm_col = 3; Norm_col < Norm_Wide_nCols; Norm_col++) {

                                Norm_valText = "";

                                if (Norm_srcCells.length > Norm_col) {
                                    Norm_valText = Norm_srcCells[Norm_col];
                                }

                                if (Norm_valText == "NaN") Norm_valText = "";
                                if (Norm_valText == "Infinity") Norm_valText = "";
                                if (Norm_valText == "-Infinity") Norm_valText = "";

                                Norm_WideLine += "\t" + Norm_valText;
                            }

                        } else {

                            // Empty treated group block
                            Norm_WideLine += "\t\t"; // Probe_ID + Filename

                            for (Norm_col = 3; Norm_col < Norm_Wide_nCols; Norm_col++) {
                                Norm_WideLine += "\t";
                            }
                        }

                        // Empty separator column between treated groups
                        Norm_WideLine += "\t";
                    }
                }

                Norm_WideText += Norm_WideLine + "\n";
            }

            // Empty line after each parent folder block for readability
            Norm_WideText += "\n";
        }


        // --------------------------------------------------------
        // 7.3 Save BLOCK-WIDE output
        // --------------------------------------------------------

        File.saveString(Norm_WideText, Norm_outDir + Norm_OutputFileBase + " (ENG).txt");
        File.saveString(replace(Norm_WideText, ".", ","), Norm_outDir + Norm_OutputFileBase + " (GER).txt");
    }


    // --------------------------------------------------------
    // 8) Save warnings and print summary
    // --------------------------------------------------------

    Norm_WarningsText += "SUMMARY\tALL\tRows_processed\t" + Norm_nRows + "\n";
    Norm_WarningsText += "SUMMARY\tALL\tParent_folders_detected\t" + Norm_nParents + "\n";
    Norm_WarningsText += "SUMMARY\tALL\tShort_or_malformed_rows\t" + Norm_WarnShortRows + "\n";
    Norm_WarningsText += "SUMMARY\tALL\tBad_or_missing_raw_values\t" + Norm_WarnBadRaw + "\n";
    Norm_WarningsText += "SUMMARY\tALL\tCells_without_valid_control_median\t" + Norm_WarnNoMedianCells + "\n";
    Norm_WarningsText += "SUMMARY\tALL\tLog2_values_not_defined_ratio_le_zero\t" + Norm_WarnLogNonPositive + "\n";
    Norm_WarningsText += "SUMMARY\tALL\tSelected_control_group\t" + Norm_ControlGroup + "\n";

    Norm_WarningsFileBase = "Normalization_WARNINGS_ControlMedian_" + Norm_DateStamp;

    File.saveString(Norm_WarningsText, Norm_outDir + Norm_WarningsFileBase + " (ENG).txt");
    File.saveString(replace(Norm_WarningsText, ".", ","), Norm_outDir + Norm_WarningsFileBase + " (GER).txt");

    print("--- BLOCK-WIDE normalization to control median finished ---");
    print("Reference group: " + Norm_ControlGroup);
    print("Rows normalized: " + Norm_nRows);
    print("Parent folders detected: " + Norm_nParents);
    print("Output path: " + Norm_outDir);
}



// *********************** Normalisierung ENDE ***********************************





// Und nun einmal alles als WIDE exportieren

// ============================================================
// ADD-ON (ImageJ Macro SAFE): SINGLE WIDE FILE (ALL parameters × ALL groups)
// - NO arrays-of-arrays (ImageJ limitation)
// - Flat storage: GroupRowsFlat[startIndex[g] + r] = rowString
// - Output columns: <ParamName>__<GroupName>
// - Pads unequal N with blanks
// Uses: FinalDataHeadline, FinalDataArray, groupNames, nGroups, outDir, fileNameBase
// ============================================================

// local safe output dir (do not touch your existing outDir variable)
outDir2 = replace(outDir, "\\", "/");
if (!endsWith(outDir2, "/")) outDir2 += "/";

// headline split
Wide_HeadParts = split(FinalDataHeadline, "\t");
Wide_nCols = lengthOf(Wide_HeadParts);

// choose first parameter column (0 Probe_ID, 1 Group_Assignment, 2 Filenames, 3 Beats counted...)
Wide_firstValueCol = 3; // set to 4 if you want to skip "Beats counted [N]"

// ------------------------------------------------------------
// 1) Count rows per group
Wide_GroupCounts = newArray(nGroups);
for (g = 0; g < nGroups; g++) Wide_GroupCounts[g] = 0;

for (i = 0; i < lengthOf(FinalDataArray); i++) {
    Wide_rowStr = FinalDataArray[i];
    Wide_cells  = split(Wide_rowStr, "\t");
    Wide_grp    = Wide_cells[1]; // Group_Assignment

    Wide_gIdx = -1;
    for (gg = 0; gg < nGroups; gg++) {
        if (groupNames[gg] == Wide_grp) { Wide_gIdx = gg; break; }
    }
    if (Wide_gIdx >= 0) Wide_GroupCounts[Wide_gIdx]++;
}

// ------------------------------------------------------------
// 2) Build start indices into ONE flat array & compute maxN / totalN
Wide_StartIndex = newArray(nGroups);
Wide_FillPos    = newArray(nGroups);

Wide_totalN = 0;
Wide_maxN   = 0;

for (g = 0; g < nGroups; g++) {
    Wide_StartIndex[g] = Wide_totalN;     // start offset for group g
    Wide_FillPos[g]    = 0;               // will be used while filling
    Wide_totalN        = Wide_totalN + Wide_GroupCounts[g];
    if (Wide_GroupCounts[g] > Wide_maxN) Wide_maxN = Wide_GroupCounts[g];
}

if (Wide_totalN == 0) {
    print("WIDE export skipped: no rows found in FinalDataArray.");
} else {

    // Flat storage for row strings (size = sum of group counts)
    Wide_GroupRowsFlat = newArray(Wide_totalN);
    for (k = 0; k < Wide_totalN; k++) Wide_GroupRowsFlat[k] = ""; // avoid NaN

    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    // 3) Fill flat storage: GroupRowsFlat[startIndex[g] + r] = rowString
    for (i = 0; i < lengthOf(FinalDataArray); i++) {
        Wide_rowStr = FinalDataArray[i];
        Wide_cells  = split(Wide_rowStr, "\t");
        Wide_grp    = Wide_cells[1];

        Wide_gIdx = -1;
        for (gg = 0; gg < nGroups; gg++) {
            if (groupNames[gg] == Wide_grp) { Wide_gIdx = gg; break; }
        }
        if (Wide_gIdx < 0) continue;

        pos = Wide_StartIndex[Wide_gIdx] + Wide_FillPos[Wide_gIdx];
        Wide_GroupRowsFlat[pos] = Wide_rowStr;
        Wide_FillPos[Wide_gIdx]++;
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    // 4) Build ONE big WIDE table: columns = (parameters × groups)
    Wide_All = "";

    // Header line: <ParamName>__<GroupName>
    for (col = Wide_firstValueCol; col < Wide_nCols; col++) {

        Wide_param = Wide_HeadParts[col];
        // keep readable, but remove line breaks/tabs
        Wide_param = replace(Wide_param, "\r", " ");
        Wide_param = replace(Wide_param, "\n", " ");
        Wide_param = replace(Wide_param, "\t", " ");

        for (g = 0; g < nGroups; g++) {
            Wide_All += Wide_param + "__" + groupNames[g];
            if (!(col == Wide_nCols-1 && g == nGroups-1)) Wide_All += "\t";
        }
    }
    Wide_All += "\n";

    // Data rows: r = replicate index within each group (0..maxN-1)
    for (rrep = 0; rrep < Wide_maxN; rrep++) {

        Wide_line = "";

        for (col = Wide_firstValueCol; col < Wide_nCols; col++) {
            for (g = 0; g < nGroups; g++) {

                Wide_v = "";

                if (rrep < Wide_GroupCounts[g]) {
                    idxFlat = Wide_StartIndex[g] + rrep;
                    Wide_rowStr = Wide_GroupRowsFlat[idxFlat];

                    Wide_cells = split(Wide_rowStr, "\t");
                    if (col < lengthOf(Wide_cells)) Wide_v = Wide_cells[col];

                    // clean tokens that break stats import
                    if (Wide_v == "NaN" || Wide_v == "Infinity" || Wide_v == "-Infinity") Wide_v = "";
                }

                Wide_line += Wide_v;
                if (!(col == Wide_nCols-1 && g == nGroups-1)) Wide_line += "\t";
            }
        }

        Wide_All += Wide_line + "\n";
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    // 5) Save ONE file (ENG + GER)
    File.saveString(Wide_All, outDir2 + fileNameBase + "_WIDE_ALLPARAMS (ENG).txt");
    File.saveString(replace(Wide_All, ".", ","), outDir2 + fileNameBase + "_WIDE_ALLPARAMS (GER).txt");

    print("--- SINGLE WIDE export finished ---");
    print("Groups: " + nGroups + " | Max N (padded): " + Wide_maxN);
    print("Saved: " + outDir2 + fileNameBase + "_WIDE_ALLPARAMS (ENG/GER).txt");
}


// Und nun die statistische Untersuchung (ANOVA)


// ============================================================
// STATISTICS ADD-ON (ImageJ Macro SAFE, no arrays-of-arrays)
// Append THIS block under your existing code.
// Input: LONG file produced by your macro: ANOVA_Ready_Data_... (ENG/GER).txt
// Output: STATS_ttest__... and/or STATS_anova__... (ENG + GER)
// Pairwise in output file: ONLY significant pairs (raw or adjusted)
// ============================================================

// ---- Run now? ----
Dialog.create("Next Step: Statistics");
Dialog.addCheckbox("Run statistics now (t-test / ANOVA)?", true);
Dialog.show();
if (!Dialog.getCheckbox()) exit("Finished without statistics.");

// ---- Choose LONG file (ENG or GER) ----
ST_path = File.openDialog("Choose LONG file: ANOVA_Ready_Data_... LONG (ENG).txt");
if (ST_path=="") exit("Aborted.");

// ---- Start ----
ST_runStatsWizard(ST_path);


// ============================================================
// MAIN
// ============================================================


    // ============================================================
    // NACH DER STATISTIK: Heatmaps + DifferenceMaps
    // ============================================================

// ============================================================
// FINAL: Heatmaps + DifferenceMaps + sichere Datenspeicherung
// - Heatmaps bleiben wie sie sind (OHNE "Max" in den Heatmaps)
// - TXT-Reports: enthalten ALLE HeatMap-Daten + zusätzlich DifferenceMap-Daten
// - RowLabels rechts sichtbar
// - Calibration Bar rechts/unten, NICHT über der Heatmap, +70px tiefer
// - TXT-Reports werden direkt mit File.saveString() geschrieben (nicht über Log) -> nie leer
// ============================================================


run("Colors...", "foreground=black background=black selection=yellow");
run("Set Measurements...", "area mean standard modal min centroid center perimeter bounding fit shape feret's integrated median skewness kurtosis area_fraction stack limit display redirect=None decimal=9");
run("Input/Output...", "jpeg=90 gif=-1 file=.txt use_file copy_column copy_row save_column save_row");

getDateAndTime(year, month, dayOfWeek, dayOfMonth, hour, minute, second, msec);
MonthNames = newArray("Jan","Feb","Mar","Apr","May","Jun","Jul","Aug","Sep","Oct","Nov","Dec"); 

if (hour<10) {hours = "0"+hour;} else {hours=hour;}
if (minute<10) {minutes = "0"+minute;} else {minutes=minute;}
if (month<10) {months = "0"+(month+1);} else {months=month+1;}
if (dayOfMonth<10) {dayOfMonths = "0"+dayOfMonth;} else {dayOfMonths=dayOfMonth;}

// 2. Reuse already selected Root Folder
if (rootDir == "") exit("Aborted.");
rootDir = replace(rootDir, "\\", "/");
if (!endsWith(rootDir, "/")) rootDir += "/";

// 3. Stack und Ergebnis-Array initialisieren
stack = newArray(rootDir);
FinalList = newArray();


// 4. Iterativer Loop: alle Unterordner sammeln
idx = 0;
while (idx < stack.length) {
    current = stack[idx];
    if (!endsWith(current, "/")) current += "/";
    items = getFileList(current);
    for (i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
        name = items[i];
        if (endsWith(name, "/")) {
            folder = replace(current + name, "\\", "/");
            FinalList = Array.concat(FinalList, folder);
            stack     = Array.concat(stack, folder);
        }
    }
    idx++;
}

// 5. Stats-Files finden
FoundStatFiles = newArray();
for (i = 0; i < FinalList.length; i++) {
    Candidates = getFileList(FinalList[i]);
    for (j = 0; j < Candidates.length; j++) {
        if (startsWith(Candidates[j], "Results Final Summary for Stats ") && endsWith(Candidates[j], " (ENG).txt")) {
            FileToOpen = FinalList[i] + Candidates[j];
            FoundStatFiles = Array.concat(FoundStatFiles, FileToOpen);
        }
    }
}

if (FoundStatFiles.length == 0) exit("Keine 'Results Final Summary for Stats ... (ENG).txt' Files gefunden.");

Array.sort(FoundStatFiles);

// Labels / Namen
RowLabels = newArray(FoundStatFiles.length);
ResultsFileNames = newArray(FoundStatFiles.length);

// Dauerhafte Arrays (Means/StdDevs pro File)
ContrThr10ArrayMean=newArray(); ContrThr10ArrayStdDev=newArray();
ContrThrUserArrayMean=newArray(); ContrThrUserArrayStdDev=newArray();
ContrThr50ArrayMean=newArray(); ContrThr50ArrayStdDev=newArray();
ContrThr90ArrayMean=newArray(); ContrThr90ArrayStdDev=newArray();
MaximumArrayMean=newArray(); MaximumArrayStdDev=newArray();      // NUR TEXTREPORT (keine Heatmap)
RelaxThr90ArrayMean=newArray(); RelaxThr90ArrayStdDev=newArray();
RelaxThr50ArrayMean=newArray(); RelaxThr50ArrayStdDev=newArray();
RelaxThrUserArrayMean=newArray(); RelaxThrUserArrayStdDev=newArray();
RelaxThr10ArrayMean=newArray(); RelaxThr10ArrayStdDev=newArray();
OverallArrayMean=newArray(); OverallArrayStdDev=newArray();

// globale Arrays (alle Werte aller Kontraktionen)
ContrThr10ArrayAllValues=newArray(); 
ContrThrUserArrayAllValues=newArray(); 
ContrThr50ArrayAllValues=newArray(); 
ContrThr90ArrayAllValues=newArray(); 
MaximumArrayAllValues=newArray();         // NUR TEXTREPORT (keine Heatmap)
RelaxThr90ArrayAllValues=newArray(); 
RelaxThr50ArrayAllValues=newArray(); 
RelaxThrUserArrayAllValues=newArray(); 
RelaxThr10ArrayAllValues=newArray();
OverallArrayAllValues=newArray();

HeatMin = 1e30;
HeatMax = -1e30;
DiffMax = 0;

// Heatmap-Spalten (OHNE Max!)
Type = newArray("C10\n[s]","CUser","C50","C90","R90","R50","RUser","R10","Ovr");

// ============================================================
// 6. Alle Files einlesen + Stats berechnen
// ============================================================
for (opn = 0; opn < FoundStatFiles.length; opn++) {

    // Arrays pro File
    ContrThr10Array=newArray(); ContrThrUserArray=newArray(); ContrThr50Array=newArray();
    ContrThr90Array=newArray(); MaximumArray=newArray(); RelaxThr90Array=newArray();    
    RelaxThr50Array=newArray(); RelaxThrUserArray=newArray(); RelaxThr10Array=newArray();
    OverallArray=newArray();

    DatenString = File.openAsString(FoundStatFiles[opn]);
    ResultsFileNames[opn] = FoundStatFiles[opn];

    // Label direkt als Rückgabewert (kein globaler Tmp-String mehr)
    RowLabels[opn] = makeRowLabel(FoundStatFiles[opn]);

    DatenSet = split(DatenString, "\r\n");

    for (i = 0; i < DatenSet.length; i++) {
        ZeilenParameter = split(DatenSet[i], "\t");
        if (ZeilenParameter.length >= 20 && ZeilenParameter[0] != "Frame") {

            ContrThr10Array=Array.concat(ContrThr10Array, ZeilenParameter[3]);
            ContrThrUserArray=Array.concat(ContrThrUserArray, ZeilenParameter[4]);
            ContrThr50Array=Array.concat(ContrThr50Array, ZeilenParameter[5]);
            ContrThr90Array=Array.concat(ContrThr90Array, ZeilenParameter[6]);
            MaximumArray=Array.concat(MaximumArray, ZeilenParameter[7]); // NUR Textreport
            RelaxThr90Array=Array.concat(RelaxThr90Array, ZeilenParameter[8]);
            RelaxThr50Array=Array.concat(RelaxThr50Array, ZeilenParameter[9]);
            RelaxThrUserArray=Array.concat(RelaxThrUserArray, ZeilenParameter[10]);
            RelaxThr10Array=Array.concat(RelaxThr10Array, ZeilenParameter[11]);

            ovr = parseFloat(ZeilenParameter[3]) + parseFloat(ZeilenParameter[4]) + parseFloat(ZeilenParameter[5]) + parseFloat(ZeilenParameter[6])
                + parseFloat(ZeilenParameter[8]) + parseFloat(ZeilenParameter[9]) + parseFloat(ZeilenParameter[10]) + parseFloat(ZeilenParameter[11]);
            OverallArray = Array.concat(OverallArray, ovr);
        }
    }

    // globale Arrays erweitern
    ContrThr10ArrayAllValues=Array.concat(ContrThr10ArrayAllValues, ContrThr10Array);
    ContrThrUserArrayAllValues=Array.concat(ContrThrUserArrayAllValues, ContrThrUserArray);
    ContrThr50ArrayAllValues=Array.concat(ContrThr50ArrayAllValues, ContrThr50Array);
    ContrThr90ArrayAllValues=Array.concat(ContrThr90ArrayAllValues, ContrThr90Array);
    MaximumArrayAllValues=Array.concat(MaximumArrayAllValues, MaximumArray); // NUR Textreport
    RelaxThr90ArrayAllValues=Array.concat(RelaxThr90ArrayAllValues, RelaxThr90Array);
    RelaxThr50ArrayAllValues=Array.concat(RelaxThr50ArrayAllValues, RelaxThr50Array);
    RelaxThrUserArrayAllValues=Array.concat(RelaxThrUserArrayAllValues, RelaxThrUserArray);
    RelaxThr10ArrayAllValues=Array.concat(RelaxThr10ArrayAllValues, RelaxThr10Array);
    OverallArrayAllValues=Array.concat(OverallArrayAllValues, OverallArray);

    // Stats pro File
    Array.getStatistics(ContrThr10Array, min, max, mean, stdDev);
    ContrThr10ArrayMean=Array.concat(ContrThr10ArrayMean, mean);
    ContrThr10ArrayStdDev=Array.concat(ContrThr10ArrayStdDev, stdDev);

    Array.getStatistics(ContrThrUserArray, min, max, mean, stdDev);
    ContrThrUserArrayMean=Array.concat(ContrThrUserArrayMean, mean);
    ContrThrUserArrayStdDev=Array.concat(ContrThrUserArrayStdDev, stdDev);

    Array.getStatistics(ContrThr50Array, min, max, mean, stdDev);
    ContrThr50ArrayMean=Array.concat(ContrThr50ArrayMean, mean);
    ContrThr50ArrayStdDev=Array.concat(ContrThr50ArrayStdDev, stdDev);

    Array.getStatistics(ContrThr90Array, min, max, mean, stdDev);
    ContrThr90ArrayMean=Array.concat(ContrThr90ArrayMean, mean);
    ContrThr90ArrayStdDev=Array.concat(ContrThr90ArrayStdDev, stdDev);

    Array.getStatistics(RelaxThr90Array, min, max, mean, stdDev);
    RelaxThr90ArrayMean=Array.concat(RelaxThr90ArrayMean, mean);
    RelaxThr90ArrayStdDev=Array.concat(RelaxThr90ArrayStdDev, stdDev);

    Array.getStatistics(RelaxThr50Array, min, max, mean, stdDev);
    RelaxThr50ArrayMean=Array.concat(RelaxThr50ArrayMean, mean);
    RelaxThr50ArrayStdDev=Array.concat(RelaxThr50ArrayStdDev, stdDev);

    Array.getStatistics(RelaxThrUserArray, min, max, mean, stdDev);
    RelaxThrUserArrayMean=Array.concat(RelaxThrUserArrayMean, mean);
    RelaxThrUserArrayStdDev=Array.concat(RelaxThrUserArrayStdDev, stdDev);

    Array.getStatistics(RelaxThr10Array, min, max, mean, stdDev);
    RelaxThr10ArrayMean=Array.concat(RelaxThr10ArrayMean, mean);
    RelaxThr10ArrayStdDev=Array.concat(RelaxThr10ArrayStdDev, stdDev);

    Array.getStatistics(OverallArray, min, max, mean, stdDev);
    OverallArrayMean=Array.concat(OverallArrayMean, mean);
    OverallArrayStdDev=Array.concat(OverallArrayStdDev, stdDev);

    Array.getStatistics(MaximumArray, min, max, mean, stdDev); // NUR Textreport
    MaximumArrayMean=Array.concat(MaximumArrayMean, mean);
    MaximumArrayStdDev=Array.concat(MaximumArrayStdDev, stdDev);
}

// robust HeatMin/HeatMax über alle Heatmap-Spalten (OHNE Max!)
HeatVals = Array.concat(ContrThr10ArrayMean, ContrThrUserArrayMean);
HeatVals = Array.concat(HeatVals, ContrThr50ArrayMean);
HeatVals = Array.concat(HeatVals, ContrThr90ArrayMean);
HeatVals = Array.concat(HeatVals, RelaxThr90ArrayMean);
HeatVals = Array.concat(HeatVals, RelaxThr50ArrayMean);
HeatVals = Array.concat(HeatVals, RelaxThrUserArrayMean);
HeatVals = Array.concat(HeatVals, RelaxThr10ArrayMean);
HeatVals = Array.concat(HeatVals, OverallArrayMean);
Array.getStatistics(HeatVals, HeatMin, HeatMax, tmpMean, tmpStd);
if (HeatMax <= HeatMin) exit("HeatMax<=HeatMin -> Heatmap Range kaputt!");

// globale Means/StdDevs (Max NUR fürs Textfile)
Array.getStatistics(ContrThr10ArrayAllValues, min, max, ContrThr10mean, ContrThr10stdDev);
Array.getStatistics(ContrThrUserArrayAllValues, min, max, ContrThrUsermean, ContrThrUserstdDev);
Array.getStatistics(ContrThr50ArrayAllValues, min, max, ContrThr50mean, ContrThr50stdDev);
Array.getStatistics(ContrThr90ArrayAllValues, min, max, ContrThr90mean, ContrThr90stdDev);
Array.getStatistics(MaximumArrayAllValues, min, max, Maximummean, MaximumstdDev); // NUR Textfile
Array.getStatistics(RelaxThr90ArrayAllValues, min, max, RelaxThr90mean, RelaxThr90stdDev);
Array.getStatistics(RelaxThr50ArrayAllValues, min, max, RelaxThr50mean, RelaxThr50stdDev);
Array.getStatistics(RelaxThrUserArrayAllValues, min, max, RelaxThrUsermean, RelaxThrUserstdDev);
Array.getStatistics(RelaxThr10ArrayAllValues, min, max, RelaxThr10mean, RelaxThr10stdDev);
Array.getStatistics(OverallArrayAllValues, min, max, Overallmean, OverallstdDev);

// ============================================================
// 7. Report-Strings bauen (statt Log) -> sichere Speicherung
//    + enthält HeatMap-AllSamples Daten (inkl. Max NUR hier)
//    + enthält zusätzlich DifferenceMap-Daten
// ============================================================
ReportENG = "";
ReportENG += "HEATMAP: All Samples (Means/StdDevs)\n";
ReportENG += "Filename\tType\tC10 [s]\tCUser [s]\tC50 [s]\tC90 [s]\tMax [au]\tR90 [s]\tR50 [s]\tRUser [s]\tR10 [s]\tOvr [s]\n";

for (prn = 0; prn < ResultsFileNames.length; prn++) {
    ReportENG += ResultsFileNames[prn] + "\tMean\t"
        + ContrThr10ArrayMean[prn] + "\t" + ContrThrUserArrayMean[prn] + "\t" + ContrThr50ArrayMean[prn] + "\t" + ContrThr90ArrayMean[prn] + "\t"
        + MaximumArrayMean[prn] + "\t"
        + RelaxThr90ArrayMean[prn] + "\t" + RelaxThr50ArrayMean[prn] + "\t" + RelaxThrUserArrayMean[prn] + "\t" + RelaxThr10ArrayMean[prn] + "\t"
        + OverallArrayMean[prn] + "\n";

    ReportENG += "\tStdDev\t"
        + ContrThr10ArrayStdDev[prn] + "\t" + ContrThrUserArrayStdDev[prn] + "\t" + ContrThr50ArrayStdDev[prn] + "\t" + ContrThr90ArrayStdDev[prn] + "\t"
        + MaximumArrayStdDev[prn] + "\t"
        + RelaxThr90ArrayStdDev[prn] + "\t" + RelaxThr50ArrayStdDev[prn] + "\t" + RelaxThrUserArrayStdDev[prn] + "\t" + RelaxThr10ArrayStdDev[prn] + "\t"
        + OverallArrayStdDev[prn] + "\n\n";
}

ReportENG += "\nGlobal-Mean\t\t" + ContrThr10mean + "\t" + ContrThrUsermean + "\t" + ContrThr50mean + "\t" + ContrThr90mean + "\t" + Maximummean + "\t"
          + RelaxThr90mean + "\t" + RelaxThr50mean + "\t" + RelaxThrUsermean + "\t" + RelaxThr10mean + "\t" + Overallmean + "\n";

ReportENG += "Global-StdDev\t\t" + ContrThr10stdDev + "\t" + ContrThrUserstdDev + "\t" + ContrThr50stdDev + "\t" + ContrThr90stdDev + "\t" + MaximumstdDev + "\t"
          + RelaxThr90stdDev + "\t" + RelaxThr50stdDev + "\t" + RelaxThrUserstdDev + "\t" + RelaxThr10stdDev + "\t" + OverallstdDev + "\n";

// --------- NEU: DifferenceMap-Daten in denselben Report (OHNE Max) ---------
ReportENG += "\n\nDIFFERENCEMAP: ABS Diff to GlobalMean (inkl. Max)\n";
ReportENG += "Filename\tC10_absdiff\tCUser_absdiff\tC50_absdiff\tC90_absdiff\tMax_absdiff\tR90_absdiff\tR50_absdiff\tRUser_absdiff\tR10_absdiff\tOvr_absdiff\n";

for (prn = 0; prn < ResultsFileNames.length; prn++) {

    dC10   = abs(ContrThr10ArrayMean[prn]   - ContrThr10mean);
    dCUser = abs(ContrThrUserArrayMean[prn] - ContrThrUsermean);
    dC50   = abs(ContrThr50ArrayMean[prn]   - ContrThr50mean);
    dC90   = abs(ContrThr90ArrayMean[prn]   - ContrThr90mean);
    dMax  = abs(MaximumArrayMean[prn] - Maximummean);
    dR90   = abs(RelaxThr90ArrayMean[prn]   - RelaxThr90mean);
    dR50   = abs(RelaxThr50ArrayMean[prn]   - RelaxThr50mean);
    dRUser = abs(RelaxThrUserArrayMean[prn] - RelaxThrUsermean);
    dR10   = abs(RelaxThr10ArrayMean[prn]   - RelaxThr10mean);

    dOvr   = abs(OverallArrayMean[prn]      - Overallmean);

    ReportENG += ResultsFileNames[prn] + "\t"
              + dC10 + "\t" + dCUser + "\t" + dC50 + "\t" + dC90 + "\t"
              + dMax + "\t"
              + dR90 + "\t" + dR50 + "\t" + dRUser + "\t" + dR10 + "\t"
              + dOvr + "\n";
}

Report2ENG="";

// --------- NEU: DifferenceMap-Daten in denselben Report (OHNE Max) ---------
Report2ENG += "\n\nDIFFERENCEMAP: Diff to GlobalMean (inkl. Max)\n";
Report2ENG += "Filename\tC10_diff\tCUser_diff\tC50_diff\tC90_diff\tMax_diff\tR90_diff\tR50_diff\tRUser_diff\tR10_diff\tOvr_diff\n";

for (prn = 0; prn < ResultsFileNames.length; prn++) {

    d2C10   = (ContrThr10ArrayMean[prn]   - ContrThr10mean);
    d2CUser = (ContrThrUserArrayMean[prn] - ContrThrUsermean);
    d2C50   = (ContrThr50ArrayMean[prn]   - ContrThr50mean);
    d2C90   = (ContrThr90ArrayMean[prn]   - ContrThr90mean);
    d2Max  = (MaximumArrayMean[prn] - Maximummean);
    d2R90   = (RelaxThr90ArrayMean[prn]   - RelaxThr90mean);
    d2R50   = (RelaxThr50ArrayMean[prn]   - RelaxThr50mean);
    d2RUser = (RelaxThrUserArrayMean[prn] - RelaxThrUsermean);
    d2R10   = (RelaxThr10ArrayMean[prn]   - RelaxThr10mean);

    d2Ovr   = (OverallArrayMean[prn]      - Overallmean);

    Report2ENG += ResultsFileNames[prn] + "\t"
              + d2C10 + "\t" + d2CUser + "\t" + d2C50 + "\t" + d2C90 + "\t"
              + d2Max + "\t"
              + d2R90 + "\t" + d2R50 + "\t" + d2RUser + "\t" + d2R10 + "\t"
              + d2Ovr + "\n";
}


// ============================================================
// 8. HEATMAP (OHNE Max!)
// ============================================================
newImage("HeatMap", "32-bit black", 9, FoundStatFiles.length, 1);
selectWindow("HeatMap");

for (yy = 0; yy < FoundStatFiles.length; yy++) {
    setPixel(0, yy, parseFloat(ContrThr10ArrayMean[yy]));
    setPixel(1, yy, parseFloat(ContrThrUserArrayMean[yy]));
    setPixel(2, yy, parseFloat(ContrThr50ArrayMean[yy]));
    setPixel(3, yy, parseFloat(ContrThr90ArrayMean[yy]));
    setPixel(4, yy, parseFloat(RelaxThr90ArrayMean[yy]));
    setPixel(5, yy, parseFloat(RelaxThr50ArrayMean[yy]));
    setPixel(6, yy, parseFloat(RelaxThrUserArrayMean[yy]));
    setPixel(7, yy, parseFloat(RelaxThr10ArrayMean[yy]));
    setPixel(8, yy, parseFloat(OverallArrayMean[yy]));
}

setMinAndMax(HeatMin, HeatMax);
run("Fire");

// EINMAL skalieren -> HeatMap-1
HeatScaleH = FoundStatFiles.length * 50;
run("Scale...", "x=50 y=50 width=450 height="+HeatScaleH+" interpolation=None create");

// ab hier nur HeatMap-1
selectWindow("HeatMap-1");
setMinAndMax(HeatMin, HeatMax);
run("Fire");

// Breite/Höhe der eigentlichen Heatmap (ohne Margins)
getDimensions(HeatMapW0, HeatMapH0, channels, slices, frames); // HeatMapW0=450

// RightMargin: Platz für Labels + Platz für Bar rechts daneben
MaxLabelLen = 0;
for (i = 0; i < RowLabels.length; i++) if (lengthOf(RowLabels[i]) > MaxLabelLen) MaxLabelLen = lengthOf(RowLabels[i]);

BarW = 140; BarH = 120;
LabelW = MaxLabelLen * 7;
RightMargin = 30 + LabelW + 30 + BarW + 40;  // Label + Abstand + Bar + Luft
if (RightMargin < 600) RightMargin = 600;

TopMargin = 60;
BottomMargin = 240; // genug Platz für Bar, +70px tiefer

// Canvas erweitern
run("Canvas Size...", "width="+(HeatMapW0+RightMargin)+" height="+HeatMapH0+" position=Center-Left");
run("Canvas Size...", "width="+(HeatMapW0+RightMargin)+" height="+(HeatMapH0+TopMargin)+" position=Bottom-Left");
run("Canvas Size...", "width="+(HeatMapW0+RightMargin)+" height="+(HeatMapH0+TopMargin+BottomMargin)+" position=Top-Left");

// Calibration Bar: unten, aber rechts neben Labels (nicht über Heatmap)
BarX = HeatMapW0 + 20 + LabelW + 30;        // rechts von Labels
BarY = TopMargin + HeatScaleH + 70;         // +70px tiefer als "direkt unter Heatmap"
makeRectangle(BarX, BarY, BarW, BarH);

setMinAndMax(HeatMin, HeatMax);
run("Calibration Bar...", "location=[At Selection] fill=Black label=White number=6 decimal=2 font=12");

// nach Calibration Bar ist das neue Fenster "... with bar" aktiv
HeatFinalTitle = getTitle();
selectWindow(HeatFinalTitle);

// ab hier RGB für Text/Lines
run("RGB Color");

// Header
setFont("Arial black", 12);
setColor(255,255,255);
HeaderY = 40;
for (i = 0; i < Type.length; i++) drawString(Type[i], 10 + i*50, HeaderY);

// Trennlinie zwischen Kontraktion (4 Spalten) und Relaxation: 4*50=200
setLineWidth(3);
drawLine(200, TopMargin, 200, TopMargin + HeatScaleH);

// RowLabels rechts (X basiert auf HeatMapW0!)
LabelX = HeatMapW0 + 10;
setFont("Arial", 12);
setColor(255,255,0);
LabelY0 = TopMargin + 35;
for (i = 0; i < RowLabels.length; i++) {
    lab = RowLabels[i];
    if (lab == "" || lab == " ") lab = ResultsFileNames[i];
    drawString(lab, LabelX, LabelY0 + 50*i);
}

// speichern: immer FINAL-Fenster
saveAs("jpg", rootDir + "HeatMap all Samples_" + year+"-"+MonthNames[month]+"-"+dayOfMonths+"-"+hours+"h"+minutes + ".jpg");

// ============================================================
// 9. DIFFERENCE MAP (OHNE Max!)
// ============================================================
newImage("DifferenceMap", "32-bit black", 9, ResultsFileNames.length, 1);
selectWindow("DifferenceMap");

DiffMax = 0;
for (yy = 0; yy < ResultsFileNames.length; yy++) {

    d = abs(ContrThr10ArrayMean[yy]-ContrThr10mean); setPixel(0, yy, d); if (d>DiffMax) DiffMax=d;
    d = abs(ContrThrUserArrayMean[yy]-ContrThrUsermean); setPixel(1, yy, d); if (d>DiffMax) DiffMax=d;
    d = abs(ContrThr50ArrayMean[yy]-ContrThr50mean); setPixel(2, yy, d); if (d>DiffMax) DiffMax=d;
    d = abs(ContrThr90ArrayMean[yy]-ContrThr90mean); setPixel(3, yy, d); if (d>DiffMax) DiffMax=d;

    d = abs(RelaxThr90ArrayMean[yy]-RelaxThr90mean); setPixel(4, yy, d); if (d>DiffMax) DiffMax=d;
    d = abs(RelaxThr50ArrayMean[yy]-RelaxThr50mean); setPixel(5, yy, d); if (d>DiffMax) DiffMax=d;
    d = abs(RelaxThrUserArrayMean[yy]-RelaxThrUsermean); setPixel(6, yy, d); if (d>DiffMax) DiffMax=d;
    d = abs(RelaxThr10ArrayMean[yy]-RelaxThr10mean); setPixel(7, yy, d); if (d>DiffMax) DiffMax=d;

    d = abs(OverallArrayMean[yy]-Overallmean); setPixel(8, yy, d); if (d>DiffMax) DiffMax=d;
}

setMinAndMax(0, DiffMax);
run("Fire");

// skalieren -> DifferenceMap-1
DiffScaleH = ResultsFileNames.length * 50;
run("Scale...", "x=50 y=50 width=450 height="+DiffScaleH+" interpolation=None create");

// ab hier nur DifferenceMap-1
selectWindow("DifferenceMap-1");
setMinAndMax(0, DiffMax);
run("Fire");

getDimensions(DiffMapW0, DiffMapH0, channels, slices, frames); // 450

TopMargin2 = 60;
BottomMargin2 = 240;

// Canvas
run("Canvas Size...", "width="+(DiffMapW0+RightMargin)+" height="+DiffMapH0+" position=Center-Left");
run("Canvas Size...", "width="+(DiffMapW0+RightMargin)+" height="+(DiffMapH0+TopMargin2)+" position=Bottom-Left");
run("Canvas Size...", "width="+(DiffMapW0+RightMargin)+" height="+(DiffMapH0+TopMargin2+BottomMargin2)+" position=Top-Left");

// Bar: unten + rechts neben Labels, +70px tiefer
BarX = DiffMapW0 + 20 + LabelW + 30;
BarY = TopMargin2 + DiffScaleH + 70;
makeRectangle(BarX, BarY, BarW, BarH);

setMinAndMax(0, DiffMax);
run("Calibration Bar...", "location=[At Selection] fill=Black label=White number=6 decimal=2 font=12");

DiffFinalTitle = getTitle();
selectWindow(DiffFinalTitle);
run("RGB Color");

// Header
setFont("Arial black", 12);
setColor(255,255,255);
HeaderY = 40;
for (i = 0; i < Type.length; i++) drawString(Type[i], 10 + i*50, HeaderY);

// Trennlinie
setLineWidth(3);
drawLine(200, TopMargin2, 200, TopMargin2 + DiffScaleH);

// RowLabels rechts
LabelX = DiffMapW0 + 10;
setFont("Arial", 12);
setColor(255,255,0);
LabelY0 = TopMargin2 + 35;
for (i = 0; i < RowLabels.length; i++) {
    lab = RowLabels[i];
    if (lab == "" || lab == " ") lab = ResultsFileNames[i];
    drawString(lab, LabelX, LabelY0 + 50*i);
}

saveAs("jpg", rootDir + "Differences to OverallMean_" + year+"-"+MonthNames[month]+"-"+dayOfMonths+"-"+hours+"h"+minutes + ".jpg");

// ============================================================
// 10. TXT speichern (sicher, ohne Log)
// ============================================================

ReportENG=ReportENG+"\n"+Report2ENG;

File.saveString(ReportENG, rootDir+ "Final Overall Analysis "+ year+"-"+MonthNames[month]+"-"+dayOfMonths+"-"+hours+"h"+minutes + " (ENG).txt");

ReportGER = replace(ReportENG, ".", ",");

File.saveString(ReportGER, rootDir+ "Final Overall Analysis "+ year+"-"+MonthNames[month]+"-"+dayOfMonths+"-"+hours+"h"+minutes + " (GER).txt");

// Cleanup
close("*");



// ============================================================
