// ============================================================
// Helper für Heatmaps
// ============================================================
function makeRowLabel(fullPath) {

    // normalisieren
    p = replace(fullPath, "\\", "/");

    // alles ab "/VidsMovement" abschneiden (inkl. VidsMovement selbst)
    idx = indexOf(p, "/VidsMovement");
    if (idx >= 0) {
        label = substring(p, 0, idx);
    } else {
        // Fallback: Parent-Folder der Datei
        pos = lastIndexOf(p, "/");
        if (pos > 0) label = substring(p, 0, pos);
        else label = p;
    }

    // Trailing "/" entfernen
    while (endsWith(label, "/")) {
        label = substring(label, 0, lengthOf(label)-1);
    }

    return label;
}


// ============================================================
// Statistikfunktionen
// ============================================================
function ST_runStatsWizard(path) {

    txt = File.openAsString(path);
    if (txt=="") exit("File empty.");

    // normalize line endings
    txt = replace(txt, "\r", "");
    lines = split(txt, "\n");
    if (lengthOf(lines) < 2) exit("Not enough data lines.");

    header = lines[0];
    cols = split(header, "\t");
    if (lengthOf(cols) < 6) exit("Header too short. Please select the LONG file produced by the macro.");

    // find required columns
    probeCol = ST_findCol(cols, "Probe_ID");
    groupCol = ST_findCol(cols, "Group_Assignment");
    if (probeCol < 0 || groupCol < 0) {
        exit("Could not find columns 'Probe_ID' and 'Group_Assignment'. Select the LONG file produced by the macro.");
    }

    // --- Settings dialog ---
    Dialog.create("Statistics: Settings");
Dialog.addChoice("Unit of analysis:",
    newArray(
        "Aggregate by Probe_ID (mean per probe)",
        "Rows (each cell = replicate)"
    ),
    "Rows (each cell = replicate)"  // oder setz hier deinen Default
);
Dialog.addCheckbox("Include 'Beats counted [N]' as parameter", true);
Dialog.addNumber("Alpha (significance threshold):", 0.05);
Dialog.addDirectory("Save results to folder (optional; empty = no files):", "");
Dialog.show();

    unitChoice   = Dialog.getChoice();
    includeBeats = Dialog.getCheckbox();
    alpha        = Dialog.getNumber();
    outDir       = Dialog.getString();

    if (outDir!="") {
        outDir = replace(outDir, "\\", "/");
        if (!endsWith(outDir, "/")) outDir = outDir + "/";
    }

    // Determine first parameter column in LONG file:
    // 0 Probe_ID | 1 Group_Assignment | 2 Filenames | 3 Beats counted [N] | 4.. parameters
    firstValueCol = 3;
    if (!includeBeats) firstValueCol = 4;

    if (lengthOf(cols) <= firstValueCol) exit("No parameter columns found (firstValueCol=" + firstValueCol + ").");

    // Build param name list (dynamic)
    P = lengthOf(cols) - firstValueCol;
    paramNames = newArray(P);
    for (p=0; p<P; p++) paramNames[p] = cols[firstValueCol + p];

    // ------------- Read data: row-level OR aggregated -------------
    groups = newArray(0);
    data   = newArray(0); // each row: tab-joined P numbers as strings ("NaN" allowed)

    if (startsWith(unitChoice, "Rows")) {

        for (i=1; i<lengthOf(lines); i++) {
            line = lines[i];
            if (line=="") continue;

            parts = split(line, "\t");
            if (lengthOf(parts) <= groupCol) continue;

            g = parts[groupCol];
            if (g=="") continue;

            // build P values row string (allow missing -> NaN)
            rowStr = "";
            for (p=0; p<P; p++) {
                colIdx = firstValueCol + p;
                raw = "";
                if (colIdx < lengthOf(parts)) raw = parts[colIdx];

                vStr = ST_toNumberStringOrNaN(raw); // "NaN" or "1.23"
                rowStr = rowStr + vStr;
                if (p < P-1) rowStr = rowStr + "\t";
            }

            groups = Array.concat(groups, g);
            data   = Array.concat(data, rowStr);
        }

    } else {
        // -------- Aggregate by Probe_ID: mean per probe within each group --------
        // key = group + "||" + probeID
        keys      = newArray(0);
        keyGroups = newArray(0);
        sumsFlat  = newArray(0); // keys.length * P
        cntsFlat  = newArray(0); // keys.length * P

        for (i=1; i<lengthOf(lines); i++) {
            line = lines[i];
            if (line=="") continue;

            parts = split(line, "\t");
            if (lengthOf(parts) <= groupCol || lengthOf(parts) <= probeCol) continue;

            g  = parts[groupCol];
            pr = parts[probeCol];
            if (g=="" || pr=="") continue;

            key = g + "||" + pr;

            // find key index (linear search)
            kIdx = -1;
            for (kk=0; kk<lengthOf(keys); kk++) {
                if (keys[kk] == key) { kIdx = kk; break; }
            }

            // create new key slot if needed
            if (kIdx < 0) {
                keys      = Array.concat(keys, key);
                keyGroups = Array.concat(keyGroups, g);

                // IMPORTANT: sums/cnts must start at 0 (NOT NaN)
                tmpS = ST_zeroArray(P);
                tmpC = ST_zeroArray(P);
                sumsFlat = Array.concat(sumsFlat, tmpS);
                cntsFlat = Array.concat(cntsFlat, tmpC);

                kIdx = lengthOf(keys) - 1;
            }

            // accumulate per parameter
            base = kIdx * P;
            for (p=0; p<P; p++) {
                colIdx = firstValueCol + p;
                raw = "";
                if (colIdx < lengthOf(parts)) raw = parts[colIdx];

                v = ST_parseFloatSafe(raw);
                if (v==v) {
                    sumsFlat[base + p] = sumsFlat[base + p] + v;
                    cntsFlat[base + p] = cntsFlat[base + p] + 1;
                }
            }
        }

        // convert to aggregated rows (means)
        for (kIdx=0; kIdx<lengthOf(keys); kIdx++) {
            base = kIdx * P;
            rowStr = "";

            for (p=0; p<P; p++) {
                if (cntsFlat[base+p] > 0) m = sumsFlat[base+p] / cntsFlat[base+p];
                else m = 0/0;

                rowStr = rowStr + ST_numOrNaNString(m);
                if (p < P-1) rowStr = rowStr + "\t";
            }

            groups = Array.concat(groups, keyGroups[kIdx]);
            data   = Array.concat(data, rowStr);
        }
    }

    if (lengthOf(groups) < 2) exit("Not enough usable data rows after parsing/aggregation.");

    // Unique groups in order of appearance
    uniq = ST_uniqueStrings(groups);
    k = lengthOf(uniq);
    if (k < 2) exit("Need at least 2 groups.");

    // N per group (units after chosen unit-of-analysis)
    groupNs = newArray(k);
    for (gi=0; gi<k; gi++) groupNs[gi] = ST_countString(groups, uniq[gi]);

    // ---------- Parameter selection ----------
    Dialog.create("Statistics: Parameters");
    Dialog.addChoice("Parameters:", newArray("All parameters", "Select parameters..."), "All parameters");
    Dialog.show();
    pickMode = Dialog.getChoice();

    useParam = newArray(P);
    for (p=0; p<P; p++) useParam[p] = 1;

    if (pickMode == "Select parameters...") {
        Dialog.create("Select parameters (checked = analyze)");
        for (p=0; p<P; p++) Dialog.addCheckbox(paramNames[p], true);
        Dialog.show();
        for (p=0; p<P; p++) {
            if (Dialog.getCheckbox()) useParam[p] = 1;
            else useParam[p] = 0;
        }
    }

    // build selected index list
    selIdx = newArray(0);
    selNames = newArray(0);
    for (p=0; p<P; p++) {
        if (useParam[p] == 1) {
            selIdx = Array.concat(selIdx, p);
            selNames = Array.concat(selNames, paramNames[p]);
        }
    }
    if (lengthOf(selIdx) < 1) exit("No parameters selected.");

    // ---------- Stats options depending on k ----------
if (k == 2) {

    Dialog.create("Mann-Whitney options (2 groups)");
    Dialog.addCheckbox("Continuity correction (recommended; Prism-like for large N)", true);
    Dialog.addChoice("Correction across selected parameters:",
        newArray("None","FDR (BH)","Holm"), "None");
    Dialog.addDirectory("Save results to folder (optional; empty = no files):", outDir);
    Dialog.show();

    MW_useCC     = Dialog.getCheckbox();
    method_param = Dialog.getChoice();
    outDir2      = Dialog.getString();

    if (outDir2!="") {
        outDir2 = replace(outDir2, "\\", "/");
        if (!endsWith(outDir2, "/")) outDir2 = outDir2 + "/";
    }

    ST_runMannWhitneyTests(data, groups, uniq, groupNs, selIdx, selNames,
                           alpha, method_param, MW_useCC,
                           path, unitChoice, includeBeats, outDir2);

} else {

    Dialog.create("Kruskal-Wallis options (k >= 3)");
Dialog.addChoice("Correction across selected parameters:",
    newArray("None","FDR (BH)","Holm"), "None");
Dialog.addChoice("Pairwise correction (within each parameter):",
    newArray("None","FDR (BH)","Holm"), "Holm");
Dialog.addDirectory("Save results to folder (optional; empty = no files):", outDir);
Dialog.show();

method_omni  = Dialog.getChoice();
method_pairs = Dialog.getChoice();
outDir2      = Dialog.getString();

if (outDir2!="") {
    outDir2 = replace(outDir2, "\\", "/");
    if (!endsWith(outDir2, "/")) outDir2 = outDir2 + "/";
}

ST_runKruskalWallis(data, groups, uniq, groupNs, selIdx, selNames,
                    alpha, method_omni, method_pairs,
                    path, unitChoice, includeBeats, outDir2);
    
    
}
  

    print("\nPlease, wait for the Heatmaps to be finished...");
}


// ============================================================
// Mann-Whitney U (k==2) per selected parameter
// - Two-sided p via Normal approximation (ties corrected)
// - Optional continuity correction (Prism-like for large N)
// - Optional correction across parameters (None / BH / Holm)
// ============================================================
function ST_runMannWhitneyTests(data, groups, uniq, groupNs, selIdx, selNames,
                                alpha, method_param, useCC,
                                inPath, unitChoice, includeBeats, outDir) {

    g1 = uniq[0];
    g2 = uniq[1];

    print("\\Clear");
    print("=== STATISTICS RESULTS ===");
    print("Input: " + inPath);
    print("Unit of analysis: " + unitChoice);
    incTxt = "ON"; if (!includeBeats) incTxt = "OFF";
    print("Include Beats counted as parameter: " + incTxt);
    print("Mode: Mann-Whitney (two groups), two-sided");
    print("Groups: " + g1 + " (N=" + groupNs[0] + ") vs " + g2 + " (N=" + groupNs[1] + ")");
        
    ccTxt = "OFF";
	if (useCC) ccTxt = "ON";
	print("Continuity correction: " + ccTxt);
    
    print("Alpha: " + alpha);
    print("Correction across selected parameters: " + method_param);
    print("");

    M = lengthOf(selIdx);
    pvals = newArray(M);

    // Header: keep param name EXACTLY as in file; other headers are just for readability
    hdr = "Param\tN1 ("+g1+")\tN2 ("+g2+")\tMean1 ("+g1+")\tMean2 ("+g2+")\tDiff(1-2)\tU\tz\tp(two-sided)\tP summary";
    print(hdr);

    for (ii=0; ii<M; ii++) {

        pIndex = selIdx[ii];
        name   = selNames[ii];

        a = ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, g1, pIndex);
        b = ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, g2, pIndex);

        n1 = lengthOf(a);
        n2 = lengthOf(b);

        m1 = ST_avg(a);
        m2 = ST_avg(b);
        diff = m1 - m2;

        // If not enough data
        if (n1<1 || n2<1) {
            U = 0/0; z = 0/0; pval = 0/0;
        } else {

            // Build combined arrays for ranking
            N = n1 + n2;
            vals = newArray(N);
            gIdx = newArray(N);

            for (i=0; i<n1; i++) { vals[i] = a[i]; gIdx[i] = 0; }
            for (j=0; j<n2; j++) { vals[n1+j] = b[j]; gIdx[n1+j] = 1; }

            rs = ST_rankSums(vals, gIdx, 2);     // rs[0]=R1, rs[1]=R2, rs[2]=tieSum
            R1 = rs[0];
            tieSum = rs[2];

            // U statistics
            U1 = R1 - (n1*(n1+1))/2.0;
            U2 = n1*n2 - U1;
            U  = U1; if (U2 < U) U = U2;         // Prism often reports the smaller U

            // Mean/Var of U with tie correction
            meanU = n1*n2/2.0;

            // Var(U) = n1*n2/12 * [ (N+1) - tieSum/(N*(N-1)) ]
            // tieSum = Σ(t^3 - t) over tie blocks
            if (N<=1 || (N-1)==0) {
                z = 0/0; pval = 0/0;
            } else {
                tc = tieSum / (N*(N-1));   // tie correction term
                varU = (n1*n2/12.0) * ((N+1) - tc);

                if (varU <= 0) {
                    z = 0/0; pval = 0/0;
                } else {
                    sd = sqrt(varU);

                    // continuity correction (two-sided) – approximate Prism behaviour for large N
                    cc = 0.0;
                    if (useCC) {
                        // U is usually <= meanU (because we take min(U1,U2)), so (U-meanU) is negative:
                        // use +0.5 in numerator (equivalent to subtracting -0.5*sign)
                        if (U < meanU) cc = 0.5;
                        else if (U > meanU) cc = -0.5;
                        else cc = 0.0;
                    }

                    z = (U - meanU + cc) / sd;
                    pval = ST_p_value_norm_two_sided(z);
                }
            }
        }

        pvals[ii] = pval;

        print(name+"\t"+n1+"\t"+n2+"\t"+ST_d4(m1)+"\t"+ST_d4(m2)+"\t"+ST_d4(diff)+"\t"+
              ST_d3(U)+"\t"+ST_d3(z)+"\t"+ST_pPrism(pval)+"\t"+ST_pSummaryPrism(pval));
    }

    // correction across parameters (optional)
    adj = newArray(0);
    doAdj = false;
    if (method_param=="FDR (BH)") { adj = ST_bh_fdr_nanaware(pvals); doAdj = true; }
    else if (method_param=="Holm") { adj = ST_holm_nanaware(pvals); doAdj = true; }

    if (doAdj) {
        print("");
        print("Adjusted p-values across selected parameters ("+method_param+"):");
        print("Param\tp\tp_adj\tAdj summary");
        for (ii=0; ii<M; ii++) {
            print(selNames[ii]+"\t"+ST_pPrism(pvals[ii])+"\t"+ST_pPrism(adj[ii])+"\t"+ST_pSummaryPrism(adj[ii]));
        }
    }

    // Save results
    if (outDir!="") {
        base = ST_baseNameNoExt(inPath);

        out = "Mode\tMann-Whitney (two groups), two-sided\n";
        out = out + "Input\t"+inPath+"\n";
        out = out + "Unit_of_analysis\t"+unitChoice+"\n";
        incTxt = "ON"; if (!includeBeats) incTxt = "OFF";
        out = out + "Include_Beats_counted\t"+incTxt+"\n";
        out = out + "Groups\t"+g1+" vs "+g2+"\n";
        
        ccTxt = "OFF";
		if (useCC) ccTxt = "ON";
		out = out + "Continuity_correction\t" + ccTxt + "\n";
        
        out = out + "Alpha\t"+alpha+"\n";
        out = out + "Correction_across_parameters\t"+method_param+"\n\n";

        out = out + hdr + "\n";

        for (ii=0; ii<M; ii++) {
            pIndex = selIdx[ii];
            name   = selNames[ii];

            a = ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, g1, pIndex);
            b = ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, g2, pIndex);

            n1 = lengthOf(a);
            n2 = lengthOf(b);
            m1 = ST_avg(a);
            m2 = ST_avg(b);
            diff = m1 - m2;

            if (n1<1 || n2<1) { U=0/0; z=0/0; pval=0/0; }
            else {
                N = n1 + n2;
                vals = newArray(N);
                gIdx = newArray(N);
                for (i=0;i<n1;i++){ vals[i]=a[i]; gIdx[i]=0; }
                for (j=0;j<n2;j++){ vals[n1+j]=b[j]; gIdx[n1+j]=1; }

                rs = ST_rankSums(vals, gIdx, 2);
                R1 = rs[0]; tieSum = rs[2];

                U1 = R1 - (n1*(n1+1))/2.0;
                U2 = n1*n2 - U1;
                U  = U1; if (U2 < U) U = U2;

                meanU = n1*n2/2.0;
                tc = tieSum / (N*(N-1));
                varU = (n1*n2/12.0) * ((N+1) - tc);

                if (varU<=0) { z=0/0; pval=0/0; }
                else {
                    sd = sqrt(varU);
                    cc=0.0;
                    if (useCC) {
                        if (U < meanU) cc = 0.5;
                        else if (U > meanU) cc = -0.5;
                    }
                    z = (U - meanU + cc) / sd;
                    pval = ST_p_value_norm_two_sided(z);
                }
            }

            out = out + name+"\t"+n1+"\t"+n2+"\t"+ST_d4(m1)+"\t"+ST_d4(m2)+"\t"+ST_d4(diff)+"\t"+
                  ST_d3(U)+"\t"+ST_d3(z)+"\t"+ST_pPrism(pval)+"\t"+ST_pSummaryPrism(pval)+"\n";
        }

        if (doAdj) {
            out = out + "\nAdjusted p-values across selected parameters ("+method_param+"):\n";
            out = out + "Param\tp\tp_adj\tAdj summary\n";
            for (ii=0; ii<M; ii++) {
                out = out + selNames[ii]+"\t"+ST_pPrism(pvals[ii])+"\t"+ST_pPrism(adj[ii])+"\t"+ST_pSummaryPrism(adj[ii])+"\n";
            }
        }


// Hier gibt es Probleme mit den runden Klammern

		base2=replace(base, "\\(ENG\\)", "");
		base2=replace(base2, "\\(GER\\)", "");
		
		
	
        File.saveString(out, outDir+"STATS_mannwhitney_"+base2+"(ENG).txt");
        File.saveString(replace(out, ".", ","), outDir+"STATS_mannwhitney_"+base2+"(GER).txt");
        print("\nSaved: "+outDir+"STATS_mannwhitney__"+base2+" (ENG/GER).txt");

        
    }
}



// ============================================================
// One-way ANOVA (k>=3) per selected parameter
// + optional pairwise Welch t-tests per parameter (with optional gatekeeping)
// Pairwise written to file: ONLY significant pairs (raw or adjusted)
// ============================================================

// ============================================================
// Kruskal-Wallis (k>=3) per selected parameter
// - Omnibus test only (no post-hoc) for “quick hint”
// - Two-sided p via Chi-square approx (ties corrected)
// - Optional correction across parameters (None / BH / Holm)
// ============================================================

function ST_runKruskalWallis(data, groups, uniq, groupNs, selIdx, selNames,
                             alpha, method_omni, method_pairs,
                             inPath, unitChoice, includeBeats, outDir) {

    k = lengthOf(uniq);
    M = lengthOf(selIdx);

    print("\\Clear");
    print("=== STATISTICS RESULTS ===");
    print("Input: " + inPath);
    print("Unit of analysis: " + unitChoice);
    incTxt = "ON"; if (!includeBeats) incTxt = "OFF";
    print("Include Beats counted as parameter: " + incTxt);
    print("Mode: Kruskal-Wallis (k=" + k + ") + pairwise Mann-Whitney");
    print("Alpha: " + alpha);
    print("Correction across selected parameters: " + method_omni);
    print("Pairwise correction within each parameter: " + method_pairs);
    print("");

    pvals = newArray(M);
    Hvals = newArray(M);
    Nvals = newArray(M);

    hdr = "Param\tk\tN\tH\tDF\tp(two-sided)\tP summary";
    print(hdr);

    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    // 1) Omnibus Kruskal-Wallis
    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    for (ii=0; ii<M; ii++) {

        pIndex = selIdx[ii];
        name   = selNames[ii];

        Ns = newArray(k);
        totalN = 0;

        for (gi=0; gi<k; gi++) {
            arr = ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gi], pIndex);
            Ns[gi] = lengthOf(arr);
            totalN = totalN + Ns[gi];
        }

        if (totalN < k) {
            H = 0/0;
            df = k-1;
            pval = 0/0;
        } else {

            vals = newArray(totalN);
            gIdx = newArray(totalN);

            pos = 0;
            for (gi=0; gi<k; gi++) {
                arr = ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gi], pIndex);
                for (j=0; j<lengthOf(arr); j++) {
                    vals[pos] = arr[j];
                    gIdx[pos] = gi;
                    pos++;
                }
            }

            rs = ST_rankSums(vals, gIdx, k);
            tieSum = rs[k];

            sumTerm = 0.0;
            for (gi=0; gi<k; gi++) {
                if (Ns[gi] > 0) sumTerm = sumTerm + (rs[gi]*rs[gi]) / Ns[gi];
            }

            N = totalN;
            H = (12.0/(N*(N+1))) * sumTerm - 3.0*(N+1);

            denom = 1.0;
            if ((N*N*N - N) != 0) denom = 1.0 - (tieSum / (N*N*N - N));
            if (denom > 0) H = H / denom;

            df = k - 1;
            pval = ST_p_value_chi2_right(H, df);
        }

        Hvals[ii] = H;
        pvals[ii] = pval;
        Nvals[ii] = totalN;

        print(name+"\t"+k+"\t"+totalN+"\t"+ST_d3(H)+"\t"+(k-1)+"\t"+ST_pPrism(pval)+"\t"+ST_pSummaryPrism(pval));
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    // 2) Korrektur über Parameter hinweg (Omnibus)
    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    adj = newArray(0);
    doAdj = false;

    if (method_omni=="FDR (BH)") {
        adj = ST_bh_fdr_nanaware(pvals);
        doAdj = true;
    } else if (method_omni=="Holm") {
        adj = ST_holm_nanaware(pvals);
        doAdj = true;
    }

    if (doAdj) {
        print("");
        print("Adjusted p-values across selected parameters ("+method_omni+"):");
        print("Param\tp\tp_adj\tAdj summary");
        for (ii=0; ii<M; ii++) {
            print(selNames[ii]+"\t"+ST_pPrism(pvals[ii])+"\t"+ST_pPrism(adj[ii])+"\t"+ST_pSummaryPrism(adj[ii]));
        }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    // 3) Pairwise Mann-Whitney pro Parameter
    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    print("");
    print("Pairwise comparisons (Mann-Whitney), parameter-wise:");

    for (ii=0; ii<M; ii++) {

        pIndex = selIdx[ii];
        name   = selNames[ii];

        print("");
        print("# " + name);

        hdr2 = "GroupA\tGroupB\tN1\tN2\tMean1\tMean2\tDiff(1-2)\tU\tz\tp(two-sided)\tP summary";
        if (method_pairs!="None") {
            if (method_pairs=="FDR (BH)") hdr2 = hdr2 + "\tq(FDR)\tAdj summary";
            else hdr2 = hdr2 + "\tpHolm\tAdj summary";
        }
        print(hdr2);

        pair_pvals = newArray(0);
        pair_lines = newArray(0);

        for (gi=0; gi<k-1; gi++) {
            for (gj=gi+1; gj<k; gj++) {

                a = ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gi], pIndex);
                b = ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gj], pIndex);

                n1 = lengthOf(a);
                n2 = lengthOf(b);

                m1 = ST_avg(a);
                m2 = ST_avg(b);
                diff = m1 - m2;

                if (n1<1 || n2<1) {
                    U = 0/0;
                    z = 0/0;
                    pPair = 0/0;
                } else {
                    N = n1 + n2;
                    vals = newArray(N);
                    gIdx = newArray(N);

                    for (i=0; i<n1; i++) {
                        vals[i] = a[i];
                        gIdx[i] = 0;
                    }
                    for (j=0; j<n2; j++) {
                        vals[n1+j] = b[j];
                        gIdx[n1+j] = 1;
                    }

                    rs = ST_rankSums(vals, gIdx, 2);
                    R1 = rs[0];
                    tieSum = rs[2];

                    U1 = R1 - (n1*(n1+1))/2.0;
                    U2 = n1*n2 - U1;
                    U  = U1;
                    if (U2 < U) U = U2;

                    meanU = n1*n2/2.0;

                    if (N<=1 || (N-1)==0) {
                        z = 0/0;
                        pPair = 0/0;
                    } else {
                        tc = tieSum / (N*(N-1));
                        varU = (n1*n2/12.0) * ((N+1) - tc);

                        if (varU <= 0) {
                            z = 0/0;
                            pPair = 0/0;
                        } else {
                            sd = sqrt(varU);
                            z = (U - meanU) / sd;   // ohne continuity correction
                            pPair = ST_p_value_norm_two_sided(z);
                        }
                    }
                }

                baseLine = uniq[gi]+"\t"+uniq[gj]+"\t"+n1+"\t"+n2+"\t"+ST_d4(m1)+"\t"+ST_d4(m2)+"\t"+ST_d4(diff)+"\t"+ST_d3(U)+"\t"+ST_d3(z)+"\t"+ST_pPrism(pPair)+"\t"+ST_pSummaryPrism(pPair);

                if (method_pairs=="None") {
                    print(baseLine);
                } else {
                    pair_lines = Array.concat(pair_lines, baseLine);
                }

                pair_pvals = Array.concat(pair_pvals, pPair);
            }
        }

        if (method_pairs!="None") {
            if (method_pairs=="FDR (BH)") adjPairs = ST_bh_fdr_nanaware(pair_pvals);
            else adjPairs = ST_holm_nanaware(pair_pvals);

            for (idxPair=0; idxPair<lengthOf(pair_lines); idxPair++) {
                print(pair_lines[idxPair] + "\t" + ST_pPrism(adjPairs[idxPair]) + "\t" + ST_pSummaryPrism(adjPairs[idxPair]));
            }
        }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    // 4) Speichern
    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    if (outDir!="") {
        base = ST_baseNameNoExt(inPath);
        
        base2=replace(base, "\\(ENG\\)", "");
		base2=replace(base2, "\\(GER\\)", "");

        out = "Mode\tKruskal-Wallis (k="+k+") + pairwise Mann-Whitney\n";
        out = out + "Input\t"+inPath+"\n";
        out = out + "Unit_of_analysis\t"+unitChoice+"\n";
        incTxt = "ON"; if (!includeBeats) incTxt = "OFF";
        out = out + "Include_Beats_counted\t"+incTxt+"\n";
        out = out + "Alpha\t"+alpha+"\n";
        out = out + "Correction_across_parameters\t"+method_omni+"\n";
        out = out + "Pairwise_correction_within_parameter\t"+method_pairs+"\n\n";

        out = out + hdr + "\n";
        for (ii=0; ii<M; ii++) {
            out = out + selNames[ii]+"\t"+k+"\t"+Nvals[ii]+"\t"+ST_d3(Hvals[ii])+"\t"+(k-1)+"\t"+ST_pPrism(pvals[ii])+"\t"+ST_pSummaryPrism(pvals[ii])+"\n";
        }

        if (doAdj) {
            out = out + "\nAdjusted p-values across selected parameters ("+method_omni+"):\n";
            out = out + "Param\tp\tp_adj\tAdj summary\n";
            for (ii=0; ii<M; ii++) {
                out = out + selNames[ii]+"\t"+ST_pPrism(pvals[ii])+"\t"+ST_pPrism(adj[ii])+"\t"+ST_pSummaryPrism(adj[ii])+"\n";
            }
        }

        out = out + "\nPairwise comparisons (Mann-Whitney), parameter-wise:\n";

        for (ii=0; ii<M; ii++) {

            pIndex = selIdx[ii];
            name   = selNames[ii];

            out = out + "\n# " + name + "\n";

            hdr2 = "GroupA\tGroupB\tN1\tN2\tMean1\tMean2\tDiff(1-2)\tU\tz\tp(two-sided)\tP summary";
            if (method_pairs!="None") {
                if (method_pairs=="FDR (BH)") hdr2 = hdr2 + "\tq(FDR)\tAdj summary";
                else hdr2 = hdr2 + "\tpHolm\tAdj summary";
            }
            out = out + hdr2 + "\n";

            pair_pvals = newArray(0);
            pair_lines = newArray(0);

            for (gi=0; gi<k-1; gi++) {
                for (gj=gi+1; gj<k; gj++) {

                    a = ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gi], pIndex);
                    b = ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gj], pIndex);

                    n1 = lengthOf(a);
                    n2 = lengthOf(b);

                    m1 = ST_avg(a);
                    m2 = ST_avg(b);
                    diff = m1 - m2;

                    if (n1<1 || n2<1) {
                        U = 0/0;
                        z = 0/0;
                        pPair = 0/0;
                    } else {
                        N = n1 + n2;
                        vals = newArray(N);
                        gIdx = newArray(N);

                        for (i=0; i<n1; i++) {
                            vals[i] = a[i];
                            gIdx[i] = 0;
                        }
                        for (j=0; j<n2; j++) {
                            vals[n1+j] = b[j];
                            gIdx[n1+j] = 1;
                        }

                        rs = ST_rankSums(vals, gIdx, 2);
                        R1 = rs[0];
                        tieSum = rs[2];

                        U1 = R1 - (n1*(n1+1))/2.0;
                        U2 = n1*n2 - U1;
                        U  = U1;
                        if (U2 < U) U = U2;

                        meanU = n1*n2/2.0;

                        if (N<=1 || (N-1)==0) {
                            z = 0/0;
                            pPair = 0/0;
                        } else {
                            tc = tieSum / (N*(N-1));
                            varU = (n1*n2/12.0) * ((N+1) - tc);

                            if (varU <= 0) {
                                z = 0/0;
                                pPair = 0/0;
                            } else {
                                sd = sqrt(varU);
                                z = (U - meanU) / sd;
                                pPair = ST_p_value_norm_two_sided(z);
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    baseLine = uniq[gi]+"\t"+uniq[gj]+"\t"+n1+"\t"+n2+"\t"+ST_d4(m1)+"\t"+ST_d4(m2)+"\t"+ST_d4(diff)+"\t"+ST_d3(U)+"\t"+ST_d3(z)+"\t"+ST_pPrism(pPair)+"\t"+ST_pSummaryPrism(pPair);

                    if (method_pairs=="None") {
                        out = out + baseLine + "\n";
                    } else {
                        pair_lines = Array.concat(pair_lines, baseLine);
                    }

                    pair_pvals = Array.concat(pair_pvals, pPair);
                }
            }

            if (method_pairs!="None") {
                if (method_pairs=="FDR (BH)") adjPairs = ST_bh_fdr_nanaware(pair_pvals);
                else adjPairs = ST_holm_nanaware(pair_pvals);

                for (idxPair=0; idxPair<lengthOf(pair_lines); idxPair++) {
                    out = out + pair_lines[idxPair] + "\t" + ST_pPrism(adjPairs[idxPair]) + "\t" + ST_pSummaryPrism(adjPairs[idxPair]) + "\n";
                }
            }
        }


		base2=replace(base, "\\(ENG\\)", "");
		base2=replace(base2, "\\(GER\\)", "");

        File.saveString(out, outDir+"STATS_kruskalwallis_"+base2+" (ENG).txt");
        File.saveString(replace(out, ".", ","), outDir+"STATS_kruskalwallis_"+base2+" (GER).txt");
        print("\nSaved: "+outDir+"STATS_kruskalwallis__"+base2+" (ENG/GER).txt");

    }
}


// ============================================================
// HELPERS
// ============================================================

function ST_findCol(cols, name) {
    for (i=0; i<lengthOf(cols); i++) if (cols[i]==name) return i;
    return -1;
}

function ST_zeroArray(n) {
    a = newArray(n);
    for (ii=0; ii<n; ii++) a[ii] = 0;
    return a;
}

function ST_uniqueStrings(arr) {
    u = newArray(0);
    for (i=0; i<lengthOf(arr); i++) {
        s = arr[i];
        found = false;
        for (j=0; j<lengthOf(u); j++) if (u[j]==s) {found=true; break;}
        if (!found) u = Array.concat(u, s);
    }
    return u;
}

function ST_countString(arr, s) {
    c = 0;
    for (i=0; i<lengthOf(arr); i++) if (arr[i]==s) c = c + 1;
    return c;
}

// convert raw field to numeric string "x.y" or "NaN"
// IMPORTANT: must return NUMERIC (or NaN) to avoid "Numeric return value expected"
function ST_toNumberStringOrNaN(raw) {
    return ST_parseFloatSafe(raw); // numeric value or NaN (0/0)
}


function ST_numOrNaNString(v) {
    if (v==v) return ""+v;
    return "NaN";
}

// robust parseFloat: supports comma decimals; strips spaces; maps Infinity/blank -> NaN
function ST_parseFloatSafe(raw) {
    if (raw=="") return 0/0;
    s = "" + raw;
    s = replace(s, " ", "");
    s = replace(s, ",", ".");
    if (s=="NaN" || s=="Infinity" || s=="-Infinity") return 0/0;
    v = parseFloat(s);
    return v;
}

// collect parameter values for a group from data rows (tab-joined numeric strings)
function ST_collectParamForGroup(data, groups, g, pIndex) {
    out = newArray(0);
    for (i=0; i<lengthOf(data); i++) {
        if (groups[i]!=g) continue;
        fields = split(data[i], "\t");
        if (pIndex >= lengthOf(fields)) continue;

        v = ST_parseFloatSafe(fields[pIndex]); // <-- FIX
        if (v==v) out = Array.concat(out, v);
    }
    return out;
}


// ---------- basic stats ----------
function ST_avg(a) {
    if (lengthOf(a)==0) return 0/0;
    s=0;
    for (i=0;i<lengthOf(a);i++) s = s + a[i];
    return s/lengthOf(a);
}
function ST_variance(a, unbiased) {
    n=lengthOf(a);
    if (n<2) return 0/0;
    m=ST_avg(a);
    ss=0;
    for (i=0;i<n;i++) ss = ss + (a[i]-m)*(a[i]-m);
    denom = n;
    if (unbiased) denom = n-1;
    return ss/denom;
}
function ST_weightedMean(means, Ns) {
    num=0; den=0;
    for (i=0;i<lengthOf(means);i++) {
        if (Ns[i]>0 && means[i]==means[i]) {
            num = num + means[i]*Ns[i];
            den = den + Ns[i];
        }
    }
    if (den>0) return num/den;
    return 0/0;
}
function ST_welchDF(s1,n1,s2,n2) {
    a = s1/n1 + s2/n2;
    b = (s1*s1)/(n1*n1*(n1-1)) + (s2*s2)/(n2*n2*(n2-1));
    return a*a / b;
}

// ---------- p-values via incomplete beta ----------
function ST_p_value_t_two_sided(t, df) {
    x = df / (df + t*t);
    return ST_betai(0.5*df, 0.5, x);
}
function ST_p_value_f_right(F, df1, df2) {
    x = df2 / (df2 + df1*F);
    return ST_betai(0.5*df2, 0.5*df1, x);
}
function ST_betai(a,b,x) {
    if (x<=0) return 0;
    if (x>=1) return 1;
    bt = exp(ST_gammln(a+b) - ST_gammln(a) - ST_gammln(b) + a*log(x) + b*log(1.0 - x));
    if (x < (a+1.0)/(a+b+2.0)) return bt*ST_betacf(a,b,x)/a;
    else return 1.0 - bt*ST_betacf(b,a,1.0-x)/b;
}
function ST_betacf(a,b,x) {
    MAXIT=200;
    EPS=3.0e-7;
    FPMIN=1.0e-30;
    qab=a+b; qap=a+1.0; qam=a-1.0;
    c=1.0;
    d=1.0 - qab*x/qap;
    if (abs(d)<FPMIN) d=FPMIN;
    d=1.0/d;
    h=d;
    for (m=1; m<=MAXIT; m++) {
        m2=2*m;
        aa = m*(b-m)*x/((qam+m2)*(a+m2));
        d = 1.0 + aa*d;
        if (abs(d)<FPMIN) d=FPMIN;
        d=1.0/d;
        c = 1.0 + aa/c;
        if (abs(c)<FPMIN) c=FPMIN;
        h = h * d * c;

        aa = -(a+m)*(qab+m)*x/((a+m2)*(qap+m2));
        d = 1.0 + aa*d;
        if (abs(d)<FPMIN) d=FPMIN;
        d=1.0/d;
        c = 1.0 + aa/c;
        if (abs(c)<FPMIN) c=FPMIN;
        del = d*c;
        h = h * del;
        if (abs(del-1.0) < EPS) break;
    }
    return h;
}
function ST_gammln(xx) {
    cof = newArray(76.18009172947146,-86.50532032941677,24.01409824083091,
                   -1.231739572450155,0.001208650973866179,-5.395239384953e-6);
    x=xx; y=xx;
    tmp = x + 5.5;
    tmp = tmp - (x + 0.5)*log(tmp);
    ser = 1.000000000190015;
    for (j=0; j<6; j++) { y = y + 1.0; ser = ser + cof[j]/y; }
    return -tmp + log(2.5066282746310005*ser/x);
}

// ---------- multiple testing ----------
function ST_bh_fdr(pvals) {
    m = lengthOf(pvals);
    idx = newArray(m);
    for (i=0;i<m;i++) idx[i]=i;
    for (i=0;i<m-1;i++) {
        imin=i;
        for (j=i+1;j<m;j++) if (pvals[idx[j]] < pvals[idx[imin]]) imin=j;
        tmp=idx[i]; idx[i]=idx[imin]; idx[imin]=tmp;
    }
    q = newArray(m);
    minQ = 1.0;
    for (r=m-1; r>=0; r--) {
        i = idx[r];
        val = pvals[i]*m/(r+1);
        if (val<minQ) minQ=val;
        if (minQ<1.0) q[i]=minQ; else q[i]=1.0;
    }
    return q;
}
function ST_bh_fdr_nanaware(pvals) {
    idxValid = newArray(0);
    pvValid  = newArray(0);
    for (i=0;i<lengthOf(pvals);i++) if (pvals[i]==pvals[i]) {
        idxValid = Array.concat(idxValid, i);
        pvValid  = Array.concat(pvValid, pvals[i]);
    }
    out = newArray(lengthOf(pvals));
    for (i=0;i<lengthOf(out);i++) out[i]=0/0;
    if (lengthOf(pvValid)==0) return out;
    adjValid = ST_bh_fdr(pvValid);
    for (k2=0;k2<lengthOf(idxValid);k2++) out[idxValid[k2]] = adjValid[k2];
    return out;
}
function ST_holm(pvals) {
    m = lengthOf(pvals);
    idx = newArray(m);
    for (i=0;i<m;i++) idx[i]=i;
    for (i=0;i<m-1;i++) {
        imin=i;
        for (j=i+1;j<m;j++) if (pvals[idx[j]] < pvals[idx[imin]]) imin=j;
        tmp=idx[i]; idx[i]=idx[imin]; idx[imin]=tmp;
    }
    padj_sorted = newArray(m);
    for (r=0; r<m; r++) {
        i = idx[r];
        val = pvals[i] * (m - r);
        if (val>1.0) val = 1.0;
        padj_sorted[r] = val;
    }
    for (r=1; r<m; r++) {
        if (padj_sorted[r] < padj_sorted[r-1]) padj_sorted[r] = padj_sorted[r-1];
    }
    padj = newArray(m);
    for (r=0; r<m; r++) {
        i = idx[r];
        padj[i] = padj_sorted[r];
    }
    return padj;
}
function ST_holm_nanaware(pvals) {
    idxValid = newArray(0);
    pvValid  = newArray(0);
    for (i=0;i<lengthOf(pvals);i++) if (pvals[i]==pvals[i]) {
        idxValid = Array.concat(idxValid, i);
        pvValid  = Array.concat(pvValid, pvals[i]);
    }
    out = newArray(lengthOf(pvals));
    for (i=0;i<lengthOf(out);i++) out[i]=0/0;
    if (lengthOf(pvValid)==0) return out;
    adjValid = ST_holm(pvValid);
    for (k2=0;k2<lengthOf(idxValid);k2++) out[idxValid[k2]] = adjValid[k2];
    return out;
}

// ---------- formatting ----------
function ST_d3(v) { return "" + round(v*1000)/1000; }
function ST_sci(v) {
    if (v!=v) return "NA";
    if (v==0) return "0";
    e = floor(log(abs(v))/log(10));
    m = v / pow(10,e);
    return "" + ST_d3(m) + "e" + e;
}
function ST_sigStars(p) {
    if (p!=p) return "NA";
    if (p <= 0.0001) return "****";
    if (p <= 0.001)  return "***";
    if (p <= 0.01)   return "**";
    if (p <= 0.05)   return "*";
    return "ns";
}

// filename helper (no lastIndexOf; manual scan)
function ST_baseNameNoExt(path) {
    p = replace(path, "\\", "/");
    last = -1;
    for (i=0; i<lengthOf(p); i++) {
        if (substring(p, i, i+1)=="/") last = i;
    }
    name = p;
    if (last >= 0) name = substring(p, last+1);

    // strip trailing ".txt"
    if (endsWith(name, ".txt")) name = substring(name, 0, lengthOf(name)-4);
    return name;
}


// ============================================================
// RANKS (ties handled): returns array length (k+1)
// [0..k-1] = rank sums per group, [k] = tieSum = Σ(t^3 - t)
// NOTE: ImageJ macro '&&' may not short-circuit reliably -> avoid vals[j+1] access in condition
// ============================================================
function ST_rankSums(vals, gIdx, k) {

    // Sort vals asc with parallel gIdx
    ST_sort2(vals, gIdx);

    rankSums = newArray(k);
    for (ii=0; ii<k; ii++) rankSums[ii] = 0.0;

    tieSum = 0.0;

    N = lengthOf(vals);
    r = 1.0; // IMPORTANT: float rank counter

    i = 0;
    while (i < N) {

        j = i;

        // SAFE tie-scan (no short-circuit assumptions!)
        while (true) {
            if (j + 1 >= N) break;
            if (vals[j + 1] != vals[i]) break;
            j++;
        }

        t = j - i + 1;

        // average rank for ties: (r + (r+t-1))/2
        avgRank = (r + (r + t - 1.0)) / 2.0;  // IMPORTANT: float math

        for (m=i; m<=j; m++) {
            gi = gIdx[m];
            if (gi >= 0 && gi < k) rankSums[gi] = rankSums[gi] + avgRank;
        }

        if (t > 1) tieSum = tieSum + (t*t*t - t);

        r = r + t;      // r stays float
        i = j + 1;
    }

    out = newArray(k+1);
    for (ii=0; ii<k; ii++) out[ii] = rankSums[ii];
    out[k] = tieSum;
    return out;
}


// ============================================================
// Iterative quicksort for numeric array vals with parallel gIdx
// ============================================================
function ST_sort2(vals, gIdx) {
    n = lengthOf(vals);
    if (n < 2) return;

    // stack for segments
    stackLo = newArray(n);
    stackHi = newArray(n);
    top = 0;
    stackLo[0] = 0;
    stackHi[0] = n-1;

    while (top >= 0) {
        lo = stackLo[top];
        hi = stackHi[top];
        top--;

        i = lo;
        j = hi;
        pivot = vals[floor((lo+hi)/2)];

        while (i <= j) {
            while (vals[i] < pivot) i++;
            while (vals[j] > pivot) j--;
            if (i <= j) {
                tmp = vals[i]; vals[i] = vals[j]; vals[j] = tmp;
                tmg = gIdx[i]; gIdx[i] = gIdx[j]; gIdx[j] = tmg;
                i++; j--;
            }
        }

        if (lo < j) { top++; stackLo[top] = lo; stackHi[top] = j; }
        if (i < hi) { top++; stackLo[top] = i;  stackHi[top] = hi; }
    }
}

// ============================================================
// Normal approx p-value (two-sided) from z
// p = 2 * (1 - Phi(|z|)) = 2 * SF(|z|)
// ============================================================
function ST_p_value_norm_two_sided(z) {
    if (z!=z) return 0/0;
    az = abs(z);
    sf = ST_norm_sf(az);
    p = 2.0 * sf;
    if (p > 1.0) p = 1.0;
    return p;
}

// survival function SF(z) for standard normal (z>=0)
// Abramowitz-Stegun approximation (fast, good enough for stats output)
function ST_norm_sf(z) {
    if (z < 0) z = -z;

    p = 0.2316419;
    b1 = 0.319381530;
    b2 = -0.356563782;
    b3 = 1.781477937;
    b4 = -1.821255978;
    b5 = 1.330274429;

    t = 1.0 / (1.0 + p*z);
    poly = ((((b5*t + b4)*t + b3)*t + b2)*t + b1)*t;

    // phi(z) = exp(-z^2/2)/sqrt(2*pi)
    phi = exp(-0.5*z*z) / 2.5066282746310002;

    // SF ≈ phi * poly
    return phi * poly;
}

// ============================================================
// Chi-square right-tail p-value: p = P(Chi^2_df >= x)
// p = gammq(df/2, x/2)
// ============================================================
function ST_p_value_chi2_right(x, df) {
    if (x!=x) return 0/0;
    if (x < 0) return 1.0;
    a = df/2.0;
    xx = x/2.0;
    return ST_gammq(a, xx);
}

// Regularized upper incomplete gamma Q(a,x)
function ST_gammq(a, x) {
    if (x < 0 || a <= 0) return 0/0;
    if (x < a + 1.0) {
        // Q = 1 - P (series)
        return 1.0 - ST_gser(a, x);
    } else {
        // Q directly (continued fraction)
        return ST_gcf(a, x);
    }
}

// Series representation of P(a,x)
function ST_gser(a, x) {
    ITMAX = 200;
    EPS = 3.0e-7;

    gln = ST_gammln(a);
    if (x <= 0) return 0.0;

    ap = a;
    sum = 1.0 / a;
    del = sum;

    for (n=1; n<=ITMAX; n++) {
        ap = ap + 1.0;
        del = del * x / ap;
        sum = sum + del;
        if (abs(del) < abs(sum)*EPS) break;
    }

    return sum * exp(-x + a*log(x) - gln);
}

// Continued fraction representation of Q(a,x)
function ST_gcf(a, x) {
    ITMAX = 200;
    EPS = 3.0e-7;
    FPMIN = 1.0e-30;

    gln = ST_gammln(a);

    b = x + 1.0 - a;
    c = 1.0 / FPMIN;
    d = 1.0 / b;
    h = d;

    for (i=1; i<=ITMAX; i++) {
        an = -i * (i - a);
        b = b + 2.0;
        d = an * d + b;
        if (abs(d) < FPMIN) d = FPMIN;
        c = b + an / c;
        if (abs(c) < FPMIN) c = FPMIN;
        d = 1.0 / d;
        del = d * c;
        h = h * del;
        if (abs(del - 1.0) < EPS) break;
    }

    return exp(-x + a*log(x) - gln) * h;
}

// ============================================================
// Formatting helpers (Prism-ish p printing)
// ============================================================
function ST_d3(v) { return "" + round(v*1000)/1000; }
function ST_d4(v) { return "" + round(v*10000)/10000; }

function ST_pPrism(p) {
    if (p!=p) return "NA";
    if (p < 0.0001) return "<0.0001";
    // show 4 decimals like Prism often does
    return "" + (round(p*10000)/10000);
}

function ST_pSummaryPrism(p) {
    if (p!=p) return "NA";
    if (p <= 0.0001) return "Yes (****)";
    if (p <= 0.001)  return "Yes (***)";
    if (p <= 0.01)   return "Yes (**)";
    if (p <= 0.05)   return "Yes (*)";
    return "ns";
}




}

// 11) Prepare for ANOVA
// =======================
if (option=="11. Prepare data for ANOVA (contractions)") {

   // =======================
   // 11) Prepare for ANOVA
   // =======================

    // --- 1) Choose main folder (""-check only) ---
    startDir = getDirectory("Choose the main folder (recursive search)");
    if (startDir=="") exit("Aborted.");

    // Normalize paths
    startDir = replace(startDir, "\\", "/");
    if (!endsWith(startDir, "/")) startDir += "/";

    print("\\Clear");
    print("Searching… please wait.\n");
    print("Root directory: " + startDir+"\n");

    // --- 2) Iterative folder scan (stack) ---
    // per folder: keep the newest file whose name contains "Extracted results (eng)"
    foundPaths = newArray(0);

    stack = newArray(startDir);
    idx = 0;
    while (idx < stack.length) {
        current = stack[idx];
        if (!endsWith(current, "/")) current += "/";

        items = getFileList(current);

        // ""-variant only: empty folder -> continue
        if (items.length==0) {
            print("WARNING: No access/empty: " + current);
            idx++;
            continue;
        }

        bestPath = "";
        bestKey  = -1;

        for (i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
            name = items[i];

            if (endsWith(name, "/")) {
                folder = current + name;
                folder = replace(folder, "\\", "/");
                stack = Array.concat(stack, folder);
            } else {
                if (indexOf(name, "Extracted results (eng)") != -1) {
                    path = current + name;
                    // last modification time as key (millis since 1970)
                    k = File.lastModified(path) + 0; // numeric
                    if (k > bestKey) { bestKey = k; bestPath = path; }
                }
            }
        }

        if (bestPath != "") {
            foundPaths = Array.concat(foundPaths, newArray(bestPath));
        }

        idx++;
    }

    nFiles = foundPaths.length;
    if (nFiles == 0) exit("No files found whose filename contains \"Extracted results (eng)\".");

    // --- 2a) Preview list of found files + RELATIVE FOLDER ---
    print("\n--- FOUND FILES (newest per directory) ---\n");
    for (i=0; i<nFiles; i++) {
        rel = relFolderFromBase(startDir, foundPaths[i]);
        print( (i+1)+": "+foundPaths[i] + "\n    Folder (relative): " + rel );
    }
    print("\n--- END OF LIST ---\n");

    // Optional: save the list as TXT before continuing
    Dialog.create("Found files – preview");
    Dialog.addMessage("Found: "+nFiles+" file(s).\nFull list is printed in the console.");
    Dialog.addCheckbox("Save list as TXT", true);
    Dialog.addDirectory("Target folder:", startDir);
    Dialog.addChoice("Continue with group assignment?", newArray("Yes","Cancel"), "Yes");
    Dialog.show();
    saveList = Dialog.getCheckbox();
    listDir  = Dialog.getString();
    goNext   = Dialog.getChoice();

    if (saveList) {
        
        listText=getInfo("log");
        
        File.saveString(listText, listDir + "FOUND_files.txt");
        print("List saved: " + listDir + "FOUND_files.txt");
    }
    if (goNext=="Cancel") exit("Canceled after preview list.");

    // --- 3) Number of groups + names ---
    Dialog.create("Define groups");
    Dialog.addNumber("Number of groups:", 2);
    Dialog.show();
    nGroups = round(Dialog.getNumber());
    if (nGroups < 1) nGroups = 1;

    Dialog.create("Group names");
    groupNames = newArray(nGroups);
    for (g = 0; g < nGroups; g++) {
        Dialog.addString("Group name " + (g+1) + ":", "Group_"+(g+1));
    }
    Dialog.show();
    for (g = 0; g < nGroups; g++) {
        nm = Dialog.getString();
        if (nm == "") nm = "Group_"+(g+1);
        groupNames[g] = nm;
    }

    // Choice list incl. Exclude
    choiceList = newArray(nGroups + 1);
    for (g = 0; g < nGroups; g++) choiceList[g] = groupNames[g];
    choiceList[nGroups] = "Exclude";

    // --- 4) Interactive assignment (chunked) ---
    assignments = newArray(nFiles);
    for (i = 0; i < nFiles; i++) assignments[i] = groupNames[0];

    CHUNK = 20;
    for (start = 0; start < nFiles; start += CHUNK) {
        stop = start + CHUNK; if (stop > nFiles) stop = nFiles;

        Dialog.create("Assignment (" + (start+1) + "–" + stop + " / " + nFiles + ")");
        for (i = start; i < stop; i++) {
            // Label with RELATIVE FOLDER + FILENAME
            rel = relFolderFromBase(startDir, foundPaths[i]);  // e.g., "58/AVI/VidsMovement .../dataplots/"
            fname = basename(foundPaths[i]);                   // e.g., "Extracted results (eng) Results (selected) ..."
            label = "" + (i+1) + ") " + rel + fname;
            Dialog.addChoice(label, choiceList, assignments[i]);
        }
        Dialog.show();
        for (i = start; i < stop; i++) {
            assignments[i] = Dialog.getChoice();
        }
    }

    // --- 5) Get header line (once) ---
    header = "";
    for (i = 0; i < nFiles; i++) {
        if (assignments[i] != "Exclude") { header = readHeaderLine(foundPaths[i]); break; }
    }
    if (header == "") header = readHeaderLine(foundPaths[0]);
    if (header == "") exit("Could not read header line.");

    // --- 6) Output folder ---
    outDir = getDirectory("Choose output folder (empty = use main folder)");
    if (outDir=="") outDir = startDir;
    outDir = replace(outDir, "\\", "/");
    if (!endsWith(outDir, "/")) outDir += "/";

    // --- 7) Write group files ---
    groupCounts = newArray(nGroups);
    for (g = 0; g < nGroups; g++) groupCounts[g] = 0;

    for (g = 0; g < nGroups; g++) {
        groupTitle = groupNames[g];
        outName = "Group_" + sanitizeFileName(groupTitle) + "_merged (ENG).txt";
        outPath = outDir + outName;
        
        outName2 = "Group_" + sanitizeFileName(groupTitle) + "_merged (GER).txt";
        outPath2 = outDir + outName2;

        outText = groupTitle + "\n" + header + "\n";

        for (i = 0; i < nFiles; i++) {
            if (assignments[i] == groupTitle) {
                body = readBody(foundPaths[i]);
                if (body != "") {
                    if (!endsWith(body, "\n")) body = body + "\n";
                    outText += body;
                    groupCounts[g]++;
                }
            }
        }

        File.saveString(outText, outPath);
        outText2=replace(outText, ".", ",");
        File.saveString(outText2, outPath2);
        print("Group \"" + groupTitle + "\": " + groupCounts[g] + " file(s) -> " + outPath);
    }

    // --- 8) Combined file (optional) ---
    makeCombined = true;
    if (makeCombined) {
        comboHeader = "Group\t" + header;
        combo = comboHeader + "\n";
        rowsAdded = 0;

        for (i = 0; i < nFiles; i++) {
            grp = assignments[i];
            if (grp == "Exclude") continue;
            body = readBody(foundPaths[i]);
            if (body != "") {
                body = replace(body, "\r", "");
                lines = split(body, "\n");
                for (k = 0; k < lines.length; k++) {
                    line = lines[k];
                    if (line == "") continue;
                    combo += grp + "\t" + line + "\n";
                    rowsAdded++;
                }
            }
        }

        comboPath = outDir + "ALL_groups_MERGED (ENG).txt";
        File.saveString(combo, comboPath);
        
        comboPath2 = outDir + "ALL_groups_MERGED (GER).txt";
        combo2=replace(combo, ".", ",");
        File.saveString(combo2, comboPath2);
        
        print("Combined file: " + rowsAdded + " row(s) -> " + comboPath);
    }

    print("Done.");



// =======================
// Helper functions (IJ1)
// =======================

// Relative folder path: difference between base (main folder) and file folder
function relFolderFromBase(base, filePath) {
    b = replace(base, "\\", "/");
    if (!endsWith(b, "/")) b += "/";
    dir = dirname(filePath);
    dir = replace(dir, "\\", "/");
    if (startsWith(dir, b)) {
        rel = substring(dir, lengthOf(b));
        if (rel=="") rel = "."; // directly in main folder
        return rel;
    }
    // Fallback: no common prefix found -> return folder
    return dir;
}

// Folder name from path
function dirname(p) {
    pp = replace(p, "\\", "/");
    n = lengthOf(pp);
    last = -1;
    for (k = 0; k < n; k++) {
        ch = substring(pp, k, k+1);
        if (ch == "/") last = k;
    }
    if (last >= 0) return substring(pp, 0, last+1);
    return "";
}

// File name from path
function basename(p) {
    n = lengthOf(p);
    last = -1;
    for (k = 0; k < n; k++) {
        ch = substring(p, k, k+1);
        if (ch == "/" || ch == "\\") last = k;
    }
    if (last >= 0) return substring(p, last+1);
    return p;
}

// Read first line (header) only
function readHeaderLine(path) {
    txt = File.openAsString(path);
    txt = replace(txt, "\r", "");
    nl = indexOf(txt, "\n");
    if (nl < 0) return trim(txt);
    return trim(substring(txt, 0, nl));
}

// Return body without first line (header)
function readBody(path) {
    txt = File.openAsString(path);
    txt = replace(txt, "\r", "");
    nl = indexOf(txt, "\n");
    if (nl < 0) return "";
    return substring(txt, nl+1);
}

// Make a filesystem-safe name
function sanitizeFileName(s) {
    t = s;
    bad = newArray("\\", "/", ":", "*", "?", "\"", "<", ">", "|");
    for (i=0; i<bad.length; i++) t = replace(t, bad[i], "_");
    t = replace(t, " ", "_");
    t = replace(t, "\t", "_");
    return t;
}

}


// Conduct ANOVA

// =====================================================================
// Stats from merged file (IJ1-only)
// Input: "ALL_groups_MERGED (ENG).txt"  (col0 = Group, cols1..14 = values)
// - 2 groups  -> Welch t-test per parameter
// - >=3 groups -> One-way ANOVA per parameter + pairwise Welch t-tests
// - p-values via incomplete beta (betai) implementation
// - Multiple testing options: None / FDR (BH) / Holm
// - Gatekeeping option: pairwise only if omnibus is significant at alpha=0.05
// - Outputs: Log + TXT (ENG) and TXT (GER, decimal comma)
// - Significance stars (Prism style): ns, *, **, ***, ****
// - No use of `null` and no ternary operator (IJ1-safe)
// =====================================================================


if (option=="12. Apply ANOVA (contractions)") {	

runStats(); // entry point

function runStats() {
    // --- Pick merged file ---
    path = File.openDialog("Choose 'ALL_groups_MERGED (ENG).txt'");
    if (path=="") exit("Aborted.");

    txt = File.openAsString(path);
    if (txt=="") exit("File empty.");

    // Normalize line endings and parse
    txt = replace(txt, "\r", "");
    lines = split(txt, "\n");
    if (lines.length < 2) exit("Not enough data lines.");

    header = lines[0];
    cols = split(header, "\t");
    if (cols.length < 15) exit("Header should be: Group + 14 columns.");

    // Parameter names (14: cols 1..14)
    paramNames = newArray(14);
    for (j=0; j<14; j++) paramNames[j] = cols[j+1];

    // Read data (group + 14 numeric values)
    groups = newArray(0);
    data = newArray(0); // store each row as tab-joined 14 numbers

    for (i=1; i<lines.length; i++) {
        line = lines[i];
        if (line=="") continue;
        parts = split(line, "\t");
        if (parts.length < 15) continue;

        // NEU (synchron)
	g = parts[0];

	rowVals = newArray(14);
	ok = true;
	for (j=0; j<14; j++) {
   	 v = replace(parts[j+1], ",", ".");
   	 if (v=="") { ok=false; break; }
    	rowVals[j] = parseFloat(v);
	}
	if (!ok) continue;

	// erst NACH erfolgreichem Parsen beides append
	groups = appendStr(groups, g);
	data   = appendStr(data, joinNumbers(rowVals, "\t"));

    }

    // Unique groups (in order of appearance)
    uniq = uniqueStrings(groups);
    k = uniq.length;
    if (k < 2) exit("Need at least 2 groups in data.");

    // Options (methods for corrections + optional save dir + gatekeeping)
    Dialog.create("Statistics Options");
    Dialog.addChoice("Omnibus correction (across 14 parameters):",
                     newArray("None","FDR (BH)","Holm"), "FDR (BH)");
    Dialog.addChoice("Pairwise correction (within each parameter):",
                     newArray("None","FDR (BH)","Holm"), "FDR (BH)");
    Dialog.addCheckbox("Gatekeep pairwise by omnibus significance (alpha = 0.05)", true);
    Dialog.addDirectory("Save results to folder (leave empty = no file):", "");
    Dialog.show();
    method_omni  = Dialog.getChoice();
    method_pairs = Dialog.getChoice();
    gatekeepPairs = Dialog.getCheckbox();
    outDir = Dialog.getString();
    if (outDir!="") {
        outDir = replace(outDir, "\\", "/");
        if (!endsWith(outDir, "/")) outDir += "/";
    }

    print("\\Clear");
    print("=== Statistics on merged file ===");
    print("File: " + path);
    print("Groups detected ("+k+"): " + joinStrings(uniq, ", "));
    print("Omnibus correction: " + method_omni);
    print("Pairwise correction: " + method_pairs);
    gateTxt = "OFF";
    if (gatekeepPairs) gateTxt = "ON";
    print("Gatekeeping (pairwise only if omnibus sig @0.05): " + gateTxt);
    print("");

    if (k==2) {
        // =========================
        // Welch t-test (two groups)
        // =========================
        print("Mode: Welch t-test (two groups)\n");
        pvals = newArray(14); // omnibus == t-tests here

        // Header mit Gruppennamen in Klammern
        hdr2 = "Param\tN1 ("+uniq[0]+")\tN2 ("+uniq[1]+")\tMean1 ("+uniq[0]+")\tMean2 ("+uniq[1]+")\tDiff(2-1)\tt\tDF\tp(two-sided)\tsig(p)";
        print(hdr2);

        for (p=0; p<14; p++) {
            a = collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[0], p);
            b = collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[1], p);
            n1=a.length; n2=b.length;
            m1=avg(a); m2=avg(b);
            s1=variance(a, true); s2=variance(b, true);

            if (n1<2 || n2<2) {
                t  = 0/0; 
                df = 0/0; 
                pval = 0/0;
            } else {
                t  = (m2 - m1) / sqrt(s1/n1 + s2/n2);
                df = welchDF(s1,n1,s2,n2);
                pval = p_value_t_two_sided(abs(t), df);
            }
            pvals[p] = pval;
            print(paramNames[p]+"\t"+n1+"\t"+n2+"\t"+d3(m1)+"\t"+d3(m2)+"\t"+d3(m2-m1)+"\t"+d3(t)+"\t"+d3(df)+"\t"+sci(pval)+"\t"+sigStars(pval));
        }

        // --- Omnibus correction across the 14 parameters (ALWAYS array) ---
        if (method_omni=="FDR (BH)") {
            adj = bh_fdr_nanaware(pvals);
        } else if (method_omni=="Holm") {
            adj = holm_nanaware(pvals);
        } else {
            adj = newArray(0);
        }

        // Safety: align length if needed
        if (adj.length>0 && adj.length!=pvals.length) {
            adj2 = newArray(pvals.length);
            for (pp=0; pp<adj2.length; pp++) adj2[pp] = 0/0;
            for (pp=0; pp<adj.length && pp<adj2.length; pp++) adj2[pp] = adj[pp];
            adj = adj2;
        }

        if (adj.length>0) {
            print("");
            if (method_omni=="FDR (BH)") {
                print("FDR (Benjamini–Hochberg) across the 14 parameters:");
                print("Param\tp\tq(FDR)\tsig(q)");
                for (p=0; p<14; p++) print(paramNames[p]+"\t"+sci(pvals[p])+"\t"+sci(adj[p])+"\t"+sigStars(adj[p]));
            } else if (method_omni=="Holm") {
                print("Holm (FWER) across the 14 parameters:");
                print("Param\tp\tpHolm\tsig(pHolm)");
                for (p=0; p<14; p++) print(paramNames[p]+"\t"+sci(pvals[p])+"\t"+sci(adj[p])+"\t"+sigStars(adj[p]));
            }
        }

        // Save files (ENG + GER)
        if (outDir!="") {
            out = "Mode\tWelch t-test (two groups)\n";
            out += "Groups\t"+uniq[0]+" vs "+uniq[1]+"\n";
            out += "Omnibus correction\t"+method_omni+"\n";
            out += "Gatekeeping\tN/A (two groups)\n\n";
            // Header mit Gruppennamen in Klammern
            out += "Param\tN1 ("+uniq[0]+")\tN2 ("+uniq[1]+")\tMean1 ("+uniq[0]+")\tMean2 ("+uniq[1]+")\tDiff(2-1)\tt\tDF\tp(two-sided)\tsig(p)\n";
            for (p=0; p<14; p++) {
                a = collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[0], p);
                b = collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[1], p);
                n1=a.length; n2=b.length;
                m1=avg(a); m2=avg(b);
                s1=variance(a, true); s2=variance(b, true);
                if (n1<2 || n2<2) { t=0/0; df=0/0; pval=0/0; }
                else { t=(m2-m1)/sqrt(s1/n1+s2/n2); df=welchDF(s1,n1,s2,n2); pval=p_value_t_two_sided(abs(t),df); }
                out += paramNames[p]+"\t"+n1+"\t"+n2+"\t"+d3(m1)+"\t"+d3(m2)+"\t"+d3(m2-m1)+"\t"+d3(t)+"\t"+d3(df)+"\t"+sci(pval)+"\t"+sigStars(pval)+"\n";
            }
            File.saveString(out, outDir+"STATS_ttest (ENG).txt");
            out_de = replace(out, ".", ",");
            File.saveString(out_de, outDir+"STATS_ttest (GER).txt");
            print("\nSaved: "+outDir+"STATS_ttest (ENG).txt");
            print("Saved: "+outDir+"STATS_ttest (GER).txt");
        }

    } else {
        // ===========================================
        // One-way ANOVA + pairwise Welch t-tests
        // ===========================================
        print("Mode: One-way ANOVA (k="+k+" groups)\n");
        pvals_omni = newArray(14);

        print("Param\tk\tN\tDF1\tDF2\tF\tp\tsig(p)\teta^2");
        for (p=0; p<14; p++) {
            Ns = newArray(k);
            Ms = newArray(k);
            SSwithin = 0.0;
            Ntot = 0;

            // gather by group
            for (gi=0; gi<k; gi++) {
                arr = collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gi], p);
                Ns[gi] = arr.length;
                Ms[gi] = avg(arr);
                SSwithin += (arr.length-1) * variance(arr, true);
                Ntot += arr.length;
            }
            grandMean = weightedMean(Ms, Ns);
            SSbetween = 0.0;
            for (gi=0; gi<k; gi++) SSbetween += Ns[gi] * pow(Ms[gi]-grandMean, 2);
            SStotal = SSbetween + SSwithin;

            df1 = k - 1;
            df2 = Ntot - k;
            MSb = SSbetween / df1;
            MSw = SSwithin  / df2;
            F = MSb / MSw;
            pval = p_value_f_right(F, df1, df2);

            if (SStotal>0) eta2 = SSbetween / SStotal; else eta2 = 0;

            pvals_omni[p] = pval;
            print(paramNames[p]+"\t"+k+"\t"+Ntot+"\t"+df1+"\t"+df2+"\t"+d3(F)+"\t"+sci(pval)+"\t"+sigStars(pval)+"\t"+d3(eta2));
        }

        // --------- Omnibus correction (robust: always array) ----------
        adjOmni = newArray(pvals_omni.length);
        for (ii=0; ii<adjOmni.length; ii++) adjOmni[ii] = 0/0;
        doAdjOmni = false;

        if (method_omni=="FDR (BH)") {
            tmpAdjOmni = bh_fdr_nanaware(pvals_omni);
            doAdjOmni = true;
        } else if (method_omni=="Holm") {
            tmpAdjOmni = holm_nanaware(pvals_omni);
            doAdjOmni = true;
        } else {
            tmpAdjOmni = newArray(0); // None
        }
        for (ii=0; ii<tmpAdjOmni.length && ii<adjOmni.length; ii++) adjOmni[ii] = tmpAdjOmni[ii];

        if (doAdjOmni) {
            print("");
            if (method_omni=="FDR (BH)") {
                print("FDR (Benjamini–Hochberg) across the 14 omnibus p-values:");
                print("Param\tp\tq(FDR)\tsig(q)");
                for (p=0; p<14; p++) print(paramNames[p]+"\t"+sci(pvals_omni[p])+"\t"+sci(adjOmni[p])+"\t"+sigStars(adjOmni[p]));
            } else if (method_omni=="Holm") {
                print("Holm (FWER) across the 14 omnibus p-values:");
                print("Param\tp\tpHolm\tsig(pHolm)");
                for (p=0; p<14; p++) print(paramNames[p]+"\t"+sci(pvals_omni[p])+"\t"+sci(adjOmni[p])+"\t"+sigStars(adjOmni[p]));
            }
        }

        // For gatekeeping, decide which p-values to use for the check
        alpha = 0.05;
        useAdjForGate = false;
        if (doAdjOmni) useAdjForGate = true;

        // -------- Pairwise comparisons (Welch t-tests) --------
        print("\nPairwise comparisons (Welch t-tests), parameter-wise:");
        for (p=0; p<14; p++) {
            // Gatekeeping decision
            allowPairs = true;
            if (gatekeepPairs) {
                if (useAdjForGate) {
                    allowPairs = (adjOmni[p] <= alpha);
                } else {
                    allowPairs = (pvals_omni[p] <= alpha);
                }
            }

            if (!allowPairs) {
                print("\n# "+paramNames[p]);
                gateLabel = "raw";
                if (useAdjForGate) gateLabel = "corrected";
                print("Omnibus not significant at alpha=0.05 (" + gateLabel + "); pairwise comparisons skipped.");
                continue;
            }

            hdr = "GroupA\tGroupB\tN1\tN2\tMean1\tMean2\tDiff(2-1)\tt\tDF\tp\tsig(p)";
            if (method_pairs!="None") {
                if (method_pairs=="FDR (BH)") hdr = hdr + "\tq(FDR)\tsig(q)";
                else hdr = hdr + "\tpHolm\tsig(pHolm)";
            }

            print("\n# "+paramNames[p]);
            print(hdr);

            pair_pvals = newArray(0);
            pair_lines = newArray(0);

            for (gi=0; gi<k-1; gi++) {
                for (gj=gi+1; gj<k; gj++) {
                    a = collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gi], p);
                    b = collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gj], p);
                    n1=a.length; n2=b.length;
                    m1=avg(a); m2=avg(b);
                    s1=variance(a, true); s2=variance(b, true);

                    if (n1<2 || n2<2) { t=0/0; df=0/0; pval=0/0; }
                    else { t=(m2-m1)/sqrt(s1/n1 + s2/n2); df=welchDF(s1,n1,s2,n2); pval=p_value_t_two_sided(abs(t), df); }

                    baseLine = uniq[gi]+"\t"+uniq[gj]+"\t"+n1+"\t"+n2+"\t"+d3(m1)+"\t"+d3(m2)+"\t"+d3(m2-m1)+"\t"+d3(t)+"\t"+d3(df)+"\t"+sci(pval)+"\t"+sigStars(pval);
                    if (method_pairs=="None") {
                        print(baseLine);
                    } else {
                        pair_lines = appendStr(pair_lines, baseLine); // adjusted appended later
                    }
                    pair_pvals = appendNum(pair_pvals, pval);
                }
            }

            if (method_pairs!="None") {
                // Robust adjusted p-values array
                adjPairs = newArray(pair_pvals.length);
                for (idxPair=0; idxPair<adjPairs.length; idxPair++) adjPairs[idxPair] = 0/0;

                if (method_pairs=="FDR (BH)") {
                    tmpAdj = bh_fdr_nanaware(pair_pvals);
                } else {
                    tmpAdj = holm_nanaware(pair_pvals);
                }
                // copy safely
                for (idxPair=0; idxPair<tmpAdj.length && idxPair<adjPairs.length; idxPair++) adjPairs[idxPair] = tmpAdj[idxPair];

                for (idxPair=0; idxPair<pair_lines.length; idxPair++) {
                    print(pair_lines[idxPair] + "\t" + sci(adjPairs[idxPair]) + "\t" + sigStars(adjPairs[idxPair]));
                }
            }
        }

        // ------- Save to file -------
        if (outDir!="") {
            out = "Mode\tOne-way ANOVA (k="+k+")\n";
            out += "Groups\t"+joinStrings(uniq, ", ")+"\n";
            out += "Omnibus correction\t"+method_omni+"\n";
            out += "Pairwise correction\t"+method_pairs+"\n";
            gateTxtOut = "OFF";
            if (gatekeepPairs) gateTxtOut = "ON (alpha=0.05)";
            out += "Gatekeeping\t"+gateTxtOut+"\n\n";
            out += "Param\tk\tN\tDF1\tDF2\tF\tp\tsig(p)\teta^2\n";
            for (p=0; p<14; p++) {
                Ns = newArray(k);
                Ms = newArray(k);
                SSwithin = 0.0;
                Ntot = 0;
                for (gi=0; gi<k; gi++) {
                    arr = collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gi], p);
                    Ns[gi] = arr.length;
                    Ms[gi] = avg(arr);
                    SSwithin += (arr.length-1) * variance(arr, true);
                    Ntot += arr.length;
                }
                grandMean = weightedMean(Ms, Ns);
                SSbetween = 0.0;
                for (gi=0; gi<k; gi++) SSbetween += Ns[gi] * pow(Ms[gi]-grandMean, 2);
                SStotal = SSbetween + SSwithin;

                df1 = k - 1;
                df2 = Ntot - k;
                MSb = SSbetween / df1;
                MSw = SSwithin  / df2;
                F = MSb / MSw;
                pval = p_value_f_right(F, df1, df2);
                if (SStotal>0) eta2 = SSbetween / SStotal; else eta2 = 0;
                out += paramNames[p]+"\t"+k+"\t"+Ntot+"\t"+df1+"\t"+df2+"\t"+d3(F)+"\t"+sci(pval)+"\t"+sigStars(pval)+"\t"+d3(eta2)+"\n";
            }

            if (doAdjOmni) {
                if (method_omni=="FDR (BH)") {
                    out += "\nFDR (Benjamini–Hochberg) across 14 omnibus p-values\nParam\tp\tq(FDR)\nsig(q)\n";
                    for (p=0; p<14; p++) out += paramNames[p]+"\t"+sci(pvals_omni[p])+"\t"+sci(adjOmni[p])+"\t"+sigStars(adjOmni[p])+"\n";
                } else if (method_omni=="Holm") {
                    out += "\nHolm across 14 omnibus p-values\nParam\tp\tpHolm\tsig(pHolm)\n";
                    for (p=0; p<14; p++) out += paramNames[p]+"\t"+sci(pvals_omni[p])+"\t"+sci(adjOmni[p])+"\t"+sigStars(adjOmni[p])+"\n";
                }
            }

            // Pairwise section with gatekeeping
            out += "\nPairwise comparisons (Welch t-tests), parameter-wise\n";
            alpha = 0.05;
            useAdjForGate = false;
            if (doAdjOmni) useAdjForGate = true;

            for (p=0; p<14; p++) {
                allowPairs = true;
                if (gatekeepPairs) {
                    if (useAdjForGate) allowPairs = (adjOmni[p] <= alpha);
                    else allowPairs = (pvals_omni[p] <= alpha);
                }

                out += "\n# "+paramNames[p]+"\n";
                if (!allowPairs) {
                    gateLabel = "raw";
                    if (useAdjForGate) gateLabel = "corrected";
                    out += "Omnibus not significant at alpha=0.05 (" + gateLabel + "); pairwise comparisons skipped.\n";
                    continue;
                }

                hdr = "GroupA\tGroupB\tN1\tN2\tMean1\tMean2\tDiff(2-1)\tt\tDF\tp\tsig(p)";
                if (method_pairs!="None") {
                    if (method_pairs=="FDR (BH)") hdr = hdr + "\tq(FDR)\tsig(q)";
                    else hdr = hdr + "\tpHolm\tsig(pHolm)";
                }
                out += hdr + "\n";

                pair_pvals = newArray(0);
                pair_lines = newArray(0);

                for (gi=0; gi<k-1; gi++) {
                    for (gj=gi+1; gj<k; gj++) {
                        a = collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gi], p);
                        b = collectParamForGroup(data, groups, uniq[gj], p);
                        n1=a.length; n2=b.length;
                        m1=avg(a); m2=avg(b);
                        s1=variance(a, true); s2=variance(b, true);
                        if (n1<2 || n2<2) { t=0/0; df=0/0; pval=0/0; }
                        else { t=(m2-m1)/sqrt(s1/n1 + s2/n2); df=welchDF(s1,n1,s2,n2); pval=p_value_t_two_sided(abs(t), df); }
                        baseLine = uniq[gi]+"\t"+uniq[gj]+"\t"+n1+"\t"+n2+"\t"+d3(m1)+"\t"+d3(m2)+"\t"+d3(m2-m1)+"\t"+d3(t)+"\t"+d3(df)+"\t"+sci(pval)+"\t"+sigStars(pval);
                        if (method_pairs=="None") out += baseLine + "\n";
                        else pair_lines = appendStr(pair_lines, baseLine);
                        pair_pvals = appendNum(pair_pvals, pval);
                    }
                }
                if (method_pairs!="None") {
                    // Robust adjusted p-values array
                    adjPairs = newArray(pair_pvals.length);
                    for (idxPair=0; idxPair<adjPairs.length; idxPair++) adjPairs[idxPair] = 0/0;

                    if (method_pairs=="FDR (BH)") {
                        tmpAdj = bh_fdr_nanaware(pair_pvals);
                    } else {
                        tmpAdj = holm_nanaware(pair_pvals);
                    }
                    for (idxPair=0; idxPair<tmpAdj.length && idxPair<adjPairs.length; idxPair++) adjPairs[idxPair] = tmpAdj[idxPair];

                    for (idxPair=0; idxPair<pair_lines.length; idxPair++) {
                        out += pair_lines[idxPair] + "\t" + sci(adjPairs[idxPair]) + "\t" + sigStars(adjPairs[idxPair]) + "\n";
                    }
                }
            }

            File.saveString(out, outDir+"STATS_anova (ENG).txt");
            out_de = replace(out, ".", ",");
            File.saveString(out_de, outDir+"STATS_anova (GER).txt");
            print("\nSaved: "+outDir+"STATS_anova (ENG).txt");
            print("Saved: "+outDir+"STATS_anova (GER).txt");
        }
    }

    print("\nFinished.");
}

// =============================
// Helpers: parsing & collecting
// =============================
function uniqueStrings(arr) {
    u = newArray(0);
    for (i=0; i<arr.length; i++) {
        s = arr[i];
        found = false;
        for (j=0; j<u.length; j++) if (u[j]==s) {found=true; break;}
        if (!found) u = appendStr(u, s);
    }
    return u;
}
function appendStr(a, s) { return Array.concat(a, s); }
function appendNum(a, v) { return Array.concat(a, v); }
function joinStrings(a, sep) {
    if (a.length==0) return "";
    out = a[0];
    for (i=1; i<a.length; i++) out += sep + a[i];
    return out;
}
function joinNumbers(a, sep) {
    if (a.length==0) return "";
    out = ""+a[0];
    for (i=1; i<a.length; i++) out += sep + a[i];
    return out;
}
function collectParamForGroup(data, groups, g, pIndex) {
    out = newArray(0);
    for (i=0; i<data.length; i++) {
        if (groups[i]!=g) continue;
        fields = split(data[i], "\t");
        v = parseFloat(fields[pIndex]);
        if (v==v) out = Array.concat(out, v); // skip NaN
    }
    return out;
}

// =============================
// Basic stats
// =============================
function avg(a) {
    if (a.length==0) return 0/0;
    s=0; for (i=0;i<a.length;i++) s+=a[i];
    return s/a.length;
}
function variance(a, unbiased) {
    n=a.length; if (n<2) return 0/0;
    m=avg(a);
    ss=0; for (i=0;i<n;i++) ss+= (a[i]-m)*(a[i]-m);
    denom = n;
    if (unbiased) denom = n-1;
    return ss/denom;
}
function weightedMean(means, Ns) {
    num=0; den=0;
    for (i=0;i<means.length;i++) { num += means[i]*Ns[i]; den += Ns[i]; }
    if (den>0) return num/den;
    return 0/0;
}
function welchDF(s1,n1,s2,n2) {
    a = s1/n1 + s2/n2;
    b = (s1*s1)/(n1*n1*(n1-1)) + (s2*s2)/(n2*n2*(n2-1));
    return a*a / b;
}

// =============================
// p-values via incomplete beta
// =============================
function p_value_t_two_sided(t, df) {
    x = df / (df + t*t);
    return betai(0.5*df, 0.5, x);
}
function p_value_f_right(F, df1, df2) {
    x = df2 / (df2 + df1*F);
    return betai(0.5*df2, 0.5*df1, x);
}

// Regularized incomplete beta I_x(a,b)
function betai(a,b,x) {
    if (x<=0) return 0;
    if (x>=1) return 1;
    bt = exp(gammln(a+b) - gammln(a) - gammln(b) + a*log(x) + b*log(1.0 - x));
    if (x < (a+1.0)/(a+b+2.0)) return bt*betacf(a,b,x)/a;
    else return 1.0 - bt*betacf(b,a,1.0-x)/b;
}
function betacf(a,b,x) {
    MAXIT=200;
    EPS=3.0e-7;
    FPMIN=1.0e-30;
    qab=a+b; qap=a+1.0; qam=a-1.0;
    c=1.0;
    d=1.0 - qab*x/qap; if (abs(d)<FPMIN) d=FPMIN;
    d=1.0/d;
    h=d;
    for (m=1; m<=MAXIT; m++) {
        m2=2*m;
        aa = m*(b-m)*x/((qam+m2)*(a+m2));
        d = 1.0 + aa*d; if (abs(d)<FPMIN) d=FPMIN; d=1.0/d;
        c = 1.0 + aa/c; if (abs(c)<FPMIN) c=FPMIN;
        h *= d*c;
        aa = -(a+m)*(qab+m)*x/((a+m2)*(qap+m2));
        d = 1.0 + aa*d; if (abs(d)<FPMIN) d=FPMIN; d=1.0/d;
        c = 1.0 + aa/c; if (abs(c)<FPMIN) c=FPMIN;
        del = d*c;
        h *= del;
        if (abs(del-1.0) < EPS) break;
    }
    return h;
}
function gammln(xx) {
    cof = newArray(76.18009172947146,-86.50532032941677,24.01409824083091,
                   -1.231739572450155,0.001208650973866179,-5.395239384953e-6);
    x=xx; y=xx;
    tmp = x + 5.5;
    tmp -= (x + 0.5)*log(tmp);
    ser = 1.000000000190015;
    for (j=0; j<6; j++) { y += 1.0; ser += cof[j]/y; }
    return -tmp + log(2.5066282746310005*ser/x);
}

// =============================
// Multiple testing: BH-FDR & Holm
// =============================
function bh_fdr(pvals) {
    m = pvals.length;
    idx = newArray(m);
    for (i=0;i<m;i++) idx[i]=i;
    for (i=0;i<m-1;i++) {
        imin=i;
        for (j=i+1;j<m;j++) if (pvals[idx[j]] < pvals[idx[imin]]) imin=j;
        tmp=idx[i]; idx[i]=idx[imin]; idx[imin]=tmp;
    }
    q = newArray(m);
    minQ = 1.0;
    for (r=m-1; r>=0; r--) {
        i = idx[r];
        val = pvals[i]*m/(r+1);
        if (val<minQ) minQ=val;
        if (minQ<1.0) q[i]=minQ; else q[i]=1.0;
    }
    return q;
}
function bh_fdr_nanaware(pvals) {
    idxValid = newArray(0);
    pvValid  = newArray(0);
    for (i=0;i<pvals.length;i++) if (pvals[i]==pvals[i]) {
        idxValid = Array.concat(idxValid, i);
        pvValid  = Array.concat(pvValid, pvals[i]);
    }
    out = newArray(pvals.length);
    for (i=0;i<out.length;i++) out[i]=0/0;
    if (pvValid.length==0) return out;
    adjValid = bh_fdr(pvValid);
    for (k2=0;k2<idxValid.length;k2++) out[idxValid[k2]] = adjValid[k2];
    return out;
}
function holm(pvals) {
    m = pvals.length;
    idx = newArray(m);
    for (i=0;i<m;i++) idx[i]=i;
    for (i=0;i<m-1;i++) {
        imin=i;
        for (j=i+1;j<m;j++) if (pvals[idx[j]] < pvals[idx[imin]]) imin=j;
        tmp=idx[i]; idx[i]=idx[imin]; idx[imin]=tmp;
    }
    padj_sorted = newArray(m);
    for (r=0; r<m; r++) {
        i = idx[r];
        val = pvals[i] * (m - r);
