        if (val>1.0) val = 1.0;
        padj_sorted[r] = val;
    }
    for (r=1; r<m; r++) {
        if (padj_sorted[r] < padj_sorted[r-1]) padj_sorted[r] = padj_sorted[r-1];
    }
    padj = newArray(m);
    for (r=0; r<m; r++) {
        i = idx[r];
        padj[i] = padj_sorted[r];
    }
    return padj;
}
function holm_nanaware(pvals) {
    idxValid = newArray(0);
    pvValid  = newArray(0);
    for (i=0;i<pvals.length;i++) if (pvals[i]==pvals[i]) {
        idxValid = Array.concat(idxValid, i);
        pvValid  = Array.concat(pvValid, pvals[i]);
    }
    out = newArray(pvals.length);
    for (i=0;i<out.length;i++) out[i]=0/0;
    if (pvValid.length==0) return out;
    adjValid = holm(pvValid);
    for (k2=0;k2<idxValid.length;k2++) out[idxValid[k2]] = adjValid[k2];
    return out;
}

// Unified adjuster (keine Pflichtnutzung; bleibt verfügbar)
function adjustByMethod(pvals, method) {
    if (method=="None") return newArray(0);
    if (method=="FDR (BH)") return bh_fdr_nanaware(pvals);
    if (method=="Holm") return holm_nanaware(pvals);
    return newArray(0);
}

// =============================
// Formatting & stars
// =============================
function d3(v) { return ""+round(v*1000)/1000; }
function sci(v) {
    if (v!=v) return "NA";
    if (v==0) return "0";
    e = floor(log(abs(v))/log(10));
    m = v / pow(10,e);
    return ""+d3(m)+"e"+e;
}
// Prism-style significance stars
function sigStars(p) {
    if (p!=p) return "NA";        // NaN
    if (p <= 0.0001) return "****";
    if (p <= 0.001)  return "***";
    if (p <= 0.01)   return "**";
    if (p <= 0.05)   return "*";
    return "ns";
}

}


if (option=="13. Comparison & visualization (single cells)") {	

// ============================================================
// QP ADD-ON (SELF-CONTAINED, SAFE TO APPEND / REPLACE)
// Quick bar-plots from STATS_mannwhitney OR STATS_kruskalwallis
//
// NEW:
// - Means + SD are always computed from the ANOVA_Ready LONG file
// - Stats file is used only for significance stars / brackets
// - User chooses BASELINE group (=100%), which is moved to the LEFT
// - Supports 2 groups (MW) and 3+ groups (KW pairwise stars)
//
// Output PNG:
//   _BASELINE_<group>_<MW/KW>_TIME_GRID_3x5.png
// ============================================================


// -----------------------------
// ENTRY: call at very end
// -----------------------------
QP_quickPlotsWizard();

function QP_quickPlotsWizard() {

    Dialog.create("Quick Visualization (MW / KW)");
    Dialog.addCheckbox("Create bar plot grid (means ± SD) + Prism stars now?", true);
    Dialog.show();
    if (!Dialog.getCheckbox()) return;

    QP_statsPath = File.openDialog("Select STATS_mannwhitney... or STATS_kruskalwallis... LONG (ENG).txt");
    if (QP_statsPath=="") return;

    QP_makeQuickBarPlots_fromStats(QP_statsPath);
}


// ============================================================
// CORE
// ============================================================
function QP_makeQuickBarPlots_fromStats(QP_statsPath) {

    QP_statsTxt = File.openAsString(QP_statsPath);
    if (QP_statsTxt=="") exit("Stats file is empty.");

    QP_statsTxt = replace(QP_statsTxt, "\r", "");
    QP_mode = QP_detectStatsMode(QP_statsTxt, QP_statsPath);
    if (QP_mode=="") exit("Could not detect stats mode. Expected Mann-Whitney or Kruskal-Wallis.");

    // normalize stats path first
    QP_statsPath = replace(QP_statsPath, "\\", "/");
    QP_outDir = QP_dirOf(QP_statsPath);

    // extract LONG path from stats file
    QP_longPath = QP_extractInputPathFromStats(QP_statsTxt);
    if (QP_longPath=="") {
        QP_longPath = File.openDialog("Could not find Input path in stats file.\nPlease select the matching ANOVA_Ready_Data ... LONG file manually.");
        if (QP_longPath=="") exit("Aborted.");
    }
    QP_longPath = replace(QP_longPath, "\\", "/");

    // resolve LONG path robustly
    QP_longPath = QP_resolveLongPath(QP_statsPath, QP_longPath);

    QP_base = QP_baseNameNoExt(QP_statsPath);
    QP_base = QP_cleanStatsBase(QP_base);

    // groups from LONG
    QP_groups = QP_getGroupsFromLong(QP_longPath);
    if (lengthOf(QP_groups) < 2)
        exit("LONG file must contain at least 2 groups in 'Group_Assignment'.");

    // baseline selection
    Dialog.create("Bar Order / Baseline");
    Dialog.addMessage("Detected groups from LONG file:\n" + QP_joinArray(QP_groups, ", ") + "\n\nSelect the BASELINE group.\nThis group will be LEFT and shown as 100%.");
    Dialog.addChoice("LEFT bar / baseline (=100%):", QP_groups, QP_groups[0]);
    Dialog.show();
    QP_baseline = Dialog.getChoice();

    QP_groupsOrdered = QP_reorderGroupsWithBaseline(QP_groups, QP_baseline);
    QP_nGroups = lengthOf(QP_groupsOrdered);

    // labels
    Dialog.create("Value Labels");
    Dialog.addCheckbox("Show value labels (absolute + %)?", true);
    Dialog.show();
    QP_showValueLabels = Dialog.getCheckbox();
    if (QP_showValueLabels) QP_showValueLabels = 1;
    else QP_showValueLabels = 0;

    // parameters
    QP_TimeParams = newArray(
        "PeakTimes10% mean [s]",   "Systoles10% mean [s]",   "Diastoles10% mean [s]",
        "PeakTimesUser mean [s]",  "SystolesUser mean [s]",  "DiastolesUser mean [s]",
        "PeakTimes50% mean [s]",   "Systoles50% mean [s]",   "Diastoles50% mean [s]",
        "PeakTimes90% mean [s]",   "Systoles90% mean [s]",   "Diastoles90% mean [s]"
    );

    QP_TimeLabels = newArray(
        "PeakTime Thr10%", "Syst Thr10%", "Diast Thr10%",
        "PeakTime UserThr","Syst UserThr","Diast UserThr",
        "PeakTime 50%", "Syst Thr50%", "Diast Thr50%",
        "PeakTime 90%", "Syst Thr90%", "Diast Thr90%"
    );

    QP_AmpParam  = "Amplitudes mean [au]";
    QP_BeatParam = "BeatTimes mean [s]";
    QP_FreqParam = "Frequencies mean [1/s]";

    QP_GridParams = QP_TimeParams;
    QP_GridParams = Array.concat(QP_GridParams, QP_AmpParam);
    QP_GridParams = Array.concat(QP_GridParams, QP_BeatParam);
    QP_GridParams = Array.concat(QP_GridParams, QP_FreqParam);

    QP_GridLabels = QP_TimeLabels;
    QP_GridLabels = Array.concat(QP_GridLabels, "Amplitude");
    QP_GridLabels = Array.concat(QP_GridLabels, "BeatTimes");
    QP_GridLabels = Array.concat(QP_GridLabels, "Frequencies");

    QP_nParams = lengthOf(QP_GridParams);

    // flattened matrices: [paramIndex * nGroups + groupIndex]
    QP_meansFlat = newArray(QP_nParams * QP_nGroups);
    QP_sdsFlat   = newArray(QP_nParams * QP_nGroups);
    QP_okFlags   = newArray(QP_nParams);

    for (QP_pi=0; QP_pi<QP_nParams; QP_pi++) {
        QP_res = QP_meanSdFromLong_groups(QP_longPath, QP_groupsOrdered, QP_GridParams[QP_pi]);
        QP_okFlags[QP_pi] = QP_res[0];

        for (QP_gi=0; QP_gi<QP_nGroups; QP_gi++) {
            QP_meansFlat[QP_pi*QP_nGroups + QP_gi] = QP_res[1 + QP_gi];
            QP_sdsFlat[QP_pi*QP_nGroups + QP_gi]   = QP_res[1 + QP_nGroups + QP_gi];
        }
    }

    QP_drawTimeGrid_generic(
        QP_outDir, QP_base, QP_mode, QP_baseline, QP_groupsOrdered,
        QP_GridLabels, QP_GridParams, QP_meansFlat, QP_sdsFlat, QP_okFlags,
        QP_statsTxt, QP_showValueLabels
    );

    print("Quick plots saved to: " + QP_outDir);
}


// ============================================================
// DRAWING
// ============================================================
function QP_drawTimeGrid_generic(QP_outDir, QP_base, QP_mode, QP_baseline, QP_groupsOrdered,
                                 QP_labels, QP_params, QP_meansFlat, QP_sdsFlat, QP_okFlags,
                                 QP_statsTxt, QP_showLabels) {

    QP_W = 1400;
    QP_H = 1300;

    QP_title = "QP_TIME_GRID_3x5";
    newImage(QP_title, "RGB white", QP_W, QP_H, 1);

    // colors: baseline first = warm red, then blue/green/violet/ochre...
    QP_cR = newArray(200,  70,  80, 150, 220, 100);
    QP_cG = newArray( 90, 110, 170, 100, 150, 120);
    QP_cB = newArray( 90, 200,  90, 210,  70, 180);

    // header
    setColor(0,0,0);
    setFont("SansSerif", 26, "antialiased");
    drawString("Parameters (means ± SD)", 30, 35);

    // legend
    setFont("SansSerif", 24, "antialiased");
    QP_drawLegendMulti(40, 40, QP_groupsOrdered, QP_cR, QP_cG, QP_cB);

    // grid geometry
    QP_gridX = 30;
    QP_gridY = 95;
    QP_gridW = QP_W - 60;
    QP_gridH = QP_H - 130;

    QP_cols = 3;
    QP_rows = 5;
    QP_cellW = QP_gridW / QP_cols;
    QP_cellH = QP_gridH / QP_rows;

    // grid lines
    setColor(220,220,220);
    setLineWidth(1);
    for (QP_cc=0; QP_cc<=QP_cols; QP_cc++) {
        QP_x = QP_gridX + QP_cc*QP_cellW;
        makeLine(QP_x, QP_gridY, QP_x, QP_gridY+QP_gridH);
        run("Draw");
    }
    for (QP_rr=0; QP_rr<=QP_rows; QP_rr++) {
        QP_y = QP_gridY + QP_rr*QP_cellH;
        makeLine(QP_gridX, QP_y, QP_gridX+QP_gridW, QP_y);
        run("Draw");
    }

    QP_nGroups = lengthOf(QP_groupsOrdered);

    // fill cells
    QP_idx = 0;
    for (QP_rr=0; QP_rr<QP_rows; QP_rr++) {
        for (QP_cc=0; QP_cc<QP_cols; QP_cc++) {

            QP_cellX = QP_gridX + QP_cc*QP_cellW;
            QP_cellY = QP_gridY + QP_rr*QP_cellH;

            if (QP_idx < lengthOf(QP_labels) && QP_okFlags[QP_idx]==1) {

                QP_meansOne = newArray(QP_nGroups);
                QP_sdsOne   = newArray(QP_nGroups);

                for (QP_gi=0; QP_gi<QP_nGroups; QP_gi++) {
                    QP_meansOne[QP_gi] = QP_meansFlat[QP_idx*QP_nGroups + QP_gi];
                    QP_sdsOne[QP_gi]   = QP_sdsFlat[QP_idx*QP_nGroups + QP_gi];
                }

                if (QP_mode=="MW")
                    QP_sigPairs = QP_getSigPairsForParam_MW(QP_statsTxt, QP_params[QP_idx], QP_groupsOrdered);
                else
                    QP_sigPairs = QP_getSigPairsForParam_KW(QP_statsTxt, QP_params[QP_idx], QP_groupsOrdered);

                QP_unit = " s";
                QP_absDigits = 4;
                QP_pctDigits = 1;

                if (QP_idx==12) {
                    QP_unit = " au";
                    QP_absDigits = 3;
                } else if (QP_idx==14) {
                    QP_unit = " 1/s";
                    QP_absDigits = 4;
                }

                QP_drawMiniBars(
                    QP_cellX, QP_cellY, QP_cellW, QP_cellH,
                    QP_labels[QP_idx],
                    QP_groupsOrdered, QP_meansOne, QP_sdsOne, QP_sigPairs,
                    QP_cR, QP_cG, QP_cB,
                    QP_showLabels, QP_unit, QP_absDigits, QP_pctDigits
                );
            }

            QP_idx++;
        }
    }

    QP_baseTag = QP_safeToken(QP_baseline);
    saveAs("PNG", QP_outDir + QP_base + "_BASELINE_" + QP_baseTag + "_" + QP_mode + "_TIME_GRID_3x5.png");
    close();
}


function QP_drawLegendBox(QP_x, QP_y, QP_r,QP_g,QP_b, QP_text) {

    QP_yShift = 8;
    QP_box = 18;
    QP_y2  = QP_y + QP_yShift;

    setColor(QP_r,QP_g,QP_b);
    makeRectangle(QP_x, QP_y2, QP_box, QP_box);
    run("Fill");

    setColor(0,0,0);
    makeRectangle(QP_x, QP_y2, QP_box, QP_box);
    run("Draw");

    drawString(QP_text, QP_x + QP_box + 10, QP_y2 + QP_box + 5);
}

function QP_drawLegendMulti(QP_x, QP_y, QP_groupNames, QP_cR, QP_cG, QP_cB) {
    QP_dx = 230;
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_groupNames); QP_i++) {
        QP_drawLegendBox(
            QP_x + QP_i*QP_dx, QP_y,
            QP_cR[QP_i % lengthOf(QP_cR)],
            QP_cG[QP_i % lengthOf(QP_cG)],
            QP_cB[QP_i % lengthOf(QP_cB)],
            QP_groupNames[QP_i]
        );
    }
}


// Generic mini bar plot: n bars + upward SD + multiple Prism-like brackets + abs/% labels
function QP_drawMiniBars(QP_cellX, QP_cellY, QP_cellW, QP_cellH,
                         QP_label,
                         QP_groupNames, QP_means, QP_sds, QP_sigPairs,
                         QP_cR, QP_cG, QP_cB,
                         QP_showLabels, QP_unitSuffix, QP_absDigits, QP_pctDigits) {

    QP_n = lengthOf(QP_groupNames);

    // margins
    QP_L = 40; QP_R = 14; QP_T = 30; QP_B = 34;

    QP_plotX = QP_cellX + QP_L;
    QP_plotY = QP_cellY + QP_T;
    QP_plotW = QP_cellW - QP_L - QP_R;
    QP_plotH = QP_cellH - QP_T - QP_B;
    QP_y0 = QP_plotY + QP_plotH;

    // sanitize + max
    QP_vmax = 0;
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<QP_n; QP_i++) {
        if (QP_sds[QP_i] != QP_sds[QP_i]) QP_sds[QP_i] = 0;
        if (QP_means[QP_i] != QP_means[QP_i]) QP_means[QP_i] = 0;
        if (QP_means[QP_i] < 0) QP_means[QP_i] = 0;
        if (QP_means[QP_i] + QP_sds[QP_i] > QP_vmax) QP_vmax = QP_means[QP_i] + QP_sds[QP_i];
    }
    if (QP_vmax <= 0) QP_vmax = 1;

    QP_sigCount = QP_countSignificantPairs(QP_sigPairs);
    QP_yMax = QP_vmax * (1.18 + 0.12*QP_sigCount);
    if (QP_yMax <= 0) QP_yMax = 1;

    // axis
    setColor(0,0,0);
    setLineWidth(2);
    makeLine(QP_plotX, QP_y0, QP_plotX+QP_plotW, QP_y0);
    run("Draw");

    // label
    setFont("SansSerif", 22, "antialiased");
    drawString(QP_label, QP_cellX + 8, QP_cellY + 28);

    // x positions
    QP_xs = newArray(QP_n);
    QP_barW = QP_plotW / (QP_n * 3.2);
    if (QP_barW > 42) QP_barW = 42;
    if (QP_barW < 12) QP_barW = 12;

    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<QP_n; QP_i++) {
        QP_xs[QP_i] = QP_plotX + QP_plotW * (QP_i + 1) / (QP_n + 1);
    }

    // bars + SD
    setLineWidth(2);
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<QP_n; QP_i++) {

        QP_h = (QP_means[QP_i] / QP_yMax) * QP_plotH;
        QP_y = QP_y0 - QP_h;

        setColor(
            QP_cR[QP_i % lengthOf(QP_cR)],
            QP_cG[QP_i % lengthOf(QP_cG)],
            QP_cB[QP_i % lengthOf(QP_cB)]
        );
        makeRectangle(QP_xs[QP_i] - QP_barW/2, QP_y, QP_barW, QP_h);
        run("Fill");

        setColor(0,0,0);
        makeRectangle(QP_xs[QP_i] - QP_barW/2, QP_y, QP_barW, QP_h);
        run("Draw");

        QP_sdH = (QP_sds[QP_i] / QP_yMax) * QP_plotH;
        QP_wTop = QP_y - QP_sdH;

        makeLine(QP_xs[QP_i], QP_y, QP_xs[QP_i], QP_wTop);
        run("Draw");
        makeLine(QP_xs[QP_i]-8, QP_wTop, QP_xs[QP_i]+8, QP_wTop);
        run("Draw");
    }

    // significance brackets
    if (lengthOf(QP_sigPairs) > 0 && QP_sigPairs[0] > 0) {

        QP_tick = 8;
        QP_drawn = 0;

        for (QP_pi=0; QP_pi<QP_sigPairs[0]; QP_pi++) {

            QP_pos = 1 + 3*QP_pi;
            QP_i1 = round(QP_sigPairs[QP_pos]);
            QP_i2 = round(QP_sigPairs[QP_pos+1]);
            QP_pv = QP_sigPairs[QP_pos+2];

            QP_stars = QP_starsOnly(QP_pv);
            if (QP_stars=="") continue;

            if (QP_i1 > QP_i2) {
                QP_tmp = QP_i1;
                QP_i1 = QP_i2;
                QP_i2 = QP_tmp;
            }

            QP_yStarVal = QP_vmax * (1.06 + 0.12*QP_drawn);
            QP_yStar = QP_y0 - (QP_yStarVal / QP_yMax) * QP_plotH;

            setColor(0,0,0);
            setLineWidth(2);

            makeLine(QP_xs[QP_i1], QP_yStar+QP_tick, QP_xs[QP_i1], QP_yStar);
            run("Draw");
            makeLine(QP_xs[QP_i2], QP_yStar+QP_tick, QP_xs[QP_i2], QP_yStar);
            run("Draw");
            makeLine(QP_xs[QP_i1], QP_yStar, QP_xs[QP_i2], QP_yStar);
            run("Draw");

            setFont("SansSerif", 30, "antialiased");
            QP_xMid = (QP_xs[QP_i1] + QP_xs[QP_i2]) / 2.0;
            QP_wApprox = QP_textWidthApprox(QP_stars, 16);
            drawString(QP_stars, QP_xMid - QP_wApprox/2.0, QP_yStar - 4);

            QP_drawn++;
        }
    }

    // labels (baseline = first group = 100%)
    if (QP_showLabels==1) {

        QP_baseMean = QP_means[0];
        setColor(0,0,0);
        setFont("SansSerif", 18, "antialiased");

        for (QP_i=0; QP_i<QP_n; QP_i++) {

            if (QP_i==0) QP_pct = 100;
            else {
                QP_pct = 0/0;
                if (QP_baseMean > 0) QP_pct = (QP_means[QP_i] / QP_baseMean) * 100;
            }

            QP_absS = QP_fmtAbs(QP_means[QP_i], QP_unitSuffix, QP_absDigits);
            QP_pctS = QP_fmtPct(QP_pct, QP_pctDigits);

            QP_yAbs = QP_yTopOfMean(QP_means[QP_i], QP_y0, QP_plotH, QP_yMax) + 14;
            if (QP_yAbs < QP_plotY + 22) QP_yAbs = QP_plotY + 22;
            QP_yPct = QP_yAbs + 18;

            if (QP_yPct > QP_y0 - 6) {
                QP_shift = QP_yPct - (QP_y0 - 6);
                QP_yAbs = QP_yAbs - QP_shift;
                QP_yPct = QP_yPct - QP_shift;
            }

            QP_wA = QP_textWidthApprox(QP_absS, 7);
            QP_wP = QP_textWidthApprox(QP_pctS, 7);
            QP_wM = QP_max2(QP_wA, QP_wP);

            drawString(QP_absS, QP_xs[QP_i] - QP_wM/2, QP_yAbs);
            drawString(QP_pctS, QP_xs[QP_i] - QP_wM/2, QP_yPct);
        }
    }
}


// ============================================================
// SIGNIFICANCE PARSING
// ============================================================

// MW -> [count, idx1, idx2, p]
function QP_getSigPairsForParam_MW(QP_statsTxt, QP_paramName, QP_groupsOrdered) {

    QP_lines = split(QP_statsTxt, "\n");
    QP_g1 = "";
    QP_g2 = "";
    QP_inMain = 0;

    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_lines); QP_i++) {
        QP_L = QP_lines[QP_i];

        if (startsWith(QP_L, "Groups\t")) {
            QP_parts = split(QP_L, "\t");
            if (lengthOf(QP_parts)>1) {
                QP_vs = QP_parts[1];
                QP_vsParts = split(QP_vs, " vs ");
                if (lengthOf(QP_vsParts)>=2) {
                    QP_g1 = QP_vsParts[0];
                    QP_g2 = QP_vsParts[1];
                }
            }
        }

        if (startsWith(QP_L, "Param\t")) {
            QP_inMain = 1;
            continue;
        }

        if (QP_inMain==1) {
            if (startsWith(QP_L, "Adjusted p-values")) break;
            if (QP_L=="") continue;

            QP_parts = split(QP_L, "\t");
            if (lengthOf(QP_parts) < 9) continue;

            if (QP_parts[0] == QP_paramName) {

                QP_p = QP_parseFloatSafe(QP_parts[8]);
                QP_i1 = QP_findStringIndex(QP_groupsOrdered, QP_g1);
                QP_i2 = QP_findStringIndex(QP_groupsOrdered, QP_g2);

                if (QP_i1 < 0 || QP_i2 < 0) return newArray(0);
                return newArray(1, QP_i1, QP_i2, QP_p);
            }
        }
    }

    return newArray(0);
}


// KW -> [count, idx1, idx2, q_or_p, idx1, idx2, q_or_p, ...]
function QP_getSigPairsForParam_KW(QP_statsTxt, QP_paramName, QP_groupsOrdered) {

    QP_lines = split(QP_statsTxt, "\n");
    QP_inBlock = 0;
    QP_foundHeader = 0;
    QP_out = newArray(0);

    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_lines); QP_i++) {
        QP_L = QP_lines[QP_i];

        if (startsWith(QP_L, "# ")) {
            if (QP_inBlock==1) break;

            QP_blockName = substring(QP_L, 2);
            if (QP_blockName == QP_paramName) {
                QP_inBlock = 1;
                QP_foundHeader = 0;
                continue;
            }
        }

        if (QP_inBlock==1) {

            if (QP_L=="") continue;

            if (QP_foundHeader==0) {
                if (startsWith(QP_L, "GroupA\tGroupB\t")) {
                    QP_foundHeader = 1;
                }
                continue;
            }

            if (startsWith(QP_L, "# ")) break;

            QP_parts = split(QP_L, "\t");
            if (lengthOf(QP_parts) < 10) continue;

            QP_g1 = QP_parts[0];
            QP_g2 = QP_parts[1];

            QP_p = QP_parseFloatSafe(QP_parts[9]);
            QP_q = 0/0;
            if (lengthOf(QP_parts) > 11) QP_q = QP_parseFloatSafe(QP_parts[11]);

            if (QP_q == QP_q) QP_use = QP_q;
            else QP_use = QP_p;

            QP_i1 = QP_findStringIndex(QP_groupsOrdered, QP_g1);
            QP_i2 = QP_findStringIndex(QP_groupsOrdered, QP_g2);

            if (QP_i1 >= 0 && QP_i2 >= 0) {
                QP_out = QP_arrayAppend(QP_out, QP_i1);
                QP_out = QP_arrayAppend(QP_out, QP_i2);
                QP_out = QP_arrayAppend(QP_out, QP_use);
            }
        }
    }

    if (lengthOf(QP_out)==0) return newArray(0);

    QP_count = lengthOf(QP_out)/3;
    QP_final = newArray(1 + lengthOf(QP_out));
    QP_final[0] = QP_count;
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_out); QP_i++) QP_final[QP_i+1] = QP_out[QP_i];
    return QP_final;
}


function QP_countSignificantPairs(QP_sigPairs) {
    if (lengthOf(QP_sigPairs)==0) return 0;
    if (QP_sigPairs[0] <= 0) return 0;

    QP_n = 0;
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<QP_sigPairs[0]; QP_i++) {
        QP_pv = QP_sigPairs[1 + 3*QP_i + 2];

        if (QP_pv == QP_pv) {
            if (QP_pv < 0.05) QP_n++;
        }
    }
    return QP_n;
}


// ============================================================
// DATA / PARSING
// ============================================================
function QP_detectStatsMode(QP_statsTxt, QP_statsPath) {

    if (indexOf(QP_statsTxt, "Mode\tMann-Whitney") >= 0) return "MW";
    if (indexOf(QP_statsTxt, "Mode\tKruskal-Wallis") >= 0) return "KW";

    QP_name = QP_baseNameNoExt(QP_statsPath);
    if (startsWith(QP_name, "STATS_mannwhitney")) return "MW";
    if (startsWith(QP_name, "STATS_kruskalwallis")) return "KW";

    return "";
}

function QP_extractInputPathFromStats(QP_statsTxt) {

    QP_statsTxt = replace(QP_statsTxt, "\r", "");

    // 1) exact line starting with Input\t
    QP_lines = split(QP_statsTxt, "\n");
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_lines); QP_i++) {
        QP_L = QP_lines[QP_i];
        if (startsWith(QP_L, "Input\t")) {
            QP_parts = split(QP_L, "\t");
            if (lengthOf(QP_parts)>1) return QP_parts[1];
        }
    }

    // 2) inline "... Input\t<path>"
    QP_pos = indexOf(QP_statsTxt, "Input\t");
    if (QP_pos >= 0) {
        QP_start = QP_pos + lengthOf("Input\t");
        QP_rest = substring(QP_statsTxt, QP_start);
        QP_nl = indexOf(QP_rest, "\n");
        if (QP_nl >= 0) return substring(QP_rest, 0, QP_nl);
        return QP_rest;
    }

    return "";
}

function QP_resolveLongPath(QP_statsPath, QP_longPathFromStats) {

    QP_candidate = "" + QP_longPathFromStats;
    QP_candidate = replace(QP_candidate, "\\", "/");

    // 1) exact path from stats file
    if (QP_isReadableLongFile(QP_candidate))
        return QP_candidate;

    // 2) same filename, but in stats directory
    QP_statsDir = QP_dirOf(QP_statsPath);
    QP_longFile = QP_fileNameOnly(QP_candidate);
    QP_candidate2 = QP_statsDir + QP_longFile;

    if (QP_isReadableLongFile(QP_candidate2))
        return QP_candidate2;

    // 3) search for likely LONG file in stats directory
    QP_candidate3 = QP_findLikelyLongInDir(QP_statsDir);
    if (QP_candidate3 != "")
        return QP_candidate3;

    // 4) ask manually
    QP_manual = File.openDialog("Could not resolve LONG file automatically.\nPlease select the matching ANOVA_Ready_Data ... LONG file manually.");
    if (QP_manual == "")
        exit("Aborted: LONG file could not be resolved.");

    QP_manual = replace(QP_manual, "\\", "/");
    if (!QP_isReadableLongFile(QP_manual))
        exit("Selected LONG file could not be read or is not a valid LONG file.");

    return QP_manual;
}

function QP_isReadableLongFile(QP_path) {

    if (QP_path == "") return false;
    QP_path = replace(QP_path, "\\", "/");

    if (!File.exists(QP_path)) return false;

    QP_txt = File.openAsString(QP_path);
    if (QP_txt == "") return false;
    if (QP_txt == "0") return false;

    QP_txt = replace(QP_txt, "\r", "");
    if (indexOf(QP_txt, "Group_Assignment") < 0) return false;
    if (indexOf(QP_txt, "Probe_ID") < 0) return false;

    return true;
}

function QP_findLikelyLongInDir(QP_dir) {

    QP_list = getFileList(QP_dir);
    if (lengthOf(QP_list) == 0) return "";

    // pass 1: prefer ANOVA_Ready_Data ... LONG ...
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_list); QP_i++) {
        QP_name = QP_list[QP_i];
        if (endsWith(QP_name, "/")) continue;

        if (startsWith(QP_name, "ANOVA_Ready_Data") && indexOf(QP_name, "LONG") >= 0) {
            QP_candidate = QP_dir + QP_name;
            if (QP_isReadableLongFile(QP_candidate))
                return QP_candidate;
        }
    }

    // pass 2: any readable txt with LONG structure
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_list); QP_i++) {
        QP_name = QP_list[QP_i];
        if (endsWith(QP_name, "/")) continue;

        if (endsWith(QP_name, ".txt")) {
            QP_candidate = QP_dir + QP_name;
            if (QP_isReadableLongFile(QP_candidate))
                return QP_candidate;
        }
    }

    return "";
}

function QP_getGroupsFromLong(QP_longPath) {

    QP_txt = File.openAsString(QP_longPath);
    QP_txt = replace(QP_txt, "\r", "");
    QP_lines = split(QP_txt, "\n");
    if (lengthOf(QP_lines) < 2) return newArray(0);

    QP_header = split(QP_lines[0], "\t");
    QP_gCol = -1;

    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_header); QP_i++) {
        if (QP_header[QP_i] == "Group_Assignment") QP_gCol = QP_i;
    }
    if (QP_gCol < 0) return newArray(0);

    QP_groups = newArray(0);

    for (QP_r=1; QP_r<lengthOf(QP_lines); QP_r++) {
        QP_line = QP_lines[QP_r];
        if (trim(QP_line)=="") continue;

        QP_parts = split(QP_line, "\t");
        if (lengthOf(QP_parts) <= QP_gCol) continue;

        QP_g = trim(QP_parts[QP_gCol]);
        if (!QP_isBadToken(QP_g) && !QP_arrayContains(QP_groups, QP_g))
            QP_groups = QP_arrayAppend(QP_groups, QP_g);
    }

    return QP_groups;
}

function QP_reorderGroupsWithBaseline(QP_groups, QP_baseline) {
    QP_out = newArray(0);
    QP_out = QP_arrayAppend(QP_out, QP_baseline);

    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_groups); QP_i++) {
        if (QP_groups[QP_i] != QP_baseline)
            QP_out = QP_arrayAppend(QP_out, QP_groups[QP_i]);
    }
    return QP_out;
}


// Return [okFlag, mean1..meanN, sd1..sdN]
function QP_meanSdFromLong_groups(QP_longPath, QP_groupsOrdered, QP_paramName) {

    QP_txt = File.openAsString(QP_longPath);
    QP_txt = replace(QP_txt, "\r", "");
    QP_lines = split(QP_txt, "\n");
    QP_nGroups = lengthOf(QP_groupsOrdered);

    QP_res = newArray(1 + 2*QP_nGroups);

    if (lengthOf(QP_lines) < 2) {
        QP_res[0] = 0;
        return QP_res;
    }

    QP_header = split(QP_lines[0], "\t");
    QP_gCol = -1;
    QP_pCol = -1;

    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_header); QP_i++) {
        if (QP_header[QP_i]=="Group_Assignment") QP_gCol = QP_i;
        if (QP_header[QP_i]==QP_paramName)       QP_pCol = QP_i;
    }

    if (QP_gCol<0 || QP_pCol<0) {
        QP_res[0] = 0;
        return QP_res;
    }

    QP_res[0] = 1;

    QP_nArr    = newArray(QP_nGroups);
    QP_meanArr = newArray(QP_nGroups);
    QP_M2Arr   = newArray(QP_nGroups);

    for (QP_r=1; QP_r<lengthOf(QP_lines); QP_r++) {
        QP_line = QP_lines[QP_r];
        if (QP_line=="") continue;

        QP_parts = split(QP_line, "\t");
        if (lengthOf(QP_parts) <= QP_pCol || lengthOf(QP_parts) <= QP_gCol) continue;

        QP_grp = QP_parts[QP_gCol];
        QP_raw = QP_parts[QP_pCol];
        QP_v   = QP_parseFloatSafe(QP_raw);

        if (QP_v != QP_v) continue;

        QP_gi = QP_findStringIndex(QP_groupsOrdered, QP_grp);
        if (QP_gi < 0) continue;

        QP_nArr[QP_gi]++;
        QP_delta = QP_v - QP_meanArr[QP_gi];
        QP_meanArr[QP_gi] = QP_meanArr[QP_gi] + QP_delta / QP_nArr[QP_gi];
        QP_M2Arr[QP_gi]   = QP_M2Arr[QP_gi] + QP_delta * (QP_v - QP_meanArr[QP_gi]);
    }

    for (QP_gi=0; QP_gi<QP_nGroups; QP_gi++) {
        QP_sd = 0/0;
        if (QP_nArr[QP_gi] > 1) QP_sd = sqrt(QP_M2Arr[QP_gi] / (QP_nArr[QP_gi] - 1));
        if (QP_nArr[QP_gi] == 0) QP_meanArr[QP_gi] = 0/0;

        QP_res[1 + QP_gi] = QP_meanArr[QP_gi];
        QP_res[1 + QP_nGroups + QP_gi] = QP_sd;
    }

    return QP_res;
}


// ============================================================
// HELPERS
// ============================================================
function QP_findStringIndex(arr, s) {
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(arr); QP_i++) if (arr[QP_i]==s) return QP_i;
    return -1;
}

function QP_parseFloatSafe(raw) {
    if (raw=="") return 0/0;
    QP_s = "" + raw;
    QP_s = replace(QP_s, " ", "");
    QP_s = replace(QP_s, ",", ".");
    if (QP_s=="NaN" || QP_s=="Infinity" || QP_s=="-Infinity") return 0/0;
    return parseFloat(QP_s);
}

function QP_isBadToken(s) {
    QP_t = toLowerCase(trim(s));
    if (QP_t == "" || QP_t == "na" || QP_t == "nan" || QP_t == "inf") return 1;
    return 0;
}

function QP_starsOnly(p) {
    if (p!=p) return "";
    if (p < 0.0001) return "****";
    if (p < 0.001)  return "***";
    if (p < 0.01)   return "**";
    if (p < 0.05)   return "*";
    return "";
}

function QP_max2(a,b) {
    if (a>b) return a;
    return b;
}

function QP_textWidthApprox(str, pxPerChar) {
    if (str=="") return 0;
    return lengthOf(str) * pxPerChar;
}

function QP_dirOf(QP_path) {
    QP_p = replace(QP_path, "\\", "/");
    QP_last = -1;
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_p); QP_i++) {
        if (substring(QP_p, QP_i, QP_i+1)=="/") QP_last = QP_i;
    }
    if (QP_last < 0) return "";
    return substring(QP_p, 0, QP_last+1);
}

function QP_fileNameOnly(QP_path) {
    QP_p = replace(QP_path, "\\", "/");
    QP_last = -1;
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(QP_p); QP_i++) {
        if (substring(QP_p, QP_i, QP_i+1)=="/") QP_last = QP_i;
    }
    if (QP_last < 0) return QP_p;
    return substring(QP_p, QP_last+1);
}

function QP_baseNameNoExt(QP_path) {
    QP_name = QP_fileNameOnly(QP_path);
    if (endsWith(QP_name, ".txt")) QP_name = substring(QP_name, 0, lengthOf(QP_name)-4);
    return QP_name;
}

function QP_cleanStatsBase(QP_base) {

    QP_b = "" + QP_base;

    if (startsWith(QP_b, "STATS_mannwhitney__"))   QP_b = substring(QP_b, lengthOf("STATS_mannwhitney__"));
    if (startsWith(QP_b, "STATS_mannwhitney_"))    QP_b = substring(QP_b, lengthOf("STATS_mannwhitney_"));
    if (startsWith(QP_b, "STATS_kruskalwallis__")) QP_b = substring(QP_b, lengthOf("STATS_kruskalwallis__"));
    if (startsWith(QP_b, "STATS_kruskalwallis_"))  QP_b = substring(QP_b, lengthOf("STATS_kruskalwallis_"));

    QP_b = replace(QP_b, " (ENG)", "");
    QP_b = replace(QP_b, " (GER)", "");
    QP_b = replace(QP_b, "(ENG)", "");
    QP_b = replace(QP_b, "(GER)", "");
    QP_b = replace(QP_b, "()", "");
    QP_b = replace(QP_b, " ()", "");
    QP_b = replace(QP_b, "  ", " ");
    QP_b = replace(QP_b, "  ", " ");

    return QP_b;
}

function QP_fmtAbs(QP_abs, QP_unitSuffix, QP_absDigits) {
    return d2s(QP_abs, QP_absDigits) + QP_unitSuffix;
}

function QP_fmtPct(QP_pct, QP_pctDigits) {
    if (QP_pct!=QP_pct) return "(NA)";
    return "(" + d2s(QP_pct, QP_pctDigits) + "%)";
}

function QP_yTopOfMean(QP_mean, QP_y0, QP_plotH, QP_yMax) {
    if (QP_yMax<=0) return QP_y0;
    return QP_y0 - (QP_mean / QP_yMax) * QP_plotH;
}

function QP_arrayContains(arr, v) {
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(arr); QP_i++) if (arr[QP_i] == v) return true;
    return false;
}

function QP_arrayAppend(arr, v) {
    QP_newArr = newArray(lengthOf(arr) + 1);
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(arr); QP_i++) QP_newArr[QP_i] = arr[QP_i];
    QP_newArr[lengthOf(arr)] = v;
    return QP_newArr;
}

function QP_joinArray(arr, sep) {
    QP_s = "";
    for (QP_i=0; QP_i<lengthOf(arr); QP_i++) {
        if (QP_i > 0) QP_s = QP_s + sep;
        QP_s = QP_s + arr[QP_i];
    }
    return QP_s;
}

function QP_safeToken(QP_s) {
    QP_t = "" + QP_s;
    QP_t = replace(QP_t, " ", "_");
    QP_t = replace(QP_t, "/", "_");
    QP_t = replace(QP_t, "\\", "_");
    QP_t = replace(QP_t, ":", "_");
    QP_t = replace(QP_t, ";", "_");
    QP_t = replace(QP_t, ",", "_");
    QP_t = replace(QP_t, "(", "");
    QP_t = replace(QP_t, ")", "");
    QP_t = replace(QP_t, "[", "");
    QP_t = replace(QP_t, "]", "");
    return QP_t;
}



// ============================================================
// CUSTOM SCATTER (ImageJ Macro) — Classic + Robust (USER CHOICE / 4 MODES)
// - 4 panels: Thr10, ThrUser, Thr50, Thr90
// - User can choose ONE regression mode, or export ALL variants (4 PNGs):
//     1) Classic (OLS)
//     2) Robust IRLS (Tukey+MAD+X-leverage)
//     3) Robust Theil-Sen
//     4) Robust Trimmed OLS (80%)
// - Smart Axis Rounding (DATA-DRIVEN, NO HARDCODED AXES)
// - Tick decimals derived from STEP size (per axis)
// - Line Clipping
//
// NEW (tiny knobs):
//   SP_xAxisLabel_YShift : moves X-axis label up/down (px). + = down
//   SP_yAxisLabel_XShift : moves Y-axis label left/right (px). + = right (towards plot), - = left
// ============================================================

macro "Scatter: Systole vs Diastole (Classic + Robust) [F9]" {

    // ---- user settings ----
    SP_dec = 6;
    SP_UI = 1.80;   // UI scaling for high-res screens
    SP_P  = 900;    // panel size (square)

    // NEW: label shift knobs (UNCHANGED)
    SP_xAxisLabel_YShift = 0;    // + moves label DOWN, - moves UP
    SP_yAxisLabel_XShift = -20;  // + moves label RIGHT (towards plot), - moves LEFT

    // Layout spacing (UNCHANGED)
    SP_titlePad    = floor(8*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_xLabelPad   = floor(50*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_yTickPad    = floor(10*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_yTickVShift = floor(10*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_xTickPad    = floor(26*SP_UI + 0.5);

    SP_marginL = floor(115*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_marginR = floor(40*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_marginT = floor(60*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_marginB = floor(85*SP_UI + 0.5);

    SP_gridN = 5; // "target" grid density (axis may choose N=4..6 for best fit)
    SP_axisW = maxOf(1, floor(2*SP_UI + 0.5));
    SP_gridW = maxOf(1, floor(1*SP_UI + 0.5));

    SP_titleFont = floor(24*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_axisFont  = floor(22*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_tickFont  = floor(22*SP_UI + 0.5);

    SP_dotD = floor(7*SP_UI + 0.5);
    if (SP_dotD < 3) SP_dotD = 3;

    // Colors (RGB)
    SP_bR=0;   SP_bG=0;   SP_bB=255; // Blue
    SP_rR=255; SP_rG=0;   SP_rB=0;   // Red
    SP_gR=210; SP_gG=210; SP_gB=210; // Grid (light grey)
    SP_kR=0;   SP_kG=0;   SP_kB=0;   // Black

    // Regression drawing
    SP_regLine  = 1;
    SP_regEq    = 1;
    SP_regEqDec = 3;
    SP_regLineW = maxOf(1, floor(3*SP_UI + 0.5));

    SP_eqPadX    = floor(12*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_eqPadY    = floor(22*SP_UI + 0.5);
    SP_eqLineGap = floor((SP_tickFont + 10) + 0.5);


    // ============================================================
    // IMPORT (1:1 aus deiner funktionierenden Version)
    // ============================================================

    // --- 1) File selection ---
    SP_path = File.openDialog("Select ANOVA_Ready_Data_[Date] LONG (ENG).txt");
    if (SP_path == "") exit("Abbruch.");
    SP_dir  = File.getParent(SP_path);
    SP_file = File.getName(SP_path);
    SP_base = SP_stripExtension(SP_file);

    // --- 2) Read file ---
    SP_txt = File.openAsString(SP_path);
    SP_lines = split(SP_txt, "\n");
    if (SP_lines.length < 2) exit("Datei ist leer.");

    // --- 3) Header / column indices ---
    SP_header = SP_trimCR(SP_lines[0]);
    SP_cols   = split(SP_header, "\t");

    SP_idxGroup = SP_findCol(SP_cols, "Group_Assignment");
    if (SP_idxGroup < 0) exit("Spalte 'Group_Assignment' nicht gefunden.");

    SP_systNames  = newArray("Systoles10% mean [s]", "SystolesUser mean [s]", "Systoles50% mean [s]", "Systoles90% mean [s]");
    SP_diastNames = newArray("Diastoles10% mean [s]", "DiastolesUser mean [s]", "Diastoles50% mean [s]", "Diastoles90% mean [s]");
    SP_thrLabels  = newArray("10%", "User", "50%", "90%");

    SP_systIdx = newArray(4); SP_diastIdx = newArray(4);
    for (t=0; t<4; t++) {
        SP_systIdx[t]  = SP_findCol(SP_cols, SP_systNames[t]);
        SP_diastIdx[t] = SP_findCol(SP_cols, SP_diastNames[t]);
        if (SP_systIdx[t] < 0)  exit("Spalte nicht gefunden: " + SP_systNames[t]);
        if (SP_diastIdx[t] < 0) exit("Spalte nicht gefunden: " + SP_diastNames[t]);
    }

    

    // --- 4) Detect groups (need at least 2) ---
    SP_groups = newArray(0);
    for (r=1; r<SP_lines.length; r++) {
        line = SP_trimCR(SP_lines[r]);
        if (trim(line) != "") {
            f = split(line, "\t");
            if (f.length > SP_idxGroup) {
                g = trim(f[SP_idxGroup]);
                if (!SP_isBadToken(g) && !SP_arrayContains(SP_groups, g)) {
                    SP_groups = SP_arrayAppend(SP_groups, g);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    if (SP_groups.length < 2)
        exit("Es werden mindestens 2 Gruppen benötigt.");

    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    // Group selection logic
    // - 2 groups: keep old behavior
    // - 3+ groups: user chooses the two groups to compare
    // ------------------------------------------------------------
    if (SP_groups.length == 2) {

        // exactly as before
        Dialog.create("Scatter Plot Settings");
        Dialog.addChoice("BLUE group:", SP_groups, SP_groups[0]);
        Dialog.show();
        SP_blue = Dialog.getChoice();

        if (SP_blue == SP_groups[0]) SP_red = SP_groups[1];
        else                         SP_red = SP_groups[0];

    } else {

        // Step 1: choose first group
        Dialog.create("Scatter Plot Settings");
        Dialog.addMessage(SP_groups.length + " groups detected.\nPlease select two to be plotted against each other.");
        Dialog.addChoice("Group 1:", SP_groups, SP_groups[0]);
        Dialog.show();
        SP_group1 = Dialog.getChoice();

        // Step 2: build remaining list and choose second group
        SP_groupsRemaining = newArray(0);
        for (i=0; i<SP_groups.length; i++) {
            if (SP_groups[i] != SP_group1)
                SP_groupsRemaining = SP_arrayAppend(SP_groupsRemaining, SP_groups[i]);
        }

        Dialog.create("Scatter Plot Settings");
        Dialog.addChoice("Group 2:", SP_groupsRemaining, SP_groupsRemaining[0]);
        Dialog.show();
        SP_group2 = Dialog.getChoice();

        // Step 3: choose which of the two is BLUE
        SP_pair = newArray(SP_group1, SP_group2);

        Dialog.create("Scatter Plot Settings");
        Dialog.addChoice("BLUE group:", SP_pair, SP_group1);
        Dialog.show();
        SP_blue = Dialog.getChoice();

        if (SP_blue == SP_group1) SP_red = SP_group2;
        else                      SP_red = SP_group1;
    }


    // --- user chooses regression (or export all 4) ---
    SP_regModes = newArray(
        "Classic (OLS)",
        "Robust IRLS (Tukey+MAD+X-leverage)",
        "Robust Theil-Sen",
        "Robust Trimmed OLS (80%)"
    );

    Dialog.create("Regression Settings");
    Dialog.addChoice("Regression:", SP_regModes, SP_regModes[1]);
    Dialog.addCheckbox("Export ALL variants (4 PNGs)", false);
    Dialog.show();
    SP_regModeStr = Dialog.getChoice();
    SP_exportAll  = Dialog.getCheckbox();

    SP_modePick = 0;
    if (SP_regModeStr == SP_regModes[1]) SP_modePick = 1;
    if (SP_regModeStr == SP_regModes[2]) SP_modePick = 2;
    if (SP_regModeStr == SP_regModes[3]) SP_modePick = 3;

    if (SP_exportAll) SP_modes = newArray(0, 1, 2, 3);
    else              SP_modes = newArray(SP_modePick);

    // ============================================================
    // END IMPORT
    // ============================================================


    for (mm=0; mm<SP_modes.length; mm++) {

        SP_mode = SP_modes[mm];

        SP_modeTag  = "Classic";
        SP_eqSuffix = "";
        if (SP_mode == 1) { SP_modeTag = "IRLS_Tukey"; SP_eqSuffix = " (IRLS)"; }
        if (SP_mode == 2) { SP_modeTag = "TheilSen";   SP_eqSuffix = " (Theil–Sen)"; }
        if (SP_mode == 3) { SP_modeTag = "Trimmed80";  SP_eqSuffix = " (Trimmed)"; }

        // --- 5) Main plot loop (4 panels) ---
        SP_stackTitle = "SP__SCATTER_STACK_TMP__" + SP_modeTag;
        newImage(SP_stackTitle, "RGB white", SP_P, SP_P, 4);

        for (t=0; t<4; t++) {

            xB = newArray(0); yB = newArray(0);
            xR = newArray(0); yR = newArray(0);

            for (r=1; r<SP_lines.length; r++) {
                line = SP_trimCR(SP_lines[r]);
                if (trim(line) == "") continue;
                f = split(line, "\t");
                if (f.length <= SP_idxGroup) continue;

                g = trim(f[SP_idxGroup]);
                x = SP_parseIfValid(f[SP_systIdx[t]]);
                y = SP_parseIfValid(f[SP_diastIdx[t]]);

                if (x==x && y==y) {
                    if (g == SP_blue) { xB = SP_arrayAppendNum(xB, x); yB = SP_arrayAppendNum(yB, y); }
                    else if (g == SP_red) { xR = SP_arrayAppendNum(xR, x); yR = SP_arrayAppendNum(yR, y); }
                }
            }

            // ============================================================
            // ADAPTIVE SCALING (FIXED) — DATA-DRIVEN, NO HARDCODED AXES
            // - axes follow loaded data
            // - "nice" rounding
            // - decimals follow step size (per axis)
            // - robust for <1, 1–99, 100+ and also min around 7 (=> axis around 7..8)
            // ============================================================

            // data bounds from BOTH groups
            xMinD =  1e99; xMaxD = -1e99;
            yMinD =  1e99; yMaxD = -1e99;

            for (i=0; i<xB.length; i++) {
                if (xB[i] < xMinD) xMinD = xB[i];
                if (xB[i] > xMaxD) xMaxD = xB[i];
                if (yB[i] < yMinD) yMinD = yB[i];
                if (yB[i] > yMaxD) yMaxD = yB[i];
            }
            for (i=0; i<xR.length; i++) {
                if (xR[i] < xMinD) xMinD = xR[i];
                if (xR[i] > xMaxD) xMaxD = xR[i];
                if (yR[i] < yMinD) yMinD = yR[i];
                if (yR[i] > yMaxD) yMaxD = yR[i];
            }

            // fallback (empty slice safety)
            if (xMaxD < -1e98) { xMinD = 0; xMaxD = 1; }
            if (yMaxD < -1e98) { yMinD = 0; yMaxD = 1; }

            // choose nice axes; returns: [min, max, step, N, dec]
            ax = SP_axisAuto(xMinD, xMaxD, SP_gridN);
            ay = SP_axisAuto(yMinD, yMaxD, SP_gridN);

            xmin = ax[0]; xmax = ax[1]; xStep = ax[2]; xN = round(ax[3]); xDec = round(ax[4]);
            ymin = ay[0]; ymax = ay[1]; yStep = ay[2]; yN = round(ay[3]); yDec = round(ay[4]);

            if (xN < 2) xN = 2;
            if (yN < 2) yN = 2;

            // ============================================================

            panelTitle = "SP__PANEL_TMP";
            newImage(panelTitle, "RGB white", SP_P, SP_P, 1);
            selectWindow(panelTitle);

            px0 = SP_marginL; py0 = SP_marginT;
            px1 = SP_P - SP_marginR; py1 = SP_P - SP_marginB;

            // Grid & frame (X and Y can have different N)
            setColor(SP_gR, SP_gG, SP_gB); setLineWidth(SP_gridW);

            // vertical grid (X)
            for (k=0; k<=xN; k++) {
                xg = px0 + (px1-px0)*k/xN;
                drawLine(xg, py0, xg, py1);
            }
            // horizontal grid (Y)
            for (k=0; k<=yN; k++) {
                yg = py0 + (py1-py0)*k/yN;
                drawLine(px0, yg, px1, yg);
            }

            setColor(SP_kR, SP_kG, SP_kB); setLineWidth(SP_axisW);
            drawRect(px0, py0, px1-px0, py1-py0);

            // Axis labels (UNCHANGED placement knobs)
            setFont("SansSerif", SP_axisFont, "plain");
            xlab = "Systole [s]"; sw = getStringWidth(xlab);
            drawString(xlab, (px0+px1-sw)/2, py1 + SP_xLabelPad + SP_xAxisLabel_YShift);

            // Ticks (DECIMALS FOLLOW STEP SIZE, per axis)
            setFont("SansSerif", SP_tickFont, "plain");

            // X ticks
            for (k=0; k<=xN; k++) {
                xg = px0 + (px1-px0)*k/xN;
                xv = xmin + xStep * k;
                drawLine(xg, py1, xg, py1+6);
                s = SP_d2sSafe(xv, xDec); sw = getStringWidth(s);
                drawString(s, xg - sw/2, py1 + SP_xTickPad);
            }

            // Y ticks
            for (k=0; k<=yN; k++) {
                yg = py0 + (py1-py0)*k/yN;
                yv = ymax - yStep * k;
                drawLine(px0-6, yg, px0, yg);
                s = SP_d2sSafe(yv, yDec); sw = getStringWidth(s);
                drawString(s, px0 - SP_yTickPad - sw, yg + SP_yTickVShift);
            }

            ylab = "Diastole [s]";
            SP_drawVerticalLabel(ylab, px0, py0, py1, yDec, ymax, ymin, yN);

            // Title
            setFont("SansSerif", SP_titleFont, "bold");
            ttl = "Thr" + SP_thrLabels[t];
            drawString(ttl, (px0 + px1 - getStringWidth(ttl))/2, py0 - SP_titlePad);

            // Regression (mode) — UNCHANGED
            if (SP_mode == 1) {
                regB = SP_irlsTukeyReg(xB, yB);
                regR = SP_irlsTukeyReg(xR, yR);
            } else if (SP_mode == 2) {
                regB = SP_theilSenReg(xB, yB);
                regR = SP_theilSenReg(xR, yR);
            } else if (SP_mode == 3) {
                regB = SP_trimmedReg(xB, yB, 0.80);
                regR = SP_trimmedReg(xR, yR, 0.80);
            } else {
                regB = SP_linReg(xB, yB);
                regR = SP_linReg(xR, yR);
            }

            // Draw regression lines — UNCHANGED
            if (SP_regLine == 1) {
                setLineWidth(SP_regLineW);
                if (regB[3] >= 2) {
                    setColor(SP_bR, SP_bG, SP_bB);
                    SP_drawRegLine(regB[0], regB[1], xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax, px0, py0, px1, py1);
                }
                if (regR[3] >= 2) {
                    setColor(SP_rR, SP_rG, SP_rB);
                    SP_drawRegLine(regR[0], regR[1], xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax, px0, py0, px1, py1);
                }
            }

            // Print equations — UNCHANGED
            if (SP_regEq == 1) {
                setFont("SansSerif", SP_tickFont, "plain");
                eqX = px0 + SP_eqPadX; eqY = py0 + SP_eqPadY;

                if (regB[3] >= 2) {
                    setColor(SP_bR, SP_bG, SP_bB);
                    drawString(SP_regEqStr(regB[0], regB[1], SP_regEqDec) + SP_eqSuffix, eqX, eqY);
                    eqY += SP_eqLineGap;
                }
                if (regR[3] >= 2) {
                    setColor(SP_rR, SP_rG, SP_rB);
                    drawString(SP_regEqStr(regR[0], regR[1], SP_regEqDec) + SP_eqSuffix, eqX, eqY);
                }
            }

            // Points (big filled circles with dark halo) — UNCHANGED
            
			rad = floor(SP_dotD/4);
			
			// Blau gefüllt
			SP_drawPoints(xB, yB, xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax, px0, py0, px1, py1, rad, SP_bR, SP_bG, SP_bB, 0, 0, 150);
			
			// Rot hohl
			SP_drawPoints(xR, yR, xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax, px0, py0, px1, py1, rad, SP_rR, SP_rG, SP_rB, 150, 0, 0);

            // Copy to stack slice
            run("Select All"); run("Copy");
            selectWindow(SP_stackTitle);
            setSlice(t+1);
            run("Paste");

            selectWindow(panelTitle);
            close();
        }

        // Montage + save
        selectWindow(SP_stackTitle);
        run("Make Montage...", "columns=2 rows=2 scale=1 border=0");
        
        SP_pairLeft  = "" + SP_blue;
        SP_pairRight = "" + SP_red;

        SP_pairLeft  = replace(SP_pairLeft,  " ", "_");
        SP_pairRight = replace(SP_pairRight, " ", "_");

        SP_pairLeft  = replace(SP_pairLeft,  "/", "_");
        SP_pairRight = replace(SP_pairRight, "/", "_");

        SP_pairLeft  = replace(SP_pairLeft,  "\\", "_");
        SP_pairRight = replace(SP_pairRight, "\\", "_");

        SP_pairLeft  = replace(SP_pairLeft,  ":", "_");
        SP_pairRight = replace(SP_pairRight, ":", "_");

        SP_pairLeft  = replace(SP_pairLeft,  ";", "_");
        SP_pairRight = replace(SP_pairRight, ";", "_");

        SP_pairLeft  = replace(SP_pairLeft,  ",", "_");
        SP_pairRight = replace(SP_pairRight, ",", "_");

        SP_pairLeft  = replace(SP_pairLeft,  "(", "");
        SP_pairRight = replace(SP_pairRight, "(", "");

        SP_pairLeft  = replace(SP_pairLeft,  ")", "");
        SP_pairRight = replace(SP_pairRight, ")","");

        SP_pairTag = SP_pairLeft + "_vs_" + SP_pairRight;

		SP_baseSafe = "" + SP_base;
		SP_baseSafe = replace(SP_baseSafe, ":", "_");
		SP_baseSafe = replace(SP_baseSafe, "/", "_");
		SP_baseSafe = replace(SP_baseSafe, "\\", "_");

       	outTitle = SP_baseSafe + "__Scatter_2x2__" + SP_pairTag + "__" + SP_modeTag;
        
        rename(outTitle);

        // Legend — UNCHANGED
        SP_drawLegendTopLeft(SP_blue, SP_red);

        saveAs("PNG", SP_dir + File.separator + outTitle + ".png");
        print("Saved: " + SP_dir + File.separator + outTitle + ".png");


    }

    print("Done.");

    close("*");
    run("Close All");
}


// ======================= TICK FORMAT (tiny bias to avoid .059 instead of .060) =======================

function SP_d2sSafe(v, dec) {
    eps = 0.0005 * pow(10, -dec);
    return d2s(v + eps, dec);
}


// ============================================================
// NEW: DATA-DRIVEN AXIS (no hardcoding)
// Returns: [niceMin, niceMax, step, N, decimals]
// - chooses N from {targetN-1, targetN, targetN+1} to reduce wasted space
// - clamps to 0 only if data are non-negative and min is near 0
// - decimals derived from step size
// ============================================================

// ============================================================
// AXIS AUTO (FORCE ZERO START IF DATA >= 0)
// Returns: [niceMin, niceMax, step, N, decimals]
// - If minD >= 0  -> niceMin is forced to 0 (always)
// - niceMax is "nice" and covers the data (with small headroom)
// - decimals derived from step size
// ============================================================

function SP_axisAuto(minD, maxD, targetN) {

    // sanitize
    if (maxD < minD) { tmp=minD; minD=maxD; maxD=tmp; }
    span = maxD - minD;
    if (span <= 1e-15) span = maxOf(1e-6, abs(maxD)*0.1 + 1e-6);

    // headroom only at the top (since min will be clamped to 0)
    padTop = 0.03 * span;
    maxP  = maxD + padTop;

    // ---- FORCE ZERO START (as requested) ----
    niceMinFixed = 0;

    // candidates around target
    cand = newArray(targetN-1, targetN, targetN+1);
    bestScore = 1e99;

    bestMin = 0;
    bestMax = 1;
    bestStep = 1;
    bestN = targetN;

    // If the user guarantees all values > 0, we always force 0.
    // If someone accidentally has negative data, we still fall back to data-driven min.
    forceZero = (minD >= 0);

    for (ci=0; ci<cand.length; ci++) {

        N = cand[ci];
        if (N < 2) continue;
        if (N > 12) continue;

        if (forceZero) {

            // choose a "nice" step so that N steps roughly reach maxP
            step = SP_axisNiceStep(maxP - 0, N);
            if (step <= 0) continue;

            niceMin = 0;
            niceMax = SP_ceilToStep(maxP, step);

            // actual step count
            aN = round((niceMax - niceMin)/step);
            if (aN < 2) aN = 2;

            // relock max to avoid float drift
            niceMax = niceMin + aN*step;

            // scoring: prefer small overshoot and staying close to targetN
            usedSpan = niceMax - niceMin;
            over = (usedSpan - maxD) / maxOf(1e-12, maxD);
            if (over < 0) over = 0;

            dec = SP_axisDecimalsForStep(step);

            score = over;
            score += 0.07 * abs(aN - targetN);
            score += 0.01 * dec;

            if (abs(step - floor(step+0.5)) < 1e-12) score -= 0.02;

            if (score < bestScore) {
                bestScore = score;
                bestMin = niceMin;
                bestMax = niceMax;
                bestStep = step;
                bestN = aN;
            }

        } else {

            // fallback: original behavior for negative ranges (rare)
            pad = 0.03 * span;
            minP = minD - pad;
            maxP2 = maxD + pad;

            step2 = SP_axisNiceStep(maxP2 - minP, N);
            if (step2 <= 0) continue;

            niceMin2 = SP_floorToStep(minP, step2);
            niceMax2 = SP_ceilToStep(maxP2, step2);

            aN2 = round((niceMax2 - niceMin2)/step2);
            if (aN2 < 2) aN2 = 2;
            niceMax2 = niceMin2 + aN2*step2;

            usedSpan2 = niceMax2 - niceMin2;
            over2 = (usedSpan2 - (maxD-minD)) / maxOf(1e-12, (maxD-minD));
            if (over2 < 0) over2 = 0;

            dec2 = SP_axisDecimalsForStep(step2);

            score2 = over2 + 0.07*abs(aN2-targetN) + 0.01*dec2;
            if (abs(step2 - floor(step2+0.5)) < 1e-12) score2 -= 0.02;

            if (score2 < bestScore) {
                bestScore = score2;
                bestMin = niceMin2;
                bestMax = niceMax2;
                bestStep = step2;
                bestN = aN2;
            }
        }
    }

    bestDec = SP_axisDecimalsForStep(bestStep);
    return newArray(bestMin, bestMax, bestStep, bestN, bestDec);
}


function SP_axisNiceStep(range, nSteps) {
    if (range <= 0) return 1.0;

    raw = range / nSteps;
    if (raw <= 0) return 1.0;

    mag  = pow(10, floor(log(raw)/log(10)));
    frac = raw / mag;

    vals = newArray(1.0, 1.5, 2.0, 2.5, 3.0, 4.0, 5.0, 10.0);
    for (i=0; i<vals.length; i++) {
        if (vals[i] >= frac) return vals[i] * mag;
    }
    return 10.0 * mag;
}

function SP_axisDecimalsForStep(step) {
    if (step <= 0) return 0;
    // integer => 0
    if (abs(step - floor(step+0.5)) < 1e-12) return 0;

    dec = 0;
    tmp = step;
    while (dec < 8) {
        if (abs(tmp - floor(tmp + 0.5)) < 1e-9) break;
        tmp *= 10;
        dec++;
    }
    return dec;
}

function SP_floorToStep(v, step) {
    if (step <= 0) return v;
    return floor((v + 1e-12)/step) * step;
}

function SP_ceil(v) {
    return -floor(-v);
}

function SP_ceilToStep(v, step) {
    if (step <= 0) return v;
    return SP_ceil((v - 1e-12)/step) * step;
}


// ======================= ROBUST: MEDIAN / MAD =======================

function SP_median(a) {
    n = a.length;
    if (n == 0) return NaN;
    tmp = newArray(n);
    for (i=0; i<n; i++) tmp[i] = a[i];
    Array.sort(tmp);
    mid = floor(n/2);
    if ((n % 2) == 1) return tmp[mid];
    return (tmp[mid-1] + tmp[mid]) / 2;
}

function SP_madAbout(a, center) {
    n = a.length;
    if (n == 0) return NaN;
    dev = newArray(n);
    for (i=0; i<n; i++) {
        d = a[i] - center;
        if (d < 0) d = -d;
        dev[i] = d;
    }
    return SP_median(dev);
}


// ======================= WEIGHTED LS =======================

function SP_linRegW(x, y, w) {
    n = x.length;
    sw=0; swx=0; swy=0; swxx=0; swxy=0; nEff=0;

    for (i=0; i<n; i++) {
        wi = w[i];
        if (wi <= 0) continue;
        nEff++;
        sw   += wi;
        swx  += wi * x[i];
        swy  += wi * y[i];
        swxx += wi * x[i] * x[i];
        swxy += wi * x[i] * y[i];
    }

    if (nEff < 2 || sw == 0) return newArray(NaN, NaN, 0, nEff);

    den = sw*swxx - swx*swx;
    if (den == 0) return newArray(NaN, NaN, 0, nEff);

    m = (sw*swxy - swx*swy) / den;
    b = (swy - m*swx) / sw;
    return newArray(m, b, 0, nEff);
}


// ======================= ROBUST: IRLS Tukey (MAD) + Leverage Downweight =======================

function SP_irlsTukeyReg(x, y) {
    n = x.length;
    if (n < 2) return newArray(NaN, NaN, 0, n);

    reg = SP_linReg(x, y);
    m = reg[0]; b = reg[1];
    if (m != m) return reg;

    medx = SP_median(x);
    madx = SP_madAbout(x, medx);
    sigx = 1.4826 * madx;
    if (sigx <= 0) sigx = 1e-12;

    cR = 4.685;
    cX = 4.685;

    maxIter = 25;
    tol = 1e-12;

    for (iter=0; iter<maxIter; iter++) {

        r = newArray(n);
        for (i=0; i<n; i++) r[i] = y[i] - (m*x[i] + b);

        medr = SP_median(r);
        madr = SP_madAbout(r, medr);
        sigma = 1.4826 * madr;
        if (sigma <= 0) break;

        w = newArray(n);
        nEff = 0;

        for (i=0; i<n; i++) {

            u  = (r[i] - medr) / (cR * sigma);
            au = u; if (au < 0) au = -au;

            wr = 0;
            if (au < 1) {
                t = 1 - u*u;
                wr = t*t;
            }

            ux = (x[i] - medx) / (cX * sigx);
            ax = ux; if (ax < 0) ax = -ax;

            wx = 0;
            if (ax < 1) {
                t2 = 1 - ux*ux;
                wx = t2*t2;
            }

            w[i] = wr * wx;
            if (w[i] > 0) nEff++;
        }

        if (nEff < 2) break;

        regW = SP_linRegW(x, y, w);
        m2 = regW[0]; b2 = regW[1];
        if (m2 != m2) break;

        if (abs(m2 - m) + abs(b2 - b) < tol * (1 + abs(m) + abs(b))) {
            m = m2; b = b2;
            return newArray(m, b, 0, nEff);
        }

        m = m2; b = b2;
    }

    return newArray(m, b, 0, n);
}


// ======================= ROBUST: Theil–Sen =======================

function SP_theilSenReg(x, y) {
    n0 = x.length;
    if (n0 < 2) return newArray(NaN, NaN, 0, n0);

    maxN = 400;
    if (n0 > maxN) {
        step = floor((n0 + maxN - 1) / maxN);
        x2 = newArray(0); y2 = newArray(0);
        for (i=0; i<n0; i+=step) {
            x2 = SP_arrayAppendNum(x2, x[i]);
            y2 = SP_arrayAppendNum(y2, y[i]);
        }
        x = x2; y = y2;
    }

    n = x.length;
    if (n < 2) return newArray(NaN, NaN, 0, n);

    pairsMax = n*(n-1)/2;
    slopes = newArray(pairsMax);
    idx = 0;

    for (i=0; i<n-1; i++) {
        for (j=i+1; j<n; j++) {
            dx = x[j] - x[i];
            if (dx == 0) continue;
            slopes[idx] = (y[j] - y[i]) / dx;
            idx++;
        }
    }
    if (idx < 1) return newArray(NaN, NaN, 0, n);

    s2 = newArray(idx);
    for (k=0; k<idx; k++) s2[k] = slopes[k];

    m = SP_median(s2);

    bArr = newArray(n);
    for (i=0; i<n; i++) bArr[i] = y[i] - m*x[i];

    b = SP_median(bArr);
    return newArray(m, b, 0, n);
}


// ======================= ROBUST: TRIMMED OLS (iterative) =======================

function SP_trimmedReg(x, y, keepFrac) {
    n = x.length;
    if (n < 2) return newArray(NaN, NaN, 0, n);

    if (keepFrac < 0.50) keepFrac = 0.50;
    if (keepFrac > 0.98) keepFrac = 0.98;

    reg = SP_linReg(x, y);
    m = reg[0]; b = reg[1];
    if (m != m) return reg;

    maxIter = 12;

    for (iter=0; iter<maxIter; iter++) {

        absRes = newArray(n);
        for (i=0; i<n; i++) {
            r = y[i] - (m*x[i] + b);
            if (r < 0) r = -r;
            absRes[i] = r;
        }

        tmp = newArray(n);
        for (i=0; i<n; i++) tmp[i] = absRes[i];
        Array.sort(tmp);

        h = floor(keepFrac*n + 0.5);
        if (h < 2) h = 2;
        if (h > n) h = n;

        cut = tmp[h-1];

        xIn = newArray(0);
        yIn = newArray(0);

        for (i=0; i<n; i++) {
            if (absRes[i] <= cut) {
                xIn = SP_arrayAppendNum(xIn, x[i]);
                yIn = SP_arrayAppendNum(yIn, y[i]);
            }
        }

        if (xIn.length < 2) break;

        reg2 = SP_linReg(xIn, yIn);
        m2 = reg2[0]; b2 = reg2[1];
        if (m2 != m2) break;

        if (abs(m2 - m) + abs(b2 - b) < 1e-12 * (1 + abs(m) + abs(b))) {
            m = m2; b = b2;
            return newArray(m, b, 0, xIn.length);
        }

        m = m2; b = b2;
    }

    return newArray(m, b, 0, n);
}


// ======================= PLOTTING HELPERS =======================

function SP_drawRegLine(m, b, xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax, px0, py0, px1, py1) {
    lx0 = xmin; ly0 = m*lx0 + b;
    lx1 = xmax; ly1 = m*lx1 + b;

    if (m != 0) {
        if (ly0 < ymin) { ly0 = ymin; lx0 = (ymin - b) / m; }
        if (ly0 > ymax) { ly0 = ymax; lx0 = (ymax - b) / m; }
        if (ly1 < ymin) { ly1 = ymin; lx1 = (ymin - b) / m; }
        if (ly1 > ymax) { ly1 = ymax; lx1 = (ymax - b) / m; }
    }

    if (lx0 < xmin) lx0 = xmin; if (lx0 > xmax) lx0 = xmax;
    if (lx1 < xmin) lx1 = xmin; if (lx1 > xmax) lx1 = xmax;

    xp0 = px0 + (lx0 - xmin)/(xmax - xmin) * (px1 - px0);
    yp0 = py1 - (ly0 - ymin)/(ymax - ymin) * (py1 - py0);
    xp1 = px0 + (lx1 - xmin)/(xmax - xmin) * (px1 - px0);
    yp1 = py1 - (ly1 - ymin)/(ymax - ymin) * (py1 - py0);

    drawLine(xp0, yp0, xp1, yp1);
}

function SP_drawPoints(x, y, xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax, px0, py0, px1, py1, rad, r, g, b, br, bg, bb) {
    for (i=0; i<x.length; i++) {
        xp = px0 + (x[i]-xmin)/(xmax-xmin)*(px1-px0);
        yp = py1 - (y[i]-ymin)/(ymax-ymin)*(py1-py0);
        setColor(br, bg, bb);
        fillOval(xp-rad-1, yp-rad-1, 2*rad+2, 2*rad+2);
        setColor(r, g, b);
        fillOval(xp-rad, yp-rad, 2*rad, 2*rad);
    }
}

// UPDATED signature: includes yN (placement unchanged, only width estimation correct)
function SP_drawVerticalLabel(text, px0, py0, py1, dec, ymax, ymin, yN) {

    if (yN < 2) yN = 2;

    swMax = 0;
    for (k=0; k<=yN; k++) {
        s = SP_d2sSafe(ymax - (ymax-ymin)*k/yN, dec);
        if (getStringWidth(s) > swMax) swMax = getStringWidth(s);
    }

    tw = py1 - py0;
    th = maxOf(40, floor(SP_axisFont*1.3 + 0.5));

    newImage("Y_TMP", "RGB white", tw, th, 1);
    setColor(0,0,0);
    setFont("SansSerif", SP_axisFont, "plain");
    drawString(text, (tw - getStringWidth(text))/2, th-6);

    run("Rotate 90 Degrees Left");
    run("Select All"); run("Copy");
    close();

    selectWindow("SP__PANEL_TMP");
    setPasteMode("Transparent-white");

    makeRectangle(px0 - swMax - 50 + SP_yAxisLabel_XShift, py0 + (py1-py0-tw)/2, th, tw);
    run("Paste");
}

function SP_drawLegendTopLeft(blueName, redName) {

    legBox    = maxOf(10, floor(12*SP_UI + 0.5));
    legPadY   = floor(6*SP_UI + 0.5);
    legTextDx = floor(8*SP_UI + 0.5);
    txtYoff   = floor(2*SP_UI + 0.5);

    legX = SP_marginL;
    legY = maxOf(4, floor(12*SP_UI + 0.5));

    legTextYShift = floor(4*SP_UI + 8);  // + = Text tiefer

    setFont("SansSerif", SP_tickFont, "plain");

    setColor(SP_bR, SP_bG, SP_bB); fillRect(legX, legY, legBox, legBox);
    setColor(SP_kR, SP_kG, SP_kB); drawRect(legX, legY, legBox, legBox);
    drawString(blueName, legX + legBox + legTextDx, legY  + legBox - txtYoff + legTextYShift);

    legY2 = legY + legBox + legPadY;
    setColor(SP_rR, SP_rG, SP_rB); fillRect(legX, legY2, legBox, legBox);
    setColor(SP_kR, SP_kG, SP_kB); drawRect(legX, legY2, legBox, legBox);
    drawString(redName,  legX + legBox + legTextDx, legY2 + legBox - txtYoff + legTextYShift);
}


// ======================= CLASSIC OLS =======================

function SP_linReg(x, y) {
    n = x.length;
    sx=0; sy=0; sxx=0; sxy=0;
    for (i=0; i<n; i++) {
        sx  += x[i];
        sy  += y[i];
        sxx += x[i]*x[i];
        sxy += x[i]*y[i];
    }
    d = n*sxx - sx*sx;
    if (d == 0) return newArray(NaN, NaN, 0, n);
    m = (n*sxy - sx*sy)/d;
    b = (sy - (m*sx))/n;
    return newArray(m, b, 0, n);
}

function SP_regEqStr(m, b, dec) {
    s = "y = " + d2s(m, dec) + "x";
    if (b < 0) s += " - " + d2s(abs(b), dec);
    else       s += " + " + d2s(b, dec);
    return s;
}


// ======================= FILE/TABLE HELPERS (IMPORT-STYLE) =======================

function SP_isBadToken(s) {
    t = toLowerCase(trim(s));
    if (t == "" || t == "na" || t == "nan" || t == "inf") return 1;
    return 0;
}

function SP_findCol(arr, name) {
    for (i=0; i<arr.length; i++)
        if (arr[i] == name) return i;
    return -1;
}

function SP_trimCR(s) {
    if (endsWith(s, "\r")) return substring(s, 0, lengthOf(s)-1);
    return s;
}

function SP_stripExtension(f) {
    i = lastIndexOf(f, ".");
    if (i < 0) return f;
    return substring(f, 0, i);
}

function SP_arrayContains(arr, v) {
    for (i=0; i<arr.length; i++)
        if (arr[i] == v) return true;
    return false;
}

function SP_arrayAppend(arr, v) {
    newArr = newArray(arr.length + 1);
    for (i=0; i<arr.length; i++) newArr[i] = arr[i];
    newArr[arr.length] = v;
    return newArr;
}

function SP_arrayAppendNum(arr, v) {
    newArr = newArray(arr.length + 1);
    for (i=0; i<arr.length; i++) newArr[i] = arr[i];
    newArr[arr.length] = v;
    return newArr;
}

function SP_parseIfValid(s) {
    if (SP_isBadToken(s)) return NaN;
    return parseFloat(s);
}


}



// =======================
// 14) Motion Heatmaps
// =======================


if (option == "14. Create Motion-Heatmaps") {

// --- MyoCyter 2.4: Motion Heatmaps & Quantitative Analysis ---
//
// Kernlogik:
// - AVI öffnen
// - Gaussian Blur auf Stack
// - Sum-Z-Projection
// - zeitnormalisierte Kopie nur zur Threshold-Bestimmung
// - Threshold = 5% von P99.5 (nur positive Pixel)
// - binäre Bewegungsmaske erzeugen
// - Binärmaske bereinigen
// - nur die größte zusammenhängende Struktur behalten
// - exakte Pixelmaske auf das rohe Summenbild anwenden
// - daraus messen: Mean_Intensity, Area_Pixels, Total_Seconds, (Area*Intensity)/Seconds
// - Heatmaps, Montagen und Summary-Plots wie bisher

// -----------------------------
// Parameter
// -----------------------------
mh_thresholdFrac = 0.05;   // 5% von P99.5
mh_percentileRef = 99.5;   // robustes "Maximum"
mh_histBins      = 4096;   // Histogramm-Auflösung für P99.5
mh_gaussSigma    = 2;      // Gaussian Blur Sigma

// --- Verzeichnis-Auswahl & Initialisierung ---
mh_startDir = getDirectory("Please choose a specific <diffMov>-directory OR the main directory");
mh_startDir = "" + mh_startDir;
if (mh_startDir == "null") exit("Canceled.");
mh_startDir = replace(mh_startDir, "\\", "/");
if (!endsWith(mh_startDir, "/")) mh_startDir = mh_startDir + "/";

// --- Variablen für die statistische Auswertung (Plotten) ---
pl_folderNames = newArray();
pl_meansInt = newArray();
pl_sdsInt = newArray();
pl_meansMet = newArray();
pl_sdsMet = newArray();

// --- Variablen für den Vereinigungs-Export ---
mh_unionFilesENG = newArray();
mh_unionHeaders = newArray();

// --- Suche nach diffMov-Ordnern ---
mh_tmp = mh_startDir;
if (endsWith(mh_tmp, "/")) mh_tmp = substring(mh_tmp, 0, lengthOf(mh_tmp)-1);
mh_lastSlash = -1;
for (mh_k = 0; mh_k < lengthOf(mh_tmp); mh_k++) {
    if (substring(mh_tmp, mh_k, mh_k+1) == "/") mh_lastSlash = mh_k;
}
mh_lastName = mh_tmp;
if (mh_lastSlash >= 0) mh_lastName = substring(mh_tmp, mh_lastSlash+1);

mh_targets = newArray();
if (mh_lastName == "diffMov") {
    mh_targets = Array.concat(mh_targets, mh_startDir);
} else {
    mh_stack = newArray(mh_startDir);
    for (mh_idx = 0; mh_idx < mh_stack.length; mh_idx++) {
        mh_current = mh_stack[mh_idx];
        if (!endsWith(mh_current, "/")) mh_current = mh_current + "/";
        mh_items = getFileList(mh_current);
        for (mh_i = 0; mh_i < mh_items.length; mh_i++) {
            mh_name = mh_items[mh_i];
            if (endsWith(mh_name, "/")) {
                if (mh_name == "diffMov/") {
                    mh_targets = Array.concat(mh_targets, mh_current + mh_name);
                }
                mh_stack = Array.concat(mh_stack, replace(mh_current + mh_name, "\\", "/"));
            }
        }
    }
}

if (mh_targets.length == 0) exit("No 'diffMov' folders found.");

// --- Hauptverarbeitung ---
for (mh_t = 0; mh_t < mh_targets.length; mh_t++) {
    mh_dir = mh_targets[mh_t];
    mh_base = mh_dir + "Motion-Heatmaps/";
    File.makeDirectory(mh_base);
    File.makeDirectory(mh_base + "Fire/");
    File.makeDirectory(mh_base + "Thermal/");
    File.makeDirectory(mh_base + "Royal/");

    mh_resultsString = "Filename\tMean_Intensity\tArea_Pixels\tTotal_Seconds\t(Area*Intensity)/Seconds\n";

    mh_currentIntVals = newArray();
    mh_currentMetVals = newArray();

    mh_list = getFileList(mh_dir);
    for (mh_i2 = 0; mh_i2 < mh_list.length; mh_i2++) {
        mh_nm = mh_list[mh_i2];
        mh_nm_low = toLowerCase(mh_nm);

        if (endsWith(mh_nm_low, ".avi") && indexOf(mh_nm_low, "mjpeg-diff-cell") >= 0) {

            // temporäre Fenster von vorher sicherheitshalber schließen
            mh_closeIfOpen("__SUMRAW__");
            mh_closeIfOpen("__SUMNORM__");
            mh_closeIfOpen("__SUMTHR__");
            mh_closeIfOpen("__MASK__");
            mh_closeIfOpen("TMP_MASK");

            mh_maskTitle = "";

            // -----------------------------
            // Video öffnen
            // -----------------------------
            run("AVI...", "open=[" + mh_dir + mh_nm + "] convert");
            mh_title = getTitle();
            mh_titleNoExt = replace(mh_title, ".avi", "");
            mh_mapName = replace(mh_titleNoExt, "mjpeg-diff-", "");

            getDimensions(mh_w, mh_h, mh_ch, mh_slices, mh_frames);
            mh_nFrames = mh_slices;
            if (mh_frames > mh_nFrames) mh_nFrames = mh_frames;
            if (mh_nFrames < 1) mh_nFrames = 1;

            mh_seconds = mh_getDurationSeconds(mh_nFrames);
            if (mh_seconds <= 0) {
                print("Warning: Could not determine duration for " + mh_nm + ". Falling back to frame count as seconds.");
                mh_seconds = mh_nFrames;
            }

            // -----------------------------
            // 1) Gaussian Blur auf Stack
            // -----------------------------
            run("Gaussian Blur...", "sigma=" + mh_gaussSigma + " stack");

            // -----------------------------
            // 2) Sum-Z-Projection
            // -----------------------------
            run("Z Project...", "projection=[Sum Slices]");
            mh_sumTitle = getTitle();

            if (isOpen(mh_title)) {
                selectWindow(mh_title);
                close();
            }

            selectWindow(mh_sumTitle);
            rename("__SUMRAW__");

            // -----------------------------
            // 3) Zeitnormalisierte Kopie nur für Threshold
            // -----------------------------
            selectWindow("__SUMRAW__");
            run("Duplicate...", "title=__SUMNORM__");
            selectWindow("__SUMNORM__");
            run("32-bit");
            run("Divide...", "value=" + mh_seconds);

            // -----------------------------
            // 4) P99.5 nur auf positiven Pixeln bestimmen
            // -----------------------------
            mh_thrRef = mh_getPositivePercentile(mh_percentileRef, mh_histBins);
            mh_threshold = mh_thresholdFrac * mh_thrRef;

            // -----------------------------
            // 5) Binärmaske aus __SUMNORM__ erzeugen
            // -----------------------------
            selectWindow("__SUMNORM__");
            run("Duplicate...", "title=TMP_MASK");
            mh_maskTitle = getTitle();
            selectWindow(mh_maskTitle);

            if (mh_thrRef > 0) {
                setThreshold(mh_threshold, 1e30);
                run("Convert to Mask");
                resetThreshold();

                selectWindow(mh_maskTitle);
                run("8-bit");

                // leichte Binärbereinigung
                run("Options...", "iterations=1 count=1 black");
                selectWindow(mh_maskTitle); run("Open");
                selectWindow(mh_maskTitle); run("Close-");
                selectWindow(mh_maskTitle); run("Fill Holes");

                // nur größte zusammenhängende Struktur behalten
                selectWindow(mh_maskTitle);
                mh_keepLargestComponentInMask(mh_maskTitle);
            } else {
                selectWindow(mh_maskTitle);
                run("8-bit");
                selectAll();
                run("Clear");
            }

            // -----------------------------
            // 6) Exakte Maske auf rohes Summenbild anwenden
            // -----------------------------
            selectWindow(mh_maskTitle);
            run("32-bit");
            run("Divide...", "value=255");

            imageCalculator("Multiply create 32-bit", "__SUMRAW__", mh_maskTitle);
            rename("__SUMTHR__");

            // -----------------------------
            // 7) Messung auf exakt maskiertem rohen Summenbild
            // -----------------------------
            selectWindow("__SUMTHR__");
            run("Clear Results");
            setThreshold(0.0000001, 1e30);
            run("Set Measurements...", "area mean limit redirect=None decimal=4");
            run("Measure");
            resetThreshold();

            mh_area = getValue("Area");
            mh_mean = getValue("Mean");

            if (isNaN(mh_area)) mh_area = 0;
            if (isNaN(mh_mean)) mh_mean = 0;

            mh_metric = 0;
            if (mh_seconds > 0) mh_metric = (mh_area * mh_mean) / mh_seconds;

            mh_currentIntVals = Array.concat(mh_currentIntVals, mh_mean);
            mh_currentMetVals = Array.concat(mh_currentMetVals, mh_metric);

            mh_resultsString = mh_resultsString + mh_mapName + "\t" + mh_mean + "\t" + mh_area + "\t" + mh_seconds + "\t" + mh_metric + "\n";

            // -----------------------------
            // 8) Heatmaps aus dem maskierten Summenbild
            // -----------------------------
            mh_LUTs = newArray("Fire", "Thermal", "Royal");
            for (mh_l = 0; mh_l < mh_LUTs.length; mh_l++) {
                selectWindow("__SUMTHR__");
                run("Duplicate...", "title=__LUT__" + mh_LUTs[mh_l]);
                run("8-bit");
                run(mh_LUTs[mh_l]);
                run("Apply LUT");
                saveAs("Jpeg", mh_base + mh_LUTs[mh_l] + "/" + mh_mapName + "_" + mh_LUTs[mh_l] + ".jpg");
                close();
            }

            // Aufräumen
            if (mh_maskTitle != "" && isOpen(mh_maskTitle)) {
                selectWindow(mh_maskTitle);
                close();
            }
            if (isOpen("__SUMNORM__")) {
                selectWindow("__SUMNORM__");
                close();
            }
            if (isOpen("__SUMRAW__")) {
                selectWindow("__SUMRAW__");
                close();
            }
            if (isOpen("__SUMTHR__")) {
                selectWindow("__SUMTHR__");
                close();
            }
            roiManager("reset");
        }
    }

    // --- Ordnerweise Statistik ---
    if (mh_currentIntVals.length > 0) {
        Array.getStatistics(mh_currentIntVals, mh_min1, mh_max1, meanInt, stdInt);
        Array.getStatistics(mh_currentMetVals, mh_min2, mh_max2, meanMet, stdMet);

        mh_dirNoSlash = mh_dir;
        if (endsWith(mh_dirNoSlash, "/")) mh_dirNoSlash = substring(mh_dirNoSlash, 0, lengthOf(mh_dirNoSlash)-1);
        splitDir = split(mh_dirNoSlash, "/");
        mh_nSplit = splitDir.length;

        folderLabel = "diffMov";
        if (mh_nSplit >= 3 && splitDir[mh_nSplit-1] == "diffMov")
            folderLabel = splitDir[mh_nSplit-3];
        else if (mh_nSplit >= 3)
            folderLabel = splitDir[mh_nSplit-3];
        else if (mh_nSplit >= 1)
            folderLabel = splitDir[mh_nSplit-1];

        pl_folderNames = Array.concat(pl_folderNames, folderLabel);
        pl_meansInt = Array.concat(pl_meansInt, meanInt);
        pl_sdsInt = Array.concat(pl_sdsInt, stdInt);
        pl_meansMet = Array.concat(pl_meansMet, meanMet);
        pl_sdsMet = Array.concat(pl_sdsMet, stdMet);
    }

    // --- TXT-Export ---
    File.saveString(mh_resultsString, mh_base + "Heatmaps Intensity (ENG).txt");
    mh_resultsGER = replace(mh_resultsString, ".", ",");
    File.saveString(mh_resultsGER, mh_base + "Heatmaps Intensity (GER).txt");

    // Header für UNITED-File = Ordnername zwei Ebenen über diffMov
    mh_dirNoSlash2 = mh_dir;
    if (endsWith(mh_dirNoSlash2, "/")) mh_dirNoSlash2 = substring(mh_dirNoSlash2, 0, lengthOf(mh_dirNoSlash2)-1);
    mh_partsUnion = split(mh_dirNoSlash2, "/");
    mh_nPartsUnion = mh_partsUnion.length;

    mh_unionHeader = "diffMov";
    if (mh_nPartsUnion >= 3 && mh_partsUnion[mh_nPartsUnion-1] == "diffMov")
        mh_unionHeader = mh_partsUnion[mh_nPartsUnion-3];
    else if (mh_nPartsUnion >= 3)
        mh_unionHeader = mh_partsUnion[mh_nPartsUnion-3];
    else if (mh_nPartsUnion >= 1)
        mh_unionHeader = mh_partsUnion[mh_nPartsUnion-1];

    mh_unionFilesENG = Array.concat(mh_unionFilesENG, mh_base + "Heatmaps Intensity (ENG).txt");
    mh_unionHeaders = Array.concat(mh_unionHeaders, mh_unionHeader);

    // --- Montagen nur wenn mindestens 2 Bilder vorhanden sind ---
    mh_folders = newArray("Fire", "Royal", "Thermal");
    for (mh_f = 0; mh_f < mh_folders.length; mh_f++) {
        mh_sub = mh_base + mh_folders[mh_f] + "/";
        mh_jlist = getFileList(mh_sub);

        mh_jpgCount = 0;
        for (mh_k2 = 0; mh_k2 < mh_jlist.length; mh_k2++) {
            if (endsWith(toLowerCase(mh_jlist[mh_k2]), ".jpg")) {
                mh_jpgCount++;
            }
        }

        if (mh_jpgCount < 2) {
            continue;
        }

        mh_opened = 0;
        for (mh_k2 = 0; mh_k2 < mh_jlist.length; mh_k2++) {
            if (endsWith(toLowerCase(mh_jlist[mh_k2]), ".jpg")) {
                open(mh_sub + mh_jlist[mh_k2]);
                rename(replace(getTitle(), "_" + mh_folders[mh_f], ""));
                mh_opened++;
            }
        }

        if (mh_opened >= 2) {
            run("Images to Stack", "use");
            run("Make Montage...", "scale=1 label");
            saveAs("Jpeg", mh_base + mh_folders[mh_f] + ".jpg");
            run("Close All");
        } else {
            run("Close All");
        }
    }
}

if (mh_unionFilesENG.length > 0) {
    mh_writeUnitedHeatmapFiles(
        mh_unionFilesENG,
        mh_unionHeaders,
        mh_startDir + "Heatmaps Intensity UNITED (ENG).txt",
        mh_startDir + "Heatmaps Intensity UNITED (GER).txt"
    );
}

// ============================================================
// --- PLOTTING SEKTION ---
// ============================================================
if (pl_folderNames.length > 0) {
    fTitle = 24;
    fAxis  = 20;
