    fTicks = 18;

    cW = 1400;
    cH = 700;
    newImage("Summary Plots", "RGB white", cW, cH, 1);

    drawBarPlot(100, 80, 520, 450, "Mean Intensity", pl_folderNames, pl_meansInt, pl_sdsInt, fTitle, fAxis, fTicks);
    drawBarPlot(760, 80, 520, 450, "(Area * Intensity) / s", pl_folderNames, pl_meansMet, pl_sdsMet, fTitle, fAxis, fTicks);

    saveAs("Jpeg", mh_startDir + "Summary_Analysis_Plots.jpg");
}

run("Close All");
if (isOpen("Log")) close("Log");
if (isOpen("Results")) close("Results");

// ------------------------------------------------------------
// Hilfsfunktionen
// ------------------------------------------------------------

function mh_getDurationSeconds(nFrames) {
    fps = Stack.getFrameRate();
    if (fps > 0) return nFrames / fps;

    interval = Stack.getFrameInterval();
    Stack.getUnits(xUnit, yUnit, zUnit, tUnit, vUnit);

    if (interval <= 0) return 0;

    t = toLowerCase(tUnit);
    factor = 1;

    if (t == "s" || t == "sec" || startsWith(t, "sec")) factor = 1;
    else if (t == "ms" || t == "msec" || startsWith(t, "mill")) factor = 0.001;
    else if (t == "us" || t == "usec" || startsWith(t, "micro")) factor = 0.000001;
    else if (startsWith(t, "min")) factor = 60;
    else if (startsWith(t, "h") || startsWith(t, "hour")) factor = 3600;
    else factor = 1;

    return nFrames * interval * factor;
}

// Bestimmt das Perzentil nur aus positiven Pixeln (>0),
// damit der Null-Hintergrund das P99.5 nicht verfälscht
function mh_getPositivePercentile(pct, bins) {
    getStatistics(mh_areaTmp, mh_meanTmp, mh_minTmp, mh_maxTmp, mh_stdTmp);

    if (mh_maxTmp <= 0) return 0;

    getHistogram(mh_vals, mh_counts, bins, 0, mh_maxTmp);

    total = 0;
    for (i = 1; i < mh_counts.length; i++) total += mh_counts[i];
    if (total <= 0) return 0;

    target = total * pct / 100.0;
    cum = 0;

    for (i = 1; i < mh_counts.length; i++) {
        cum += mh_counts[i];
        if (cum >= target) {
            return mh_vals[i];
        }
    }
    return mh_maxTmp;
}

// Behält in der aktuellen Binärmaske nur die größte zusammenhängende Struktur
function mh_keepLargestComponentInMask(maskTitle) {
    selectWindow(maskTitle);
    run("8-bit");

    roiManager("reset");
    run("Clear Results");
    run("Set Measurements...", "area redirect=None decimal=4");
    run("Analyze Particles...", "size=0-Infinity show=Nothing add");

    n = roiManager("count");
    if (n < 1) {
        selectWindow(maskTitle);
        selectAll();
        run("Clear");
        roiManager("reset");
        return -1;
    }

    maxArea = -1;
    maxIdx = -1;

    run("Clear Results");
    for (i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        roiManager("Select", i);
        run("Measure");
        a = getResult("Area", i);
        if (a > maxArea) {
            maxArea = a;
            maxIdx = i;
        }
    }

    if (maxIdx < 0) {
        selectWindow(maskTitle);
        selectAll();
        run("Clear");
        roiManager("reset");
        return -1;
    }

    selectWindow(maskTitle);
    roiManager("Select", maxIdx);
    setBackgroundColor(0, 0, 0);
    run("Clear Outside");
    roiManager("reset");
    return 0;
}

function mh_closeIfOpen(title) {
    if (isOpen(title)) {
        selectWindow(title);
        close();
    }
}

function mh_getEffectiveLineCount(lines) {
    n = lines.length;
    for (i = n; i > 0; i--) {
        if (lines[i-1] != "") return i;
    }
    return 0;
}

function mh_padLineToColumns(line, nCols) {
    out = "" + line;
    nTabs = 0;
    for (i = 0; i < lengthOf(out); i++) {
        if (substring(out, i, i+1) == "\t") nTabs++;
    }

    neededTabs = (nCols - 1) - nTabs;
    if (neededTabs < 0) neededTabs = 0;

    for (i = 0; i < neededTabs; i++) out = out + "\t";
    return out;
}

function mh_writeUnitedHeatmapFiles(filePaths, headers, outPathENG, outPathGER) {
    nFiles = filePaths.length;
    if (nFiles < 1) return;

    blockCols = 5;
    contents = newArray();
    lineCounts = newArray();
    maxLines = 0;

    for (i = 0; i < nFiles; i++) {
        txt = File.openAsString(filePaths[i]);
        txt = replace(txt, "\r\n", "\n");
        txt = replace(txt, "\r", "\n");

        contents = Array.concat(contents, txt);

        lines = split(txt, "\n");
        eff = mh_getEffectiveLineCount(lines);
        lineCounts = Array.concat(lineCounts, eff);
        if (eff > maxLines) maxLines = eff;
    }

    united = "";

    // 1. Kopfzeile: Probenname / Ordner zwei Ebenen über diffMov
    row = "";
    for (i = 0; i < nFiles; i++) {
        row = row + mh_padLineToColumns(headers[i], blockCols);
        if (i < nFiles-1) row = row + "\t";
    }
    united = united + row + "\n";

    // Danach alle Zeilen der einzelnen Dateien nebeneinander
    for (r = 0; r < maxLines; r++) {
        row = "";
        for (i = 0; i < nFiles; i++) {
            lines = split(contents[i], "\n");
            line = "";
            if (r < lineCounts[i]) line = lines[r];

            row = row + mh_padLineToColumns(line, blockCols);
            if (i < nFiles-1) row = row + "\t";
        }
        united = united + row + "\n";
    }

    File.saveString(united, outPathENG);
    File.saveString(replace(united, ".", ","), outPathGER);
}

function drawBarPlot(xOff, yOff, w, h, title, labels, means, sds, fT, fA, fTk) {
    maxV = 0;
    for (i=0; i<means.length; i++) {
        val = means[i] + sds[i];
        if (val > maxV) maxV = val;
    }

    yMax = getNiceMax(maxV * 1.15);

    setColor(0,0,0);
    setLineWidth(2);
    drawLine(xOff, yOff+h, xOff+w, yOff+h);
    drawLine(xOff, yOff, xOff, yOff+h);

    setFont("SansSerif", fT, "bold antialiased");
    drawString(title, xOff + (w/2) - (lengthOf(title)*fT/4), yOff - 30);

    n = means.length;
    barW = (w / (n * 2.5));
    gap = (w - (n * barW)) / (n + 1);

    for (i=0; i<n; i++) {
        bX = xOff + gap + (i * (barW + gap)) + barW/2;
        bH = (means[i] / yMax) * h;
        sdH = (sds[i] / yMax) * h;

        setColor(70, 130, 180);
        fillRect(bX - barW/2, yOff + h - bH, barW, bH);
        setColor(0,0,0);
        drawRect(bX - barW/2, yOff + h - bH, barW, bH);

        drawLine(bX, yOff + h - bH, bX, yOff + h - bH - sdH);
        drawLine(bX - 8, yOff + h - bH - sdH, bX + 8, yOff + h - bH - sdH);

        // X-Achsen-Beschriftung = Probenname
        setFont("SansSerif", fTk, "antialiased");
        lab = labels[i];
        labW = getStringWidth(lab);
        drawString(lab, bX - labW/2, yOff + h + 30);
    }

    setFont("SansSerif", fTk, "antialiased");
    precision = getRequiredPrecision(yMax);

    for (j=0; j<=10; j++) {
        val = (j / 10) * yMax;
        yPos = yOff + h - (j / 10 * h);

        setColor(0,0,0);
        drawLine(xOff - 5, yPos, xOff, yPos);

        lab = d2s(val, precision);
        w_lab = getStringWidth(lab);
        drawString(lab, xOff - 10 - w_lab, yPos + 7);
    }
}

function getNiceMax(val) {
    if (val <= 0) return 1;
    mh_log10val = log(val) / log(10);
    mag = pow(10, floor(mh_log10val));
    norm = val / mag;
    if (norm <= 1.0) nice = 1.0;
    else if (norm <= 2.0) nice = 2.0;
    else if (norm <= 5.0) nice = 5.0;
    else if (norm <= 8.0) nice = 8.0;
    else nice = 10.0;
    return nice * mag;
}

function getRequiredPrecision(yMax) {
    if (yMax >= 10) return 1;
    if (yMax >= 1) return 2;
    if (yMax >= 0.1) return 3;
    return 4;
}

close("*");
if (isOpen("ROI Manager")) {close("ROI Manager");}

}
